### Luke

[1:1] Son wheesh as dy vel ymmodee er ghoaill ayns laue dy chur coontey cairagh jeh ny reddyn ta dy firrinagh er nyn gredjal nyn mast'ain.
[1:2] Eer myr hoilshee ad dooinyn ad, va er-dyn toshiaght nyn veanishyn sooilley as nyn shirveishee jeh'n ghoo.
[1:3] Ta mish myrgeddin er vakin eh mie, myr ta slane toiggal aym jeh dy chooilley nhee er-dyn eer toshiaght, dy scrieu hoods ayns order, Theophilus smoo ooasle,
[1:4] Dy vod tushtey share y ve ayd jeh firrinys ny reddyn shen, t'ou er ny ve ynsit ayndoo.
[1:5] Rish lhing Heron ree Yudea, va saggyrt dy row enmyssit Zacharias, jeh coorse Abia; as va'n ven echey jeh inneenyn Aaron, as yn ennym eck Elizabeth.
[1:6] As v'ad ny-neesht cairagh kiongoyrt rish Jee, gimmeeaght ayns ooilley annaghyn as oardaghyn y Chiarn gyn loght.
[1:7] As cha row sluight oc, er-yn-oyr dy row Elizabeth gennish, as v'ad ny-neesht er roie dy mie ayns eash.
[1:8] As haink eh gy-kione, choud as v'eh cooilleeney oik y taggyrt kiongoyrt rish Jee, myr va e choorse er jeet magh,
[1:9] Cordail rish cliaghtey oik y taggyrt, dy haghyr eh dy ve yn currym echey dy lostey oural-millish, tra v'eh goll stiagh ayns chiamble y Chiarn.
[1:10] As va'n slane chaglym jeh'n pobble cheu-mooie ec padjer rish traa yn oural-millish.
[1:11] As haink ainle y Chiarn, as hass eh er cheu yesh altar yn oural-millish.
[1:12] As tra honnick Zacharias eh, v'eh seaghnit, as huitt aggle er.
[1:13] Agh dooyrt yn ainle rish, Ny gow aggle Zacharias: son ta dty phadjer er ny chlashtyn, as nee yn ven ayd Elizabeth mac y ymmyrkey dhyt, as nee oo genmys eh Ean.
[1:14] As bee boggey as gerjagh ayd, as nee ymmodee boggey y ghoaill tra hig eh er y theihll.
[1:15] Son bee eh ooasle ayns shilley yn Chiarn, as cha n'iu eh feeyn ny jough lajer, as bee eh er ny lhieeney lesh y Spyrryd Noo, veih eer brein e vayrey.
[1:16] As ymmodee jeh cloan Israel nee eh y hyndaa gys y Chiarn y Jee oc.
[1:17] As hed eh roishyn ayns spyrryd as pooar Elias, dy hyndaa creeaghyn ny ayragh yn gys y chloan, as ny mee-viallee gys creenaght yn vooinjer chairal, dy yannoo aarloo pobble kiarit son y Chiarn.
[1:18] As dooyrt Zacharias rish yn ainle, Cre liorish vees fys aym's er shoh son ta mee shenn, as ta'n ven er roie dy mie ayns eash.
[1:19] As dreggyr yn aile as dooyrt e rish, Mish Gabriel ta shirveish fenish Yee: as ta mee-er my choyrt dy loayrt rhyt, as dy hoilshaghey dhyt ny naightyn mie shoh.
[1:20] As cur-my-ner bee oo balloo, as cha jig dty ghlare lhiat, derrey yn laa vees ny reddyn shoh cooilleenit, er-y-fa nagh vel oo er chredjal my ghoan's vees er nyn gooilleeney ayns nyn imbagh cooie.
[1:21] As va'n pobble fieau son Zacharias, as yindys orroo dy row eh cumrail choud ayns y chiamble.
[1:22] As tra haink eh magh, cha voddagh eh loayrt roo; as hoig ad dy row eh er vakin ashlish ayns y chiamble: son v'eh jannoo signyn daue, as hannee eh balloo.
[1:23] As shen myr ve, tra v'eh er chooilleeney laghyn e hirveish, dy jimmee eh gys e hie hene.
[1:24] As lurg ny laghyn shen ren e ven Elizabeth giennaghtyn, as dollee ee ee-hene queig meeghyn, gra,
[1:25] Shoh myr ta'n Chiarn er n'yannoo er my hon tra yeeagh eh orrym, dy ghoaill ersooyl my oltooan mastey deiney.
[1:26] As ayns y cheyoo vee, va'n ainle Gabriel er ny choyrt veih Jee, gys ard-valley dy Ghalilee, va enmyssit Nazareth,
[1:27] Gys moidyn nasht rish dooinney enmyssit Joseph, jeh thie Ghavid; as va ennym y voidyn Moirrey.
[1:28] As haink yn ainle stiagh as dooyrt eh r'ee, Dy vannee dhyt's ta ayns ard-foayr ta'n Chiarn mayrt; bannit t'ou uss mastey mraane.
[1:29] As tra honnick ee eh, v'ee seaghnit ec y raa echey, as smooinee ee r'ee hene cre'n monney dy vannaghey va shoh.
[1:30] As dooyrt yn ainle r'ee, Ny bee aggle ort, O Voirrey; son t'ou er gheddyn foayr veih Jee.
[1:31] As cur-my-ner, nee oo giennaghtyn, as mac y ymmyrkey, as enmyssee oo yn ennym echey Yeesey.
[1:32] Bee eshyn cronnal, as enmyssit Mac yn Er-syrjey; as ver y Chiarn Jee dasyn stoyl-reeoil e ayr David.
[1:33] As nee eh reill harrish thie Yacob gys earishyn foddey beayn, as er e reeriaght cha bee jerrey erbee.
[1:34] Eisht dooyrt Moirrey rish yn ainle, Kys oddys shoh y ve, fakin nagh nione dou dooinney?
[1:35] As dreggyr yn ainle as dooyrt eh r'ee, Hig yn Spyrryd Noo neose ort, as bee pooar yn Er-syrjey er ny skeayley harryd: shen-y-fa bee yn sluight chasherick shen ver oo son y theihll, enmyssit Mac Yee.
[1:36] As cur-my-ner, dty ven-vooinjerey Elizabeth, t'eeish myrgeddin er ghiennaght yn mac ayns ny shenn laghyn eck: as shoh yn cheyoo vee jeeish va raait dy ve gennish.
[1:37] Son da Jee cha bee nhee erbee neu-phossible.
[1:38] As dooyrt Moirrey, Cur-my-ner sharvaant y Chiarn, dy jig eh lhiam cordail rish dty ghoo. As jimmee yn ainle voee.
[1:39] As mysh ny laghyn shen hrog Moirrey urree lesh siyr dy gholl gys cheer ny liargagh, gys ard-valley dy Yudah,
[1:40] As hie ee stiagh ayns thie Zacharias as vannee ee da Elizabeth.
[1:41] As haink eh gy-kione, tra cheayll Elizabeth bannaghey Moirrey, dy lheim yn oikan ayns e brein, as va Elizabeth lhieent lesh y Spyrryd Noo.
[1:42] As loayr ee lesh ard-choraa as dooyrt ee, Bannit t'ou uss mastey mraane, as bannit ta sluight dty vre&iuml;n.
[1:43] As kys ta'n (ooashley) aym, dy vel moir my Hiarn er jeet dy my yeeaghyn?
[1:44] Son cur-my-ner, cha leah as ren coraa dty vannaghey bingys ayns my chleayshyn, lheim yn oikan ayns my vrein son boggey.
[1:45] As bannit t'eeish ta er chredjal: son bee slane cooilleeney ny reddyn shen v'er ny hoilshaghey jee liorish y Chiarn.
[1:46] As dooyrt Moirrey, Ta m'annym cur ard-voylley da'n Chiarn.
[1:47] As ta my spyrryd er ghoaill boggey ayns Jee my Haualtagh.
[1:48] Son t'eh er chur tastey da stayd injil e harvaant: son cur-my-ner, maghey shoh nee dy chooilley heeloghe mish y enmys bannit.
[1:49] Son s'mooar ta'n Ooilley-niartal er n'yannoo er my hon, as s'casherick ta e ennym.
[1:50] As ta e vyghin orroosyn ta goaill aggle roish, veih sheeloghe gys sheeloghe.
[1:51] T'eh er hoilshaghey niart lesh e roih t'eh er skeayley ny moyrnee ayns mooaralys nyn greeaghyn.
[1:52] T'eh er lhieggal sheese ny treanee veih nyn stuill-reeoil, as er hoiaghey seose ny imlee.
[1:53] T'eh er lhieeney ny accryssee lesh reddyn mie, as ny berchee t'eh er chur follym ersooyl.
[1:54] T'eh er chooney lesh e harvaant Israel ayns cooinaghtyn jeh e vyghin.
[1:55] (Myr loayr eh rish nyn shenn-ayryn, rish Abraham as e luight) er son dy bragh.
[1:56] As duirree Moirrey m&acirc;ree mysh three meeghyn, as haink ee reesht gys e thie hene.
[1:57] Nish va slane traa Elizabeth er jeet dy ve livreit, as hug ee mac son y theihll.
[1:58] As cheayll ny naboonyn as y sleih mooinjerey eck, kys va'n Chiarn er hoilshaghey ard-vyghin jee; as ghow ad boggey m&acirc;ree.
[1:59] As haink eh gy-kione er yn hoghtoo laa dy daink ad dy ghiarey-chymmylt yn lhiannoo; as denmys ad eh Zacharias, lurg ennym e ayrey.
[1:60] As dreggyr e voir, as dooyrt ee, Cha nee; agh bee eh enmyssit Ean.
[1:61] As dooyrt ad r'ee, Cha vel veg jeh dty chynney jeh'n ennym shen.
[1:62] As ren ad signyn gys e ayr, cre'n ennym bailIishyn y ve er.
[1:63] As hir eh boayrd-screeuee, as scrieu eh, gra, Ta'n ennym echey Ean. As ghow ad ooilley yindys.
[1:64] As er-y-chooyl va e veeal er ny osley, as e hengey er ny eaysley, as loayr eh, as hug eh moylley da Jee.
[1:65] As huitt aggle (arrymagh) er ooilley nyn naboonyn: as hie goo jeh ooilley ny reddyn shoh magh trooid ooilley cheer sleitagh Yudea.
[1:66] As adsyn ooilley cheayll shoh, hasht ad ayns nyn greeaghyn ad, gra, Cren monney dy ghooinney vees eh shoh? as va laue yn Chiarn m&acirc;rish.
[1:67] As va'n ayr echey Zacharias lhieent lesh y Spyrryd Noo, as ren eh phadeyrys, gra,
[1:68] Bannit dy row yn Chiarn Jee Israel, son t'eh er yeeaghyn er, as er livrey e phobble,
[1:69] As t'eh er hroggal seose saualtys niartal er nyn son, ayns thie e harvaant David;
[1:70] Myr loayr eh liorish beeal e adeyryn crauee, t'er ny ve er-dy hoshiaght y theihll;
[1:71] Dy hauail shin veih nyn noidyn, as veih'n lane ocsyn ooilley ta dwoaie oc orrin.
[1:72] Dy chooilleeney yn vyghin va giallit da ny ayraghyn ain, as dy chooinaghtyn er e chonaant casherick:
[1:73] Eer yn breearrey ren eh gys yn ayr ain Abraham,
[1:74] Dy giallagh eh dooinyn, dy beagh shin er nyn livrey veih laueyn nyn noidyn, as shirveish eh fegooish aggle.
[1:75] Ayns craueeaght as cairys kiongoyrt rish, ooilley laghyn nyn mea.
[1:76] As bee uss lhiannoo enmyssit phadeyr yn Er-syrjey; son hed oo roish eddin y Chiarn, dy yannoo aarloo e raaidyn;
[1:77] Dy chur tushtey dy haualtys da e phobble, liorish leih nyn beccaghyn,
[1:78] Trooid myghin meiygh yn Jee ain; liorish ta irree-ny-greiney veih yn yrjid er hoilshean orrin
[1:79] Dy chur soilshey dauesyn ta nyn soie ayns dorraghys as ayns scadoo yn vaaish, dy leeideil ny cassyn ain ayns raad y chee.
[1:80] As daase y lhiannoo, as v'eh er ny niartaghey 'sy spyrryd, as v'eh ayns ny faasaghyn, derrey'n laa v'eh er ny hoilshaghey da Israel.
[2:1] As haink eh gy-kione ayns ny laghyn shen, dy jagh sarey magh veih Cesar Augustus, dy beagh coontey er ny ghoaill jeh'n slane rheam.
[2:2] (As va'n recortys shoh jeant magh roish my va Cyremus ny chiannoort er Syria.)
[2:3] As hie ad ooilley dy chur stiagh nyn enmyn, dagh unnane gys e ard-valley hene.
[2:4] As hie Joseph myrgeddin seose veih Galilee, veih ard-valley Nazareth, gys Judea, gys ard-valley Ghavid, ta enmyssit Bethlehem (son dy row eh jeh thie as kynney Ghavid.)
[2:5] Dy chur stiagh e ennym hene as ennym Moirrey yn ven va nasht rish, va trome torragh.
[2:6] As shen myr ve, choud as v'ad ayns shen, dy row yn traa er jeet jeeish dy ve livreit.
[2:7] As hug ee son y theihll yn chied mac rug jee, as hoill ee eh ayns aanrityn so&iuml;llee, as hug ee eh ny lhie ayns manjoor, er-y-fa nagh row room er nyn son ayns y thie-oast.
[2:8] Nish v'ayns y cheer cheddin bochilley mooie er y vagher freayll arrey er nyn shioltaneyn 'syn oie.
[2:9] As cur-my-ner haink ainle y Chiarn neose orroo, as ren gloyr y Chiarn soilshean mygeayrt-y-moo; as v'ad fo aggle feer atchimagh.
[2:10] As dooyrt yn ainle roo, Ny bee aggle erriu: son cur-my-ner, ta mish coyrt lhiam hiu naightyn mie dy voggey mooar vees gys dy chooilley phobble.
[2:11] Son diuish t'er ny ruggey jiu ayns ard valley Ghavid, Saualtagh, ta shen Creest yn Chiarn.
[2:12] As bee shoh son cowrey diu; Yiow shiu yn oikan ayns aanrityn soillee, as ny lhie ayns manjoor.
[2:13] As ayns y tullogh va marish yn ainle ymmodee jeh'n cheshaght flaunyssagh cur moylley da Jee, as gra,
[2:14] Gloyr dy row gys Jee ayns yn yrjid, as er y thalloo shee, aigney-mie gys deiney.
[2:15] As haink eh gy-kione, cha leah as va ny ainleyn er n'gholl ersooyl voue gys niau, dy dooyrt ny bochillyn yn derrey yeh rish y jeh elley, Lhig dooin goll nish derrey Bethlehem, dy akin yn red shoh t'er jeet gy-kione, ta'n Chiarn er hoilshaghey dooin.
[2:16] As haink ad lesh siyr, as hooar ad Moirrey as Joseph, as yn oikan ny lhie ayns manjoor.
[2:17] As tra honnick ad eh, hoilshee ad magh yn raa va er ny insh daue mychione y lhiannoo shoh.
[2:18] As ghow dy chooilley unnane cheayll eh, yindys jeh ny reddyn va inshit daue liorish ny bochillyn.
[2:19] Agh hasht Moirrey ooilley ny raaghyn shoh (ayns e haigney) as smooinee ee orroo dy dowin ayns e cree.
[2:20] As haink ny bochillyn roue, cur gloyr as moylley da Jee son dy chooilley nhee v'ad er chlashtyn as er vakin, myr ve inshit daue.
[2:21] As tra va hoght laa ec kione son giarey-chymmylt y lhiannoo, v'eh enmyssit YEESEY, son shen yn ennym hug yn ainle er, roish my row eh er ny ghiennaghtyn 'sy vrein.
[2:22] As tra va laghyn nyn ghlenney, cordail rish leigh Voses, er jeet, hug ad lhieu eh gys Jerusalem, dy hebbal eh gys y Chiarn,
[2:23] (Myr te scruit ayns leih yn Chiarn, Bee dy chooilley chied-ruggit yrrynagh er ny chasherickey gys y Chiarn.)
[2:24] As dy hebbal yn oural t'er ny harey ayns leigh yn Chiarn, Piyr dy chalmaneyn turtle, ny daa chalmane aegey.
[2:25] As cur-my-ner va dooinney ayns Jerusalem va enmyssit Simeon; as va'n dooinney cheddin cairagh as crauee, farkiaght son gerjagh Israel: as va'n Spyrryd Noo ersyn.
[2:26] As ve er ny hoilshaghey da liorish y Spyrryd Noo, nagh noghe eh baase, roish da v'er vakin Creest yn Chiarn.
[2:27] As haink eh liorish y Spyrryd stiagh ayns y chiamble: as tra va'n ayr as y voir er chur lhieu yn lhiannoo Yeesey stiagh, dy yannoo er e hon, lurg cliaghtey yn leigh;
[2:28] Eisht ghow eh seose eh ayns e roihaghyn, as hug eh moylley da Jee, as dooyrt eh,
[2:29] Hiarn nish t'ou cur kied da dty harvaant paartail ayns she, cordail rish dty ghoo.
[2:30] Son ta my hooillyn er vakin dty haualtys;
[2:31] T'ou er chiarail dy ve er ny hoilshaghey fenish dy chooilley phobble;
[2:32] Soilshey dy hoilshean er ny Ashoonee as gloyr dty phobble Israel.
[2:33] As ghow Joseph as e voir yindys jeh ny reddyn va loayrit my-e-chione,
[2:34] As vannee Simeon ad, as dooyrt eh rish Moirrey e voir, Cur-my-ner ta'n lhiannoo shoh soit dy chur sheese as dy hoiaghey seose ymmodee ayns Israel; as son cowrey dy oltooan.
[2:35] (As dy jarroo hed cliwe trooid dty annym hene neesht) dy vod smooinaghtyn ymmodee creeaghyn v'er ny chronnaghey.
[2:36] As va myrgeddin phadeyrben enmyssit Anna, inneen Phanuel, jeh kynney Aser: v'ee dy eash vooar, as v'ee er veaghey marish e sheshey shiaght bleeaney neayr as v'ee ny moidyn.
[2:37] As v'ee ny ben-treoghe mysh kiare feed as kiare bleeaney dy eash, as v'ee dy kinjagh taaghey yn chiamble, shirveish Jee lesh trostey as padjeryn oie as laa.
[2:38] As haink ish stiagh ec y traa cheddin, as hug ee booise myrgeddin da'n Chiarn, as loayr ee jeh roosyn ooilley va jeeaghyn son livrey-ys ayns Jerusalem.
[2:39] As tra v'ad er chooilleeney dy chooilley nhee cordail rish leigh yn Chiarn, haink ad reesht gys Galilee, gys yn ard-valley oc hene Nazareth.
[2:40] As daase y lhiannoo, as v'eh er ny niartaghey 'sy spyrryd, as lhieent lesh creenaght, as va grayse Yee m&acirc;rish.
[2:41] Nish va e ayr as e voir goll seose gys Jerusalem dy chooilley vlein ec feailley ny caisht.
[2:42] As tra v'eh daa vlein jeig dy eash, hie ad seose gys Jerusalem lurg cliaghtey ny feailley.
[2:43] As tra va ny laghyn harrish, as ad goll thie reesht, duirree yn lhiannoo Yeesey nyn yei ayns Jerusalem, gyn-yss da Joseph as e voir.
[2:44] Agh smooinaghtgn dy row eh ayns y cheshaght, hie ad jurnah laa; as v'ad briaght er e hon mastey nyn gheiney mooinjerey as nyn ainjys.
[2:45] As tra nagh dooar ad eh, hie ad reesht gys Jerusalem shirrey er e hon.
[2:46] As haink eh gy-kione, lurg three laa dy dooar ad eh ayns y chiamble, ny hoie mastey ny fir-ynsee, chammah geaishtagh roo, as cur feyshtyn orroo.
[2:47] As ghow ooilley ny va geaishtagh rish yindys jeh'n toiggal as jeh ny ansooryn echey.
[2:48] As tra honnick ad eh, v'ad fo mooarane atchim; as dooyrt e voir rish, Vac, cre'n-fa t'ou er n'yannoo myr shoh rooin? cur-my-ner, ta dty ayr as mish er ve briaght dy trimshagh er dty hon.
[2:49] As dooyrt eh roo, Kys dy row shiu briaght er my hon's? nagh row fys eu dy beign dou ve mysh obbyr my Ayrey ?
[2:50] As cha row toiggyl oc jeh'n raa loayr eh roo.
[2:51] As hie eh sheese m&acirc;roo, as haink eh gys Nazareth, as v'eh biallagh daue: as hasht e voir ooilley ny raaghyn shoh ayns e cree.
[2:52] As ren Yeesey bishaghey ayns creenaght as aase, as ayns foayr rish Jee as dooinney.
[3:1] NISH ayns y wheiggoo vlein jeig jeh reill, Tiberius Cesar, tra va Pontius Pilate ny chiannoort er Judea, as Herod ny hetrarch er Galilee, as e vraar Philip reill ayns Iturea as cheer Trachonitis, as Lysanias reill ayns Abilene.
[3:2] Tra va Annas as Caiaphas nyn ard-saggyrtyn, haink goo Yee gys Ean mac Zacharias ayns yn aasagh.
[3:3] As haink eh gys ooilley yn cheer my geayrt Jordan, preacheil bashtey arrys son leih peccaghyn.
[3:4] Myr te scruit ayns lioar goan Esaias yn phadeyr, gra, Coraa fer geamagh ayns yn aasagh, Kiartee-jee raad y Chiarn, jean-jee ny cassanyn echey jeeragh.
[3:5] Bee dy chooilley choan er ny lhieeney as dy chooilley slieau as cronk er nyn injillaghey, as ny ynnydyn cammey er nyn yannoo jeeragh, as ny raaidyn garroo er nyn yannoo rea.
[3:6] As hee dy chooilley eill saualtys Yee.
[3:7] Eisht dooyrt eh rish y pobble v'er jeet magh huggey dy ve er nyn mashtey, O shiuish heeloghe dy ard-nieughyn, quoi t'er chur raaue diu dy hea veih yn jymmoose ta ry-heet?
[3:8] Cur-jee magh nish er-y-fa shen messyn cooie dy arrys, as ny jean-jee toshiaght dy ghra riu hene, Ta Abraham ain son nyn ayr: son ta mee gra riu, dy vel pooar ec Jee eer jeh ny claghyn shoh cloan y hroggal seose da Abraham.
[3:9] As nish hannah ta'n teigh er ny choyrt gys fraue ny biljyn: shen-y-fa ta dy chooilley villey nagh vel gymmyrkey mess mie, dy ve giarit sheese as tilgit ayns yn aile.
[3:10] As denee yn pobble jeh, gra, Cre ta orrinyn dy yannoo?
[3:11] Dreggyr eh as dooyrt eh roo, Eshyn ta daa chooat echey, lhig da y choyrt dasyn nagh vel cooat eddyr echey as eshyn ta beaghey echey, lhig da jannoo er yn aght cheddin.
[3:12] Eisht haink myrgeddin ny publicanee dy ve er nyn mashtey, as dooyrt ad rish, Vainshter, cre ta orrinyn dy yannoo?
[3:13] As dooyrt eh roo, Ny trog-jee ny smoo na ta er nyn gurrym.
[3:14] As d&ecirc;nee ny sidooryn myrgeddin, jeh, gra, As cre ta orrinyn dy yannoo? As dooyrt eh roo, Ny jean-jee tranlaase er dooinney erbee, ny jean-jee cassid vreagagh er dooinney erbee, as bee-jee booiagh lesh nyn vaill.
[3:15] As myr va'n pobble ayns imnea, as dy chooilley ghooinney smooinaghtyn ayns nyn greeaghyn mychione Ean, nee eh va'n Creest mannagh nee;
[3:16] Dreggyr Ean as dooyrt eh roo ooilley, Ta mish dy jarroo bashtey shiu lesh ushtey; agh ta fer s'pooaral na mish cheet kiangley ny braagyn echey cha vel mee feeu dy eaysley: nee eshyn shiu y vashtey lesh y Spyrryd Noo, as lesh aile.
[3:17] Ta'n cleayst echey ayns e laue, as fasnee eh dy bollagh e laare-vooie, as gowee eh yn churnaght stiagh ayns e hie tashtee; agh yn coau nee eh y lostey lesh aile nagh bee er ny vooghey.
[3:18] As ymmodee dy reddyn elley ren eh y choyrlaghey as y phreacheil gys y pobble.
[3:19] Agh tra v'eh er choyrt oghsan da Herod yn Tetrarch kyndagh rish Herodias ben e vraar Philip, as ooilley ny huilk va Herod er n'yannoo,
[3:20] Ren eh shoh marish y chooid elley, dy dug eh Ean ayns pryssoon.
[3:21] Nish tra va ooilley'n pobble er nyn mashtey, haink eh gy-kione dy row Yeesey myrgeddin er ny vashtey, as ghow eh padjer, as va niau er ny osley;
[3:22] As haink y Spyrryd Noo neose er, myr ayns cummey dooghyssagh calmane, as haink coraa veih niau, gra, Oo my vac ennoil, jeed ta mee dy mooar soiaghey.
[3:23] As ghow Yeesey eh-hene toshiaght dy ve mysh jeih bleeaney as feed dy eash, as (goit dy ve) mac Yoseph, mac Heli,

[3:29] Mac Jose, mac Eliezer, mac Jorim, mac Matthat, mac Levi,

[4:1] As va Yeesey lane jeh'n Spyrryd Noo, as hyndaa eh veih Jordan, as v'eh er ny leeideil liorish y Spyrryd gys yn aasagh,
[4:2] As v'eh da-eed laa er ny violaghey liorish y drogh-spyrryd, as ayns ny laghyn shen cha d'ee eh veg; as tra v'ad harrish, v'eh ny lurg shen accryssagh.
[4:3] As dooyrt y drogh-spyrryd rish, My she Mac Yee oo, abbyr rish yn chlagh shoh dy ve jeant ny arran.
[4:4] As dreggyr Yeesey eh, gra, Te scruit, Nagh nee er arran ny-lomarcan nee dooinney beaghey, agh liorish ooilley goan Yee.
[4:5] As hug y drogh-spyrryd lesh seose eh gys mullagh slieau ard, as ayns y tullogh hug eh shilley da jeh ooilley reeriaghtyn y theihll.
[4:6] As dooyrt y drogh-spyrryd rish, Ooilley yn phooar shoh ver-ym dhyt's, as y ghloyr oc; son ta shen er ny livrey dou, as da quoi-erbee saillym, ta mee dy choyrt eh.
[4:7] My ver oo er-y-fa shen ooashley dou bee ooilley lhiat hene.
[4:8] As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Ass my enish oo, Noid-ny-hanmey: son te scruit, Ver oo ooashley da'n Chiarn dty Yee, as eshyn ynrycan nee oo y hirveish.
[4:9] As hug eh lesh eh gys Jerusalem, as hoie eh eh er beinn toor syrjey yn chiamble, as dooyrt eh rish, My she Mac Yee oo, tilg oo hene sheese veih shoh.
[4:10] Son te scruit, Ver eh currym da e ainleyn harryd, dy dty reayll:
[4:11] As ayns nyn laueyn nee ad oo y ymmyrkey, er-aggle ec traa erbee dy bwoaill oo dty chass noi clagh.
[4:12] As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Te er ny ghra, Cha jean oo daanys er y Chiarn dty Yee.
[4:13] As erreish da'n drogh-spyrryd v'er n'yannoo jerrey er ooilley yn violagh, daag eh eh son earish.
[4:14] As haink Yeesey reesht ayns pooar y spyrryd gys Galilee: as hie goo magh jeh trooid ooilley yn cheer mygeayrt.
[4:15] As dynsee eh ayns ny kialteenyn oc, as v'eh ayns ard-voylley rish y theay.
[4:16] As haink eh gys Nazareth, raad v'eh er ny ve troggit: as hie eh, myr v'eh cliaghtey, stiagh ayns y synagogue er laa yn doonaght, as hass eh seose dy lhaih.
[4:17] As va lioar y phadeyr Esaias er ny livrey da, as tra v'eh er vosley yn lioar, hooar eh yn ynnyd raad v'eh scruit,
[4:18] Ta spyrryd y Chiarn orrym's, er-y-fa dy vel eh er my ooillaghey dy phreacheil y sushtal gys ny boghtyn, t'eh er my choyrt dy laanaghey yn vooinjer hrome-chreeagh, dy phreacheil livrey-ys gys ny cappeeyn, dy chur soilshey da ny doail, as reamys dauesyn ta broojit,
[4:19] Dy phreacheil blein eunyssagh y Chiarn.
[4:20] As yeigh eh yn lioar, as hug eh ee reesht da'n chirveishagh, as hoie eh sheese: as va sooillyn dy chooilley unnane v'ayns y synagogue dy jeean soit er.
[4:21] As ren eh toshiaght dy ghra roo, Jiu ta'n scriptyr shoh cooilleenit ayns y chlashtyn euish.
[4:22] As dymmyrk ad ooilley feanish lesh, as ghow ad yindys jeh ny goan graysoil haink ass y veeal echey. As dooyrt ad, Nagh nee shoh mac Yoseph?
[4:23] As dooyrt eh roo, Jir shiu ayns shickyrys yn chenn raa shoh rhym, Er-lhee, jean oo hene y lheihys: cre-erbee ta shin er chlashtyn va jeant ayns Capernaum, jean myrgeddin ayns shoh ayns dty heer hene.
[4:24] As dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Nagh vel soiagh jeant jeh phadeyr erbee ayns e heer hene.
[4:25] Agh ta mee ginsh diu ayns firrinys, dy row ymmodee mraane treoghe ayns Israel rish hing Elias, tra va'n aer jeight seose three bleeaney as shey meeghyn, tra va genney vooar trooid ooilley yn cheer:
[4:26] Agh gys unnane oc cha row Elias er ny choyrt, cheu mooie jeh gys Sarepta ard-valley dy Sidon, gys ben-treoghe v'ayns shen.
[4:27] As va ymmodee louranee ayns Israel rish traa Eliseus yn phadeyr, as cha row fer jeu er ny ghlenney, cheu-mooie jeh Naaman yn Syrian.
[4:28] As va ooilley ny v'ayns y synagogue tra cheayll ad ny goan shoh, lhieent lesh jymmoose,
[4:29] As dirree ad, as deiyr ad eh magh ass yn ard-valley, as hug ad lhieu eh gys broogh yn chronk (er va'n ard-valley oc troggit) ry-hoi tilgey sheese eh gour e vullee.
[4:30] Agh hie eh magh trooid mean y cheshaght, as jimmee eh roish:
[4:31] As haink eh neose gys Capernaum, ard-valley dy Ghalilee, as dynsee eh ad er laghyn y doonaght.
[4:32] As ghow ad yindys mooar jeh'n ynsaghey echey: son va e ghoo lesh pooar.
[4:33] As ayns y synagogue va dooinney seaghnit lesh spyrryd neu-ghlen, as dyllee eh lesh ard-choraa.
[4:34] Gra, Faag shin; cre'n eie t'ayd orrin uss Yeesey dy Nazareth? vel oo er jeet dy nyn stroie? ta fys aym quoi oo hene; Fer-casherick Yee.
[4:35] As hug Yeesey oghsan da, gra Bee dty-host, as tar magh ass. As tra va'n drogh spyrryd er hilgey neeal eh, haink eh magh ass, gyn assee da.
[4:36] As v'ad ooilley fo atchim, as loayr ad ny mast' oc hene, gra, Cre'n fockle (vreeoil) shoh? son lesh pooar as niart t'eh cur ny spyrrydyn neu ghlen fo harey, as t'ad cheet magh.
[4:37] As hie goo magh jeh trooid dy chooilley ard jeh'n cheer mygeayrt.
[4:38] As hrog eh magh ass y synagogoe, as hie eh stiagh ayns thie Simon: as va moir ben Simon feer ching ayns y chiassaghey; as ren ad aghin huggey er e son.
[4:39] As hass eh er-e-skyn, as hug eh oghsan da'n chiassaghey, as daag eh ee. As chelleeragh dirree ee seose, as ren ee shirveish orroo.
[4:40] Nish ec lhie ny greiney, whilleen as va sleih chingey oc fo mooarane doghanyn hug ad lhieu ad huggey; as hug eh e laueyn er dy chooilley unnane oc, as ren eh ad y lheihys.
[4:41] As haink drogh-spyrrydyn myrgeddin magh ass ymmodee, gyllagh as gra, Oo yn Creest Mac Yee. As hug eh oghsan daue, as cha lhig eh daue loayrt; son va fys oc dy nee eh va'n Creest.
[4:42] As 'sy vadran, jimmee eh roish, as hie eh gys boayl er-lheh: as va'n pobble briaght er e hon, as cheet huggey, as chionney er, eh dy uirriaght m&acirc;roo.
[4:43] As dooyrt eh roo, Shegin dooys reeriaght Yee y phreacheil gys ard-valjyn elley myrgeddin: son er yn oyr shen ta mee er my choyrt.
[4:44] As ren eh preacheil ayns kialteenyn Ghalilee.
[5:1] As haink eh gy-kione myr va'n pobble chionney stiagh er dy chlashtyn goo Yee, as eh ny hassoo liorish faarkey Ghennesareth,
[5:2] As honnick eh daa lhong rish oirr y traie: agh va ny eeasteyryn er n'gholl assdoo, as v'ad niee yn lieen.
[5:3] As hie eh er-board unnane jeh ny lhongyn va lesh Simon, as ghuee eh er, eh dy heiy magh tammylt veih yn thalloo: as hoie eh sheese, as dynsee eh yn pobble ass y lhong.
[5:4] Nish tra v'eh erreish loayrt, dooyrt eh rish Simon, Ymmyrt-jee magh gys y diunid, as cuir-jee yn lieen son tayrn.
[5:5] As dreggyr Simon as dooyrt eh rish, Vainshter, ta shin er hooilleil fud ny hoie, as cha vel shin er ghoaill monney: ny-yeih er dty ockle's cuir-yms yn lieen.
[5:6] As tra v'ad er n'yannoo shoh chruinnee ad dy cheilley lheid yn earroo mooar dy eeastyn; dy row yn lieen oc brishey.
[5:7] As chrie ad er ny parteeassyn oc v'ayns y lhong elley, ad dy heet dy chooney lhieu. As haink ad, as lhieen ad y daa lhong, myr shen dy row ad ayns gaue goll fo.
[5:8] Tra honnick Simon Peddyr shoh, huitt eh sheese ec glioonyn Yeesey, gra, Immee voym, son ta mee my ghooinney peccoil, O Hiarn.
[5:9] Son ghow eshyn, as ooilley ny va m&acirc;rish, yindys mooar jeh'n lught dy eeastyn v'ad er ghoaill:
[5:10] Myr ren neesht Jamys as Ean mec Zebedee, va nyn barteeassyn marish Simon. As dooyrt Yeesey rish Simon, Ny bee aggle ort, veih shoh magh nee oo goaill deiney.
[5:11] As tra v'ad er chur lhieu nyn lhongyn gys thalloo, hreig ad ooilley, as deiyr ad er.
[5:12] As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'eh ayns ard-valley dy row, cur-my-ner, dooinney lane jeh'n louraneys: as tra honnick eh Yeesey, huitt eh sheese er e eddin, jannoo aghin huggey as gra, Hiarn, my she dty aigney eh, foddee oo mish y yannoo glen.
[5:13] As heeyn eh magh e laue, as venn eh rish, gra, M'aigney's eh; bee er dty ghlenney. As chelleeragh daag y louraneys eh.
[5:14] As hug eh currym er gyn eh dy insh shoh da dooinney erbee: agh immee, as jeeagh oo hene da'n taggyrt, as cheb son dty ghlenney, myr ta Moses er harey, dy ve son feanish daue.
[5:15] Agh wheesh shen smoo hie goo magh jeh: as haink earrooyn mooarey dy leih cooidjagh dy chlashtyn, as dy ve er nyn lheihys liorish jeh nyn aslayntyn.
[5:16] Agh hie eshyn eh-hene roish gys yn aasagh, dy ghoaill padjer.
[5:17] As haink eh gy-kione laa dy row, myr v'eh gynsaghey, dy row Phariseeyn as fir-ynsee yn leigh nyn soie liorish, v'er jeet magh ass ooilley baljyn Ghalilee, as Judea as Jerusalem: as va pooar y Chiarn feer vreeoil m&acirc;rish ayns lheihys doghanyn.
[5:18] As cur-my-ner, hug sleih lhieu ayns lhiabbee dooinney va ching jeh'n palsee: as v'ad shirrey y chur lhieu stiagh eh, dy hoiaghey eh kiongoyrt rish
[5:19] As tra nagh row saase erbee oc dy chur lhieu stiagh eh kyndagh rish chennid y phobble, hie ad seose er mullagh y thie, as lhig ad sheese ny hrooid, eh-hene as e lhaibbee, er y laare kiongoyrt rish Yeesey.
[5:20] As tra hug eh tastey da'n chredjue oc, dooyrt eh rish, Ghooinney, ta dty pheccaghyn er nyn leih dhyt.
[5:21] As ren ny scrudeyryn as ny Phariseeyn toshiaght dy phleadeil ry-cheilley, gra, Quoi eh shoh ta loayrt goan mollaghtagh? Quoi oddys peccaghyn y leih, agh Jee ny lomarcan?
[5:22] Agh va fys ec Yeesey er ny smooinaghtyn oc, as dreggyr eh, as dooyrt eh roo, Cre er ta shiu resooney ayns nyn greeaghyn?
[5:23] Quoi sassey dy ghra, Ta dty pheccagh yn er nyn leih dhyt, ny dy ghra, Irree seose as shooill?
[5:24] Agh dy vod fys y ve eu, dy vel pooar ec Mac y dooinney er y thalloo dy leih peccaghyn (dooyrt eh rishyn va ching jeh'n chingys craa-ee.) Ta mee gra rhtt, Irree, as trog seose dty lhiabbee, as gow royd gys dty hie.
[5:25] As chelleeragh dirree eh seose kiongoyrt roo, as hrog eh shen v'eh ny lhie er, as jimmee eh gys e hie, cur moylley da Jee.
[5:26] As ghow ad ooilley lane yindys, as ren ad Jee y ghloyraghey, as v'ad lhieent lesh aggle, gra, Ta shin er vakin reddyn yindyssagh jiu.
[5:27] As ny lurg shoh hie eh magh, as honnick eh publican va enmyssit Levi, ny hoie ec boayrd y cheesh: as dooyrt eh rish, Eiyr orrym's.
[5:28] As daag eh ooilley as dirree eh seose, as deiyr eh er.
[5:29] As ren Levi aarlaghey mooar er e hon ayns e hie hene: as va sheshaght vooar dy phublicanee as dy eallagh elley nyn soie ec y voayrd m&acirc;roo.
[5:30] Agh va ny scrudeyryn oc as ny Phariseeyn jymmoosagh rish e ynseydee, gra, Cre'n-fa ta shiu gee as giu marish publicanee as peccee?
[5:31] As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Cha vel feme ocsyn ta slane er yn er-lhee: agh ec sleih chingey.
[5:32] Cha daink mish dy eamagh er yn vooinjer chairagh, agh er peccee gys arrys.
[5:33] As dooyrt ad roo, Cre'n-fa ta ynseydee Ean trostey dy mennick, as jannoo padjeryn, as myrgeddin ynseydee ny Phariseeyn; agh ta'n vooinjer ayd's gee as giu?
[5:34] As dooyrt eh roo, Bailliu mooinjer y chamyr-phoosee dy hrostey, choud as ta dooinney yn phoosee m&acirc;roo?
[5:35] Agh hig ny laghyn, tra vees dooinney yn phoosee er ny ghoaill ersooyl voue, as eisht nee ad trostey ayns ny laghyn shen.
[5:36] As loayr eh myrgeddin coraa-dorraghey roo, Cha vel dooinney erbee cur peesh dy eaddagh noa er shenn gharmad: er-nonney, ta chammah yn noa raipey yn laane lesh, as cha vel yn pheesh va goit ass yn noa coardail rish y chenn
[5:37] As cha vel dooinney erbee cur feeyn noa ayns shenn voteilyn er-nonney scoltee yn feeyn noa ny boteilyn, as bee eh deayrit, as bee ny boteilyn dy choayl er.
[5:38] Agh shegin da feeyn noa v'er ny chur ayns boteilyn noa; as t'ad ny-neesht sauchey.
[5:39] Chamoo ta dooinney erbee, erreish da v'er n'iu shenn feeyn, chelleeragh shirrey feeyn noa: son t'eh gra, Ta'n shenn ny share.
[6:1] AS haink eh gy-kione er y chied doonaght lurg yn nah laa jeh'n chaisht, myr v'eh goll trooid ny magheryn-arrooo dy ren e ynseydee ny jeeassyn y phluckey, as rubbey yn arroo assdoo ayns nyn laueyn ren ad gee jeh.
[6:2] As dooyrt shiartanse jeh ny Phariseeyn roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu jannoo shen nagh vel lowal dy ve jeant er laghyn y doonaght?
[6:3] As dreggyr Yeesey ad, gra, Nagh vel shiu er lhaih wheesh shoh, cre ren David tra v'eh hene as e heshaght accryssagh:
[6:4] Kys hie eh stiagh ayns thie Yee, as ghow eh as d'ee eh yn arran casherick, as hug eh eh myrgeddin dauesyn va marish, ga nagh row eh lowit dy ve eeit, agh liorish ny sag gyrtyn ny-lomarcan?
[6:5] As dooyrt eh roo, Dy row yn Mac dooinney ny Hiarn myrgeddin er y doonaght.
[6:6] As haink eh gy-kione er doonaght elley, dy jagh eh stiagh ayns y synagogne, as dy dynsee eh: as va dooinney ayns shen va'n laue yesh echey er shyrgaghey.
[6:7] As va sooill gheyre ec ny scruderyn as ny Phariseeyn er, dy yeeaghyn jinnag eh eh y lheihys er laa yn doonaght: dy voddagh cooish chassid 've oc n'oi.
[6:8] Agh va fys echeysyn er ny smooinaghtyn oc, as dooyrt eh rish y dooinney lesh y laue shyrgit, Irree seose as shass magh er y laare. As dirree eh, as hass eh magh.
[6:9] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, F&ecirc;nyms un red jiuish, Vel eh lowal er laghyn y doonaght dy yannoo mie, ny dy yannoo olk? dy hauail bioys, ny dy stroie eh?
[6:10] As yeeagh eh mygeayrt orroo ooilley, as dooyrt eh rish y dooinney, Sheeyn magh dty laue. As ren eh shen; as va'n laue echey er ny lheihys myr y laue elley.
[6:11] As v'adsyn myr deiney baanrit; as hug ad nyn goyrle dy cheilley, cre dy yannoo rish Yeesey.
[6:12] As haink eh gy-kione ayns ny laghyn shen, dy jagh eh seose er slieau dy ghoaill padjer, as dy ren eh tannaghtyn fud ny hoie ayns padjer gys Jee.
[6:13] As tra va'n laa er hoilshagh, de&iuml;e eh er e ynseydee huggey: as jeusyn reih eh ghhaa-yeig, denmys eh myrgeddin nyn os tyllyn:
[6:14] Simon (denmys eh myrgeddin Peddyr) as Andreays e vraar, Jamys as Ean, Philip as Parlane,
[6:15] Mian as Thomase, Jamys mac Alpheus, as Simon va enmyssit Zelotes
[6:16] As Judas braar Yamys, as Yuaase Iscariot, va myrgeddin yn traitoor.
[6:17] As haink eh neose maroo gys y cheer-rea, as haggil huggey sheshaght e eiyrtee, as earroo mooar dy leih veih ooilley Judea as Jerusalem, as veih ardjyn ny marrey Tyre as Sidon, haink dy eaishtagh rish, as dy ve er nyn lheihys jeh nyn ghoghanyn;
[6:18] As adsyn va seaghnit lesh spyrrydyn neu-ghlen; as v'ad er nyn lheihys.
[6:19] As va'n slane chaglym shirrey bentyn rish: son va bree goll magh ass, va dyn lheihys ad ooilley.
[6:20] As hrog eh seose e hooillyn er e eiyrtee, as dooyrt eh, Bannit ta shiuish voghtyn: son lhieuish reeriaght Yee.
[6:21] Bannit ta shiuish ta accryssagh nish: son bee shiu er nyn yannoo magh. Bannit ta shiuish ta nish dobberan: son nee shiu garaghtee.
[6:22] Bannit ta shiuish, tra ta deiney cur feoh diu, as tra nee ad nyn scarrey shiu voue, as nyn oltooaney shiu, as nyn ennym y ghiarey magh myr olk, er coontey Mac y dooinney.
[6:23] Bee-jee dy ghien mie ayns y laa shen, as lheim-jee son boggey son cur-my-ner, s'mooar ta nyn leagh ayns niau: son er yn aght cheddin ren ny shenn-ayryn oc rish ny phadeyryn.
[6:24] Agh smerg diuish verchee: son ta shiu er gheddyn nyn gherjagh.
[6:25] Smerg diuish ta lane: son bee shiu accryssagh. Smerg diuish ta garaghtee nish: son nee shiu dobberan as keayney.
[6:26] Smerg diuish tra nee dy chooilley ghooinney loayrt dy mie jiu: son shen myr ren ny ayraghyn oc jeh ny phadeyryn foalsey.
[6:27] Agh ta mish gra riuish ta clashtyn, Bee-jee graihagh er nyn noidyn, bee-jee dooie roosyn ta cur feoh diu:
[6:28] Bannee-jee adsyn ta gwee mollaght diu, as gow-jee padjer er nyn son ocsyn ta cur seaghyn erriu.
[6:29] As huggeysyn woaillys oo er y derrey lieckan, chyndaa myrgeddin yn lieckan elley: as eshyn ghoys ersooyl dty chloagey, ny bee noi dty chooat y lhiggey lesh myrgeddin.
[6:30] Cur da dy chooilley ghooinney ta jannoo aghin hood; as jehsyn ta goaill ersooyl dty chooid vo&iuml;d, ny shir ad reesht.
[6:31] As myr bailliuish deiney dy yannoo riuish, jean-jee shiuish myrgeddin roosyn.
[6:32] Son my ta shiu dooie dauesyn ta dooie riu, s'beg ta nyn mooise; son ta eer drogh-yantee dooie dauesyn ta dooie roo.
[6:33] As my ta shiu jannoo mie dauesyn ta jannoo mie diuish, cre'n booise ta nyn gour? son ta ny eer drogh-yantee jannoo yn lheid cheddin.
[6:34] As my ta shiu geeasaght dauesyn voue ta shiu jeeaghyn son cooilleeney, cre ta nyn mooise? son ta eer drogh-sleih geeasaght da drogh-sleih; dy gheddyn wheesh cheddin reesht.
[6:35] Agh cur-jee graih da nyn noidyn, as jean-jee mie, as eeasee-jee, fegooish jerkal rish veg y gheddyn reesht: as s'mooar vees nyn leagh! as bee shiu cloan yn Er-syrjey: son t'eh dooie da'n vooinjer neu-wooisal as ny mee-chrauee.
[6:36] Bee-jee er-y-fa shen myghinagh, myr ta'n Ayr eu myrgeddin myghinagh.
[6:37] Ny jean-jee briwnys, as cha bee shiu er nyn mriwnys: ny jean-jee deyrey, as cha bee shiu er nyn gheyrey: leih-jee, as yiow shiu leih:
[6:38] Jean-jee coyrt, as bee eh er ny choyrt diu; towse mie, jingit sheese, as criht cooidjagh, as roie harrish, ver deiney diu ayns nyn oghrish. Son lesh y towse cheddin ta shiu towse, bee eh er ny howse diu reesht.
[6:39] As loayr eh coraa-dorraghey roo, Vod y doal shooyll kione y doal? as nagh duitt ad ny-neesht ayns y jeeg?
[6:40] Cha vel y schoillar erskyn e vainshter: agh bee dy chooilley unnane ta slane-ynsit, corrym rish e vainshter.
[6:41] As cre'n-fa t'ou cronnaghey yn brenneein t'ayns sooill dty vraarey, agh cha vel oo gennaghtyn yn darrag t'ayns dty hooill hene?
[6:42] Ny kys oddys oo gra rish dty vraar, Vraar, lhig dou yn brenneein y ghoaill ass dty hooill's, tra nagh vel oo goaill tastey dy vel darrag ayns dty hooill hene? Er-crauee-oalsey, tilg hoshiaght yn darrag ass dty hooill hene, eisht bee soilshey ayd dy ghoaill yn brenneein ass sooill dty vraarey.
[6:43] Son cha vel billey mie tilgey drogh vess: ny drogh villey tilgey mess mie.
[6:44] Son ta dy chooilley villey er ny chronnaghey liorish e vess: son cha vel mess y villey figgagh er ny heiy jeh drineyn, ny mess y villey-feeyney jeh thammag-ghress.
[6:45] Ta dooinney mie ass stoyr mie e chree, cur magh shen ny ta mie: as drogh-ghooinney ass drogh stoyr e chree, gymmyrkey shen ny ta olk: son magh ass stoyr y chree ta'n beeal loayrt.
[6:46] As cre'n-fa ta shiu dy my enmys Hiarn, Hiarn, fegooish jannoo ny reddyn ta mee dy ghra?
[6:47] Quoi-erbee ta cheet hym's, as clashtyn my ghoan, as jannoo ymmyd mie jeu, jeeaghym's diu quoi rish t'eh er ny hoylaghey.
[6:48] T'eh er ny hoylaghey rish dooinney ren thie y hroggal, as chleiy dy dowin, as hoie yn undin er creg: as tra dhatt yn ushtey, vrish yn thooilley stiagh dy trome er y thie shen, agh cha yiarg eh er y chraa eh; er-yn-oyr dy row yn undin echey er creg.
[6:49] Agh eshyn ta clashtyn as nagh vel jannoo ymmyd mie jeh, t'eh goll-rish dooinney, ren fegooish undin thie y hroggal er yn ooir, as ren y thooilley brishey stiagh dy trome, as chelleeragh huitt eh, as s'mooar va toyrt-mow yn thie shen.
[7:1] NISH tra v'eh erreish ooilley ny goan shoh y loayrt ayns clashtyn y phobble, hie eh stiagh ayns Calpernaum.
[7:2] As va centurion dy row va fer-mooinjerey echey, v'eh dy mooar soiaghey jeh, as v'eh ching, as raad y vaaish.
[7:3] As tra cheayll eh jeh Yeesey, hug eh shanstyr ny Hewnyn huggey, guee er eh dy heet dy laanaghey e er-mooinjerey.
[7:4] As tra v'ad er jeet gys Yeesey, ren ad aghin huggey dy jeean, gra, Dy row eshyn feeu v'eh dy yannoo shoh er y hon:
[7:5] Son t'eh ny charrey da'n ashoon ain, as t'eh er hroggal synagogue dooin.
[7:6] Eisht hie Yeesey m&acirc;roo. As tra v'eh er jeet er-gerrey da'n thie, hug y centurion caarjyn huggey, gra rish, Hiarn, ny boir oo hene, son cha vel mish feeu oo dy heet stiagh fo my chlea.
[7:7] As er-yn-oyr shen cha yeeagh mee orrym pene dy ve feeu dy heet hood: agh loayr y fockle, as nee my er-mooinjerey coural.
[7:8] Son ta mish mee hene my ghooinney ayns pooar, as ta sidooryn aym foym, as ta mee gra rish shoh, Immee, as t'eh goll: as rish fer elley, Tar, as t'eh cheet: as rish my harvaant, Jean shoh, as t'eh dy yannoo eh.
[7:9] Tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, ghow eh yindys, as hyndaa eh mygeayrt, as dooyrt eh rish y pobble va geiyrt er, Ta mee gra riu, Lheid y credjue lajer shoh, cha vel mee er gheddyn ayns Israel hene.
[7:10] As tra haink ny chaghteryn reesht gys y thie, hooar ad dy row yn fer-mooinjerey va ching dy slane er choural.
[7:11] As haink eh gy-kione yn laa er-giyn dy jagh eh gys ard-valley va enmyssit Nain, as hie ymmodee jeh e ynseydee marish, as mooarrane sleih.
[7:12] Nish tra haink eh er-gerrey da giat yn ard-valley, cur-my-ner, va sleih cur lhieu magh dooinney marroo, va ny ynrycan mac da e voir, as v'eeish ny ben-treoghe: as va ymmodee jeh sleih yn ard-valley m&acirc;ree.
[7:13] As tra honnick y Chiarn ee, va chymmey echey urree, as dooyrt eh r'ee, Ny jean keayney.
[7:14] As haink eh, as venn eh rish y carbyd (as hass adsyn va fo) as dooyrt eh, Ghooinney aeg, ta mee gra rhyt, Irree.
[7:15] As hoie yn dooinney marroo seose, as ren eh toshiaght dy loayrt: as livrey eh eh gys e vo1r.
[7:16] As haink aggle orroo ooilley: as hug ad moylley da Jee, gra, Ta phadeyr mooar er n'irree seose ny mast' ain; as, Ta Jee er yeeaghyn er e phobble.
[7:17] As hie yn goo shoh magh my-e-chione trooid ooilley Judea, as trooid ooilley yn cheer mygeayrt.
[7:18] As hug ynseydee Ean coontey da jeh ooilley ny reddyn shoh.
[7:19] As deie Ean er jees jeh e ynseydee as hug eh ad er chaghteraght gys Yeesey, gra, Nee uss Eh va ry-hoi cheet, ny vel shin dy yeeaghyn son fer elley?
[7:20] Tra va ny deiney er jeet huggey, dooyrt ad, Ta Ean Bastey er nyn goyrt shin dy &ecirc;naght jeed, Nee uss Eh va ry-hoi cheet, ny vel shin dy yeeaghyn son fer elley?
[7:21] As ayns yn oor cheddin v'eh lheihys ymmodee jeh ny aslayntyn as ny doghanyn, as ny drogh-spyrrydyn oc, as da ymmodee va doal v'eh coyrt soilshey.
[7:22] Eisht dregyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee reue, as insh-jee da Ean cre y reddyn ta shiu er vakin as er chlashtyn kys dy vel ny doail geddyn nyn soilshey, ny croobee shooyll, ny louraanee er nyn ghlenney, ny beuyr clashtyn, ny merriu er nyn mioghey, as y sushtal er ny phreacheil da ny boghtyn.
[7:23] As bannit ta eshyn nagh jean beg y hoiaghey jeem's.
[7:24] As tra va chaghteryn Ean er n'immeeaght, ren eh toshiaght dy ghra rish y pobble mychione Ean, Cre hie shiu magh gys yn aasagh dy akin? Nee cuirtliagh criht lesh y gheay.
[7:25] Agh cre hie shiu magh dy akin? Dooinney soit magh ayns coamrey moyrnagh! Cur-my-ner t'adsyn ta ceau coamrey costal, as farrail dy seyr, ayns plaaseyn reeoil.
[7:26] Agh cre hie shiu magh dy akin? Phadeyr? dy jarroo, ta mee gra riu, as fer s'ooasle na phadeyr.
[7:27] Shoh eh jeh te scruit, Cur-my-ner, ta mee cur my haghter magh royd, dy chiartaghey yn raad kiongoyrt rhyt.
[7:28] Son ta mee gra riu, Ny mast' oc syn t'er nyn ruggey jeh mraane, cha vel phadeyr syrjey na Ean Bashtey: agh ta'n fer sloo t'ayns reeriaght Yee ny syrjey na eshyn.
[7:29] As ren ooilley yn pobble cheayll eh as ny publicanee Jee y heyrey, as v'ad er nyn mashtey lesh bashtey Ean.
[7:30] Agh ren ny Phariseeyn as fir-ynsee yn leigh soiaghey beg jeh coyrle Yee nyn 'o&iuml; oc hene, as cha row ad er nyn mashtey liorish.
[7:31] As dooyrt y Chiarn, Cre gys nee'm deiney yn cheeloghe shoh y hoylaghey? as cre rish t'ad goll?
[7:32] T'ad goll-rish cloan, ta nyn soie ayns ny margaghyn, geamagh yn derrey yeh gys y jeh elley, as gra, Ta shin er n'yannoo bingys diu, as cha vel shiu er ghaunsin: ta shin er hroggal bardoon diu, as cha vel shiu er ghobberan.
[7:33] Son cha daink Ean Bashtey gee arran, ny giu feeyn; as ta shiu gra, Ta drogh spyrryd echey.
[7:34] Ta'n Mac dooinney er jeet gee as giu; as ta shiu gra, Cur-my-ner dooinney jollyssagh, as iuder-feeyney, carrey dy phublicanee as dy pheccee.
[7:35] Agh ta creenaght er ny heyrey liorish ooilley e cloan.
[7:36] As chuir fer jeh ny Phariseeyn eh gys bee marish. As hie eh stiagh ayns thie yn Pharisee, as hoie eh sheese gys bee.
[7:37] As cur-my-ner va ben ayns yn ard-valley, va ny drogh yantagh, tra va fys eck dy row Yeesey ny hoie ec bee ayns thie yn Pharisee, hug ee lh'ee box alabaster dy ooil chostal.
[7:38] As hass ee ec e chassyn cheu e chooylloo keayney, as ren ee toshiaght dy niee e chassyn lesh jeir, as rub ee ad lesh folt e king, as phaag ee e chassyn, as ren ee ad y ooillaghey lesh yn ooil.
[7:39] Nish yn Pharisee ren y chuirrey eh, tra honnick eh shoh, loayr eh cheu-sthie jeh hene, gra, Veagh fys er ve ec y dooinney shoh, dy beagh eh ny adeyr, quoi, as cre'n monney dy ven ee shoh, ta bentyn rish: son t'ee ny ben pheccoil.
[7:40] As dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh rish, Simon, ta red aym's dy ghra rhyt, As dooyrt eh, Abbyr eh, vainshter.
[7:41] Va dooinney dy row, as jees ayns lhiastynys da: va'n derrey yeh lhiastyn queig cheead ping, as y jeh elley jeih pingyn as da-eed.
[7:42] As tra nagh row oc dy eeck, leih eh daue ny-neesht dy arryltagh. Insh dou eisht, quoi jeu s'booisal vees da?
[7:43] Dreggyr Simon as dooyrt eh, Er-lhiam dy nee eshyn, da smoo ren eh leih. As dooyrt eh rish, T'ou er vriwnys dy cairagh.
[7:44] As hyndaa eh gys y ven, as dooyrt eh rish Simon, Vel oo cur-my-ner yn ven shoh? Haink mee stiagh ayns dty hie's, as cha dug oo dou ushtey son my chassyn: agh t'eeish er niee my chassyn lesh jeir, as er jyrmagh ad lesh folt e king.
[7:45] Cha dug uss paag dou: agh ta'n ven shoh, er-dyn traa haink mee stiagh, er ve kinjagh paagey my chassyn.
[7:46] My chione lesh ooil cha ren oo y ooillaghey: agh ta'n ven shoh er n'ooillaghey my chassyn lesh ooil.
[7:47] Shen-y-fa ta mee gra rhyt, Ta ny peccaghyn eck ta ymmodee, er nyn leih jee: shen-y-fa wheesh shen smoo ta yn ghraih eck: agh dasyn ta beggan er ny leih, cha vel e ghraih agh beggan.
[7:48] As dooyrt eh r'ee, Ta dty pheccaghyn er nyn leih dhyt.
[7:49] As ren y vooinjer va nyn soie ec bee m&acirc;rish, toshiaght dy ghra cheu-sthie jeu hene, Quoi eh shoh ta myrgeddin leih peccaghyn?
[7:50] As dooyrt eh rish y ven, Ta dty chredjue er dty hauail; immee ayns shee.
[8:1] As haink eh gy-kione ny lurg shen, dy jagh eh trooid dy chooilley valley, mooar as beg preacheil as soilshaghey sushtal gerjoilagh reeriaght Yee: as va'n daa ostyl yeig marish:
[8:2] As shiartanse dy vraane, v'er nyn lheihys jeh drogh-spyrrydyn, as aslayntyn, Moirrey va enmyssit Malaine, ass-jee hie shiaght drogh-spyrrydyn,
[8:3] As Joanna ben Chusa stiurt Herod, as Susanna, as ymmodee elley, v'er hirveish er Jeh nyn gooid.
[8:4] As tra va earroo mooar dy leih er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, as er jeet huggey ass dy chooilley ard-valley; loayr eh liorish coraa dorraghey:
[8:5] Hie correyder magh dy chuir e rass: as myr v'eh cuir, huitt paart rish oirr y raad, as ve stampit sheese, as d'ee eeanlee yn aer eh.
[8:6] As huitt paart er creg, as cha leah as ve er n'aase seose, hie eh naardey, er-yn-oyr dy row eh laccal soo.
[8:7] As huitt paart mastey drineyn, as daase ny drineyn seose m&acirc;rish, as phloogh ad eh.
[8:8] As huitt cooid elley jeh ayns thalloo mie, as daase eh seose, as dymmyrk eh mess keead-filley. As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, de&iuml;e eh, Eshyn ta cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn, lhig da clashtyn.
[8:9] As d&ecirc;nee e ostyllyn jeh, gra, Cre ta er ny hoiggal liorish y coraa-dorraghey shoh?
[8:10] As dooyrt eh, Diuish te er ny choyrt dy hoiggal folliaghtyn reeriaght Yee; agh da feallagh elley ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey: ga t'ad fakin cha vel ad cur-my-ner, as clashtyn cha vel ad toiggal.
[8:11] Nish shoh bun y choraa-dorraghey: Yn rass goo Yee.
[8:12] Shen rish oirr y raad, yn vooinjer ta clashtyn: eisht ta'n drogh-spyrryd cheet, as goaill ersooyl yn goo ass ny creeaghyn oc, er-aggle dy jinnagh ad credjal, as dy beagh ad er nyn sauail.
[8:13] Adsyn er y chreg, yn vooinjer, tra t'ad er chlashtyn, ta goaill y goo dy arryltagh; as cha vel fraue oc shoh, son tammylt t'ad credjal, agh ayns earish miolagh ta nyn gredjue failleil.
[8:14] As shen huitt mastey drineyn, yn vooinjer, tra t'ad er chlashtyn, ta goll magh as ta plooghit lesh kiarail as berchys, as eunyssyn y vea shoh, as cha vel ad gymmyrkey magh mess gys lhieeney vie.
[8:15] Agh shen er y thalloo mie, yn vooinjer ta lesh creeaghyn onneragh as mie, er chlashtyn yn goo, as ta dy reayll oc eh, as cur magh mess lesh meenid.
[8:16] Cha vel doooinney erbee, tra t'eh er voaddey cainle, dy choodaghey ee lesh saagh ny dy choyrt ee fo lhiabbee: agh soiaghey ee ayns cainleyr, dy vod adsyn ta cheet stiagh yn soilshey y akin.
[8:17] Son cha vel nhee erbee follit, nagh jig gys soilshey: ny nhee erbee kiellit, nagh bee fys er, as nagh jig magh.
[8:18] Cur-jee twoaee er-y-fa shen kys ta shiu clashtyn: son quoi-erbee ta echey, dasyn vees er ny choyrt; as quoi-erbee nagh vel echey, veihsyn vees er ny ghoaill eer shen hene er-lesh dy vel echey.
[8:19] Eisht haink huggey e voir as e vraaraghyn, as cha voddagh ad cheet n'aare, kyndagh rish y chennid.
[8:20] As va shoh er ny insh da, lioroosyn dooyrt, Ta dty voir as dty vraaraghyn nyn shassoo mooie, geearee dy dty akin.
[8:21] Agh dreggyr eh, as dooyrt eh roo, My voir as my vraaraghyn ad shoh ta clashtyn goo Yee, as ta dy yannoo eh.
[8:22] Nish haink eh gy-kione, er laa dy row, dy jagh eh er-board lhong marish e ostyllyn: as dooyrt eh roo, Lhig dooin goll harrish gys y cheu elley jeh'n logh. As hie ad magh son y cheayn.
[8:23] Agh myr v'ad shiaulley, huitt eh ny chadley: as dirree sterrym mooar dy gheay er y cheayn, as lhieen yn ushtey stiagh orroo, dy row ad ayns gaue.
[8:24] As haink ad huggey as ghooisht ad eh, gra, Vainshter, vainshter, bee mayd caillit. Eisht dirree eh, as smaghtee eh yn gheay as freaney ny tonnyn: as ghow ad fea, as va kiuney ayn.
[8:25] As dooyrt eh roo, Cre vel y credjue eu? As va aggle orroo, goaill yindys as gra ry-cheilley, Cre'n monney dy ghooinney eh shoh? son t'eh cur ny eer geayghyn as yn ushtey fo harey, as t'ad ayns biallys da.
[8:26] As haink ad gys cheer ny Gadarenee ta harrish noi Galilee.
[8:27] As tra v'eh er n'gholl er thalloo, haink ny whail ass yn ard-valley, dooinney dy row va ry-foddey seaghnit lesh drogh-spyrrydyn, as cha row eh ceau eaddagh, chamoo duirree eh ayns thie erbee, agh mastey ny hoaiaghyn.
[8:28] Tra honnick eh Yeesey, dyllee eh, as huitt eh sheese kiongoyrt rish, as dooyrt eh lesh ard-choraa, Cre'n eie t'ayd orrym Yeesey, Vac yn Jee smoo ard? Guee-ym ort nagh jean oo my horchaghey.
[8:29] (Son v'eh er harey yn spyrryd neu ghlen dy heet magh ass y dooinney. Son v'eh dy mennick er hoiaghey er: as v'eh freilt kianlt lesh geulaghyn, as ayns yiarnyn; as vrish eh ny geulaghyn, as v'eh er ny ve eiyrit liorish y drogh-spyrryd gys yn aasagh.)
[8:30] As d&ecirc;nee Yeesey jeh, gra, Cre'n ennym t'ort? As dooyrt eh, Legion: er-yn oyr dy row ymmodee drogh-spyrrydyn er n'gholl stiagh ayn.
[8:31] As ghuee ad er gyn eh dy oardaghey daue goll sheese gys y diunid.
[8:32] As va griagh mooar dy vuckyn fo bochillyn er y clieau: as ghuee ad er, eh dy chur kied daue goll stiagh ayndoo. As hug eh kied daue.
[8:33] Eisht hie ny drogh-spyrrydyn ass y dooinney, as hie ad stiagh ayns ny muckyn: as roie yn ghriagh gour nyn mullee lesh yn eaynee gys y cheayn, as v'ad plooghit.
[8:34] Tra honnick ny bochillyn cre va jeant, roie ad roue, as hie ad as dinsh ad eh ayns yn ard-valley, as trooid y cheer.
[8:35] Eisht hie ad magh dy yeeaghyn cre va jeant; as haink ad gys Yeesey, as hooar ad y dooinney, ass va ny drogh spyrrydyn er n'gholl, ny hoie ec cassyn Yeesey, as e eaddagh er, as v'eh dy mie ayns e cheeayl: as ghow ad aggle.
[8:36] Dinsh myrgeddin yn vooinjer honnick eh daue, kys va fer ny drogh-spyrrydyn er ny lheihys.
[8:37] Eisht ren y slane chaglym jeh cheer y Gadalenee mygeayrt, guee er eh dy gholl roish: son va aggle mooar er duittym orroo: as hie eh er-board yn lhong, as hyndaa eh back reesht.
[8:38] Nish va'n dooinney ass va ny drogh spyrrydyn er n'immeeaght geearree dy ve marish: agh hug Yeesey ersooyl eh, gra,
[8:39] Gow royd gys dty hie hene, as soilshee cre ny reddyn mooarey ta Jee er n'yannoo er dty hon. As hie eh roish, as dinsh eh magh trooid ooilley yn ard-valley, cre ny reddyn mooarey va Yeesey er n'yannoo er e hon.
[8:40] As haink eh gy-kione, tra va Yeesey er jeet back, dy ghow yn pobble lane boggey jeh: son v'ad ooilley fieau er.

[8:42] Son va un ynrycan inneen echey, va mysh daa vlein jeig dy eash, as v'ee raad y vaaish. (Agh myr v'eh goll, va'n pobble chionney er.
[8:43] As va ben va roie foalley er ve eck rish daa vlein jeig, v'er vaarail ooilley e cooid-seihlt er fir-lhee, as cha daink eh lesh veg jeu ee y lheihys,
[8:44] Haink ee shoh cheu e chooylloo, as venn ee rish oirr e gharmad: as chelleeragh hyrmee yn roie-foalley eck.
[8:45] As dooyrt Yeesey, Quoi venn rhym? Tra ren ooilley gobbal, dooyrt Peddyr, as adsyn va marish, Vainshter, ta'n pohble chionney ort, as dy dty yingey, as t'ou uss gra, Quoi venn rhym?
[8:46] As dooyrt Yeesey, Ta peccagh ennagh er ventyn rhym: son ta mee gennaghtyn dy vel bree er n'gholl ass-ym.

[8:48] As dooyrt eh r'ee, Inneen, bee dy ghien mie; ta dty chredjue er dty laanaghey: immee ayns shee.)
[8:49] Choud as v'eh foast loayrt, haink fer veih thie fer-reill yn synagogue, gra rish, Ta dty inneen marroo; ny cur trubbyl sodjey da'n Vainshter.
[8:50] Agh tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, dreggyr eh eh, gra, Ny bee aggle ort: cha vel ort agh dy chredjal, as bee ee er ny lheihys.
[8:51] As tra v'eh er jeet stiagh 'sy thie, cha lhig eh da dooinney erbee goll stiagh marish, agh Peddyr, as Jamys, as Ean, as ayr as moir y ven-aeg.
[8:52] As v'ad ooilley keayney, as jannoo dobberan er e son: agh dooyrt eshyn, Ny jean-jee keayney; cha vel ee marroo, agh ny cadley.

[9:1] Eisht deie eh er y daa ostyl yeig cooidjagh, as hug eh daue pooar as eaghtyrys harrish dy chooilley ghrogh-spyrryd, as dy lheihys doghanyn.
[9:2] As hug eh ad magh dy phreacheil reeriaght Yee, as dy laanaghey sleih chingey.
[9:3] As dooyrt eh roo, Ny cur-jee lhieu nhee erbee son nyn yurnah, chamoo luirg, ny spagey, ny arran, ny argid; as ny lhig da daa chooat y pheesh y ve eu.
[9:4] As thie erbee dy jed shiu stiagh ayn, gow-jee aaght ayns shen, derrey hed shiu reue.

[9:7] Nish va Herod yn tetrarch er chlasht yn jeh ooilley e yannoo: as v'eh seaghnit, er-y-fa dy row paart gra, dy row Ean er n'irree veih ny merriu:

[9:13] Agh dooyrt eh roo, Cur-jee shiuish bee daue. As dooyrt ad, Cha vel ain agh queig bwilleenyn as daa eeast; mannagh jem mayd dy chionnaghey bee son ooilley yn pobble shoh.

[9:17] As ren ad ooilley gee, as v'ad er nyn yannoo magh: as hrog ad jeh'n fooilliagh daag ad, lane daa vaskad jeig.

[9:22] Gra, Shegin da Mac y dooinney ymmodee reddyn y hurranse, as ve beg soit jeh liorish y chanstyr, as ny ard-saggyrtyn, as ny scrudeyryn, as ve er ny varroo, as girree reesht yn trass laa.
[9:23] As dooyrt eh roo ooilley, My ta dooinney erbee aggindagh geiyrt orrym's lhig da eh-hene y obbal, as e chrosh y hroggal gagh laa, as geiyrt orrym.

[10:1] Ny lurg shoh, doardee yn Chiarn three-feed as jeih elley, as hug eh ad magh jees as jees roish hene, gys dy chooilley ard valley as ynnyd, raad v'eh hene ry-hoi cheet.
[10:2] Shen-y-fa dooyrt eh roo, Ta'n fouyr dy jarroo mooar, agh ta ny labreeyn beggan: guee-jee shiuish er-y-fa shen er Chiarn y fouyr, eh dy chur magh labreeyn gys y fouyr echey.
[10:3] Immee-jee eisht: cur-jee my-ner, ta mish dyn goyrt shiu magh myr eayin mastey moddee-oaldey.
