[11:1] As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh ec padjer ayns ynnyd dy row, tra daag eh jeh, dy dooyrt fer jeh e ostyllyn rish, Hiarn ynsee dooinyn dy ghoaill padjer, myr dynsee Ean myrgeddin da ny ynseydee echeysyn.
[11:2] As dooyrt eh, Tra ghoys shiu padjer, abbyr-jee, Ayr ain t'ayns niau, Casherick dy row dty ennym. Dy jig dty reeriaght. Dty aigney dy row jeant er y thalloo, myr te ayns niau.
[11:3] Cur dooin laa Iurg laa nyn arran gagh laa.
[11:4] As leih dooin nyn beccaghyn; son ta shinyn myrgeddin leih da dy chooilley unnane ta ayns lhiastynys dooin. As ny leeid shin ayns miolagh, agh livrey shin veih olk.
[11:5] As dooyrt eh roo, Quoi jiuish vees carrey echey, as hed huggey ec main-oie, as jir rish, Charrey, eeasee dou three bwilleenyn;
[11:6] Son ta dooinney-mooinjerey dou, va er e yurnah, er jeet hym, as cha vel monney aym dy hoiaghey roish:
[11:7] As freggyr-ee eshyn veih cheu-sthie gra, Ny boir mee: ta'n dorrys nish jeight, as ta my chloan 'sy lhiabbee marym; cha voddym girree dy chur dhyt.
[11:8] Ta mee gra riu, Ga nagh n'irree eh dy chur da, er-coontey dy nee e charrey eh: ny-yeih kyndagh rish yn jeeanid echey, irree eh, as ver eh da whilleen as vees eh ny eme.
[11:9] As ta mish gra riuish, Yeearree-jee, as yiow shiu: shir-jee, as nee shiu feddyn: bee-jee aignagh fosley y gheddyn, as bee eh er ny osley diu.
[11:10] Son ta dy chooilley unnane ta geearree, geddyn: as y fer ta shirrey, feddyn: as eshyn ta aignagh fosley y gheddyn, bee eh er ny osley da.
[11:11] My nee mac arran y hirrey er fer jiuish ta ny ayr, nee clagh ver eh da? ny my hirrys eh eeast, jean eh ayns ynnyd eeast ard-nieu y chur da?
[11:12] Ny my hirrys eh ooh, jeb eh scorpion da?
[11:13] My ta toiggal er-y-fa shen euish, ta olk, kys dy choyrt giootyn mie da nyn gloan; cre-woad smoo nee yn Ayr flaunyssagh eu yn Spyrryd Noo y choyrt dauesyn ta jannoo aghin huggey?
[11:14] As v'eh tilgey magh drogh-spyrryd, as v'eh balloo. As haink eh gy-kione, tra va'n drogh-spyrryd er gholl ass dy loayr y balloo: as ghow yn pobble yindys.
[11:15] Agh dooyrt paart jeu, She liorish Beelzebub, yn ard drogh-spyrryd, t'eh castey drogh-spyrrydyn.
[11:16] As va feallagh elley er-chee prowal eh shirrey er cowrey veih niau.
[11:17] Agh eshyn toiggal ny smooinaghtyn oc dooyrt roo, Ta dy chooilley reeriaght ta girree-magh n'oi hene, er ny choyrt mow: as thie ta n'oi hene goll naardey.
[11:18] As my ta'n jouyl girree-magh n'oi hene, kys nee yn reeriaght echey shassoo? er-y-fa dy vel shiu gra, dy nee liorish Beelzebub ta mish castey drogh-spyrrydyn.
[11:19] As my ta mish liorish Beelzebub castey drogh-spyrrydyn, quoi liorish ta ny mec eu hene dy chastey ad? bee adsyn er-y-fa shen ny briwnyn eu.
[11:20] Agh my ta mish liorish mair Yee tilgey magh drogh-spyrrydyn, fegooish dooyt ta reeriaght Yee er jeet erriuish.
[11:21] Tra ta dooinney-caggee eillit freayll arrey er e hie, ta e chooid sauchey.
[11:22] Agh tra ta fer stroshey na eh soiaghey er, as geddyn yn varriaght, t'eh goaill veih ooilley e eilley, huggey v'eh treishteil, as t'eh rheynn e chooid.
[11:23] Eshyn nagh vel lhiam, t'eh m'oi; as eshyn nagh vel chymsaghey marym, t'eh skeayley.
[11:24] Tra ta'n spyrryd neu-ghlen er gholl ass dooinney, t'eh shooyll trooid faasaghyn fadaneagh, chee aash, agh ayns fardail, eisht t'eh gra, Hem reesht gys my hie, veih haink mee.
[11:25] As tra t'eh cheet, t'eh dy gheddyn eh sceabit as soit magh dy stooamey.
[11:26] Eisht t'eh goll as goaill marish shiaght spyrrydyn elley, ny smessey na eh-hene, as t'ad goll stiagh as cummal ayns shen: as ta stayd yerrinagh yn dooinney shen ny s'doogh na'n toshiaght.
[11:27] As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh loayrt ny goan shoh, dy hrog ben dy row jeh'n cheshaght seose e coraa, as dooyrt ee rish, Bannit ta'n vrein ren oo y ymmyrkey, as ny keeaghyn t'ou er yiole.
[11:28] Agh dooyrt eshyn, Dy jarroo foddey s'bannee t'adsyn ta clashtyn goo Yee, as freayll eh.
[11:29] As tra va'n pobble er nyn jaglym chion dy cheilley, ghow eh toshiaght dy ghra, s'drogh y cheeloghe shoh: t'ad shirrey cowrey, as cha bee cowrey er ny choyrt daue, agh cowrey yn phadeyr Jonas.
[11:30] Son myr va Jonas ny chowrey da ny Nineviteyn, er yn aght cheddin neesht vees Mac y dooinney da'n cheeloghe shoh.
[11:31] Nee ben-rein y jiass girree seose ayns briwnys noi deiney yn cheeloghe shoh, as ad y gheyrey: son haink ish veih ardjyn sodjey magh y thallooin dy chlashtyn creenaght Solomon; as cur-my-ner, ta fer syrjey na Solomon ayns shoh.
[11:32] Nee deiney Nineveh girree seose ayns briwnys, as y cheeloghe shoh y gheyrey: son ghow adsyn arrys ec preacheil Yonas; as cur-my-ner, ta fer syrjey na Jonas ayns shoh.
[11:33] Cha vel dooinney erbee, tra t'eh er voaddey cainle, dy choyrt ee ayns ynnyd follit, ny fo saagh; agh ayns cainleyr, dy vod adsyn ta cheet stiagh yn soilshey y akin.
[11:34] Yn tooill ta cur soilshey da'n chorp: shen-y-fa tra ta dty hooill glen, bee dty chorp ooilley ayns slane soilshey: agh tra ta lheamys er dty hooill, bee dty chorp myrgeddin ayns slane dorraghys.
[11:35] Cur twoaie er-y-fa shen nagh bee yn soilshey ta aynyd ny ghorraghys.
[11:36] My ta ooilley dty chorp er-y-fa shen ayns slane soilshey, gyn dorraghys ayns ayrn erbee, bee yn clane sollys, myr t'ou, tra ta soilshey sollys ayd veih cainle,
[11:37] As myr v'eh loayrt, chuir Pharisee dy row eh gys jinnair marish: as hie eh stiagh, as hoie eh sheese gys bee.
[11:38] As tra honnick yn Pharisee shoh, ghow eh yindys nagh niee eh (e laueyn) roish jinnair.
[11:39] As dooyrt y Chiarn rish, Nish ta shiuish Phariseeyn glenney yn cappan as y claare er cheu-mooie: agh ta'n cheu-sthie eu lane dy hranlaase as dy olkys.
[11:40] Gheiney vee-cheaylagh, nagh nee eshyn ren y cheu-mooie, ren y cheu-sthie myrgeddin?
[11:41] Agh cur-jee lheid as t'eu da ny boghtyn: as cur-my-ner, bee dy chooilley nhee glen diu.
[11:42] Agh smerg diuish Phariseeyn: son ta shiu jagheenys mynthey, rue, as dy chooilley horch dy lossreeyn, agh s'beg ta shiu soiaghey jeh briwnys as graih Yee: ad shoh lhisagh shiu v'er n'yannoo, gyn faagail y chooid elley gyn jannoo.
[11:43] Smerg diuish Phariseeyn: son shynney lhieu ny ard-stuill ayns ny kialteenyn, as sleih dy vannaghey diu ayns ny margaghyn.
[11:44] Smerg diuish scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee-oalsey: son ta shiu myr oaiaghyn nagh vel ry-akin, as ny deiney ta shooyl harrystoo, cha vel fys oc dy vel ad ayn.
[11:45] Eisht dreggyr fer jeh fir-ynsee yn leigh, as dooyrt eh rish, Vainshter, liorish shen y ghra, t'ou dy oltooan shinyn myrgeddin.
[11:46] As dooyrt eh, Smerg diuish neesht fir-ynsee yn leigh son ta shiu laadey deiney lesh erraghyn doillee dy ve er nyn ymmyrkey, as cha vel shiu hene bentyn rish ny er raghyn lesh unnane jeh nyn meir.
[11:47] Smerg diuish: son ta shiu troggal lhiaghtyn ny phadeyryn, as ny ayraghyn eu ren y varroo ad.
[11:48] Dy firrinagh ta shiu gymmyrkey feanish dy vel shiu lowal jeh jannoo ny ayraghyn eu: son ren adsyn dy jarroo y varroo ad, as ta shiuish coamrey ny lhiaghtyn oc.
[11:49] As shoh yn oyr ta creenaght Yee er ghra, Ver-ym huc phadeyryn, as ostyllyn, as paart jeu nee ad y varroo, as tranlaase y yannoo orroo:
[11:50] Dy vod fuill ooilley ny phadeyryn v'er ny gheayrtey er-dy hoshiaght y theihll v'er ny chooilleeney er y cheeloghe shoh
[11:51] Veih fuill Abel gys fuill Zacharias ren cherraghtyn eddyr yn altar as y chiamble: dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy bee eh er ny chooilleeney er y cheeloghe shoh.
[11:52] Smerg diu fir-ynsee yn leigh: son ta shiu er ghoaill ersooyl ogher yn ysseree: cha jagh shiu stiagh shiu hene, as adsyn va goll stiagh, ren shiu y lhiettal.
[11:53] As tra v'eh er ghra ny reddyn shoh roo, ren ny scrudeyryn as ny Phariseeyn toshiaght dy eginaghey, as dy ghreinnaghey eh dy loayrt jeh ymmodee reddyn:
[11:54] Lhie ayns farkiaght er e hon, as shegin er tayrtyn red ennagh ass e veeal son oyr plaiynt n'oi.
[12:1] Nish mysh y traa shen va ymmodee erskyn-earroo dy leih er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, ayns wheesh as dy row ad stampey yn derrey yeh er yn jeh elley, ghow eh toshiaght dy ghra rish e ostyllyn, Erskyn ooilley bee-jee twoaiagh jeh soorid ny Phariseeyn, ta shen dy ghra, craueeaght oalsey.
[12:2] Son cha vel nhee erbee follit nagh jig gys soilshey; ny kiellit, nagh jig er-ash.
[12:3] Shen-y-fa cre-erbee ta shiuish er loayrt ayns y dorraghys, bee eh er ny chlashtyn ayns y toilshey: as shen ta shiu er ghra myr hannish, ayns shamyryn, bee eh er ny ockley magh er mullagh ny dhieyn.
[12:4] As ta mee gra riuish, my chaarjyn, Ny gow-jee aggle rouesyn varrys y corp, as ny lurg shen nagh vel arragh oc oddys ad y vannoo.
[12:5] Agh ver-yms raaue diu quoi roish ghoys shiu aggle: Gow-jee aggle roishyn, echey ta pooar, erreish da v'er varroo dy hilgey ayns niurin; dy jarroo ta mee dy ghra riu, Gow jee aggle roishyn.
[12:6] Nagh vel queig sperriu er nyn greck son daa farling, as cha vel unnane oc jarroodit kiongoyrt rish Jee?
[12:7] Agh ta eer renaigyn nyn ghing ooilley er nyn earroo. Ny gow-jee aggle er-y-fa shen: ta ny smoo dy ve soit jiuish, na jeh ymmodee sperriu.
[12:8] Myrgeddin ta mee gra riu, Quoi-erbee ghoys rhyms kiongoyrt rish deiney, nee yn Mac dooinney myrgeddin goaill rishyn kiongoyrt rish ainleyn Yee.
[12:9] Agh bee eshyn obbys mie fenish deiney, er ny obbal fenish ainleyn Yee.
[12:10] As quoi-erbee loayrys fockle noi Mac y dooinney, bee eh er ny leih da: agh dasyn ta loayrt goan-mollaghtagh noi yn Spyrryd Noo, cha bee eh er ny leih.
[12:11] As tra ver ad lhieu shiu gys ny quaiylyn, as gys fir-reill as pooaraghyn, ny bee-jee imneagh kys ny cre nee shiu y reggyrt, ny cre nee shiu y ghra:
[12:12] Son ynsee yn Spyrryd Noo diu, ayns yn oor cheddin cre lhisagh shiu y ghra.
[12:13] As dooyrt fer jeh'n cheshaght rish Vainshter, loayr rish my vraar eh dy rheynn yn eiraght rhym.
[12:14] As dooyrt eh rish, Ghooinney, quoi t'er my hoiaghey's seose son briw ny rheynneyder harrishdiu?
[12:15] As dooyrt eh roo, Gow-jee tastey, as cur-jee twoaie jeh saynt: son cha vel maynrys bea yn dooinney lhie ayns mooarane e chooid-seihlt.
[12:16] As loayr eh coraa-dorraghey roo, gra, Ren thalloo dooinney berchagh dy row mess y chur magh dy palchey.
[12:17] As smooinee eh rish hene, gra, Cre share dou jannoo, tra nagh vel boayl tashtee aym dy ghoaill my hroar?
[12:18] Eisht dooyrt eh, Shoh nee'm y yannoo: Lhieg-ym my hoaltyn, as trog-ym soaltyn smoo; as shen y raad nee'm ooilley my vess as my chooid y hashtey.
[12:19] As jir-ym rish my annym, O my annym, ta mooarane cooid ayd tashtit seose cour ymmodee bleeantyn: gow dty aash, ee, iu, as bee gennal.
[12:20] Agh dooyrt Jee rish, Uss ommydan yn oie noght vees dty annym er ny ghoaill void: quoi lesh eisht vees yn chooid shen t'ou uss er jaglym?
[12:21] Myr shoh ta eshyn ta tashtey seose berchys ny chour hene, as nagh vel berchagh ass lieh Yee.
[12:22] As dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Shen y fa ta mish gra riuish, Ny bee-jee imneagh son nyn mea, cre nee shiu y ee: ny son nyn girp, cre ver shiu miu.
[12:23] Ta'n vea ny smoo dy ve soit jeh na beaghey, as y corp na coamrey.
[12:24] Smooinee-jee er ny fee: son cha vel ad cuirr, ny buinn: cha vel thie stoyr ny soalt oc, as ta Jee dyn meaghey ad: As nagh vel shiuish foddey share na ny eeanlee?
[12:25] Quoi jiuish liorish smooinaghtyn dy imneagh oddys un chubit y chur gys e yrjid hene?
[12:26] Mannagh vod shiuish wheesh shen hene y yannoo, cre'n-fa ta shiu imneagh son y chooid elley?
[12:27] Gow-jee tastey jeh lileeyn ny magher agh kys t'ad gaase, cha vel ad tooilleil, chamoo t'ad sneeu: as foast ta mee gra riu, nagh row Solomon ayns ooilley e ghloyr er ny choamrey myr unnane jeu shoh.
[12:28] My ta Jee eisht myr shoh coamrey blaa ny magheragh, ta jiu 'sy vagher, as mairagh ceaut ayns yn oghe: nagh jean eh foddey smoo er nyn son euish, O gheiney faase-chredjuagh?
[12:29] As ny bee-jee seaghnit mysh cre ee-ys, ny cre iu-ys shiu, chamoo bee-jee jeh aigney imneagh nagh bee eh twoaiagh jeh, as giaree eh eh veih my-cheilley, as pointee eh e chronney marish y vooinjer vee-chredjuagh.
[12:30] Son er ooilley ny reddyn shoh ta ashoonyn y theihll dy jeean aggindagh: agh ta fys ec yn Ayr eu dy vel shiu feme ny reddyn shoh.
[12:31] Agh shir-jee hoshiaght reeriaght Yee, as bee shiu jeant magh lesh ooilley ny reddyn shoh.
[12:32] Ny gow-jee aggle my hioltane veg; son she aigney-mie nyn Ayr eh; dy chur diuish yn reeriaght.
[12:33] Creck-jee ny t'eu, as cur-jee da ny boghtyn: kiare-jee diu hene sporranyn nagh naase shenn, berchys ayns ny niaughyn nagh vel failleil, raad nagh vel y maarliagh cheet er-gerrey, ny'n lhemeen cur mow.
[12:34] Son raad ta nyn merchys, shen y raad vees y cree eu myrgeddin.
[12:35] Lhig da ny meeghyn eu ve cryssit, as ny cainleyn eu foaddit;
[12:36] As shiu hene goll-rish deiney ta farkiaght son cheet-thie nyn Jiarn veih'n vannish, ec y cheet echey tra nee eh cronkal dy vod ad fosley da chelleeragh.
[12:37] Bannit ta ny sharvaantyn shen yiow yn Chiarn er nyn arrey, tra hig eh: dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy gryss eh e gharmad mysh, as dy der eh orroo soie sheese gys bee, as dy jig eh magh dy hirveish orroo.
[12:38] As my hig eh ayns yn nah arrey, ny my hig eh ayns y trass arrey, as ad y gheddyn myr shen, bannit ta'n vooinjer cheddin.
[12:39] As shoh toig-jee, dy beagh fys er ve ec mainshter y thie cre'n oor veagh y maarliagh er jeet, veagh eh er ve er e arrey, as cha lhiggagh eh da e hie v'er ny vrishey stiagh.
[12:40] Bee-jee shiuish myrgeddin er-y-fa shen er nyn arrey: son hig Mac y dooinney ec oor nagh vel shiu smooinaghtyn er.
[12:41] Eisht dooyrt Peddyr rish, Hiarn nee orrinyn t'ou cheet 'sy choraa-dorraghey shoh, ny myrgeddin er ooilley?
[12:42] As dooyrt y Chiarn, Quoi eisht yn stiurt firrinagh as creeney shen nee e hiarn y yannoo ny er-reill er lught e hie, dy hirveish orroo nyn meaghey ayns traa cooie?
[12:43] S'maynrey yn charvaant cheddin, yiow e hiarn tra hig eh jannoo myr shen.
[12:44] Ayns firrinys ta mee gra riu, dy der eh da yn stiurtys er ooilley e chooid.
[12:45] Agh my jir y charvaant shen ayns e chree, Ta my hiarn lhiggey shaghey dy heet; as goaill er dy woalley ny fir-vooinjerey, as ny inneenyn, as dy ee, as dy iu, as dy ve er meshtey.
[12:46] Hig chiarn y charvaant shen ec laa nagh bee eh jeeaghyn er e hon, as ayns oor nagh bee eh twoaiagh jeh, as giaree ehe eh veih my-cheilley, as pointee eh e chronney marish y vooinjer vee-chredjuagh.
[12:47] As y charvaant shen va toiggal aigney e hiarn, as nagh dooar eh-hene aarloo, as nagh ren cordail rish e aigney, s'mooar vees y kerraghey echey.
[12:48] Agh eshyn nagh row toiggal, as ren foiljyn va toilliu kerraghey, cha bee yn kerraghey echey cha trome. Son da quoi erbee ta mooarane er ny choyrt, ersyn vees mooarane er ny hirrey: as da quoi-erbee ta lane currit er e churrym, veihsyn nee sleih jeeaghyn son ny smoo
[12:49] Haink mish dy chur aile er y thalloo, as cre ta my yeearree, agh dy bee eh hannah er ny oaddey?
[12:50] Agh ta bashtey ayms dy ve er my vashtey lesh, as kys ta mee eginit, derrey vees eh er ny chooilleeney?
[12:51] Vel shiu smooinaghtyn dy daink mish dy chur shee er y thalloo? Cha nee, ta mee gra riu, agh anvea.
[12:52] Son veih shoh magh bee queig ayns un thie noi-ry-hoi, three noi jees, as jees noi three.
[12:53] Bee yn ayr noi yn mac, as y mac noi yn ayr; yn voir noi yn inneen, as yn inneen noi yn voir yn voir-'sy-leigh noi e ben chleuin, as y ven-chleuin noi e moir-'sy-leigh.
[12:54] As dooyrt eh myrgeddin rish y pobble, Tra heeys shiu bodjal troggal ass y sheear; chelleeragh ta shiu gra, Ta frass cheet; as shen myr te.
[12:55] As tra ta'n gheay-jiass sheidey, ta shiu gra, Bee chiass ayn, as te cheet gy-kione.
[12:56] Chrauee-oalsey, ta shiu son baght y ghoaill jeh neeal yn aer as y thalloo: agh kys te nagh vel shiu goaill baght jeh'n earish shoh?
[12:57] As cre'n-fa myrgeddin nagh vel shiu eer j'iu hene briwnys shen ny ta cairagh?
[12:58] Tra t'ou goll fenish yn er-reill marishyn ta ec streeu rhyt, jean ny oddys oo er y raad dy gheddyn rea rish; er-aggle dy dayrn eh lesh oo gys y vriw, as dy livrey yn briw oo da'n tidoor, as dy dilg eh shen oo ayns pryssoon.
[12:59] Ta mee ginsh dhyt, nagh jig oo magh ass shen derrey t'ou er n'eeck yn farling s'jerree.
[13:1] Va kionfenish ec y traa shen paart dinsh y da mychione ny Galileanee, yn uill oc va Pilate er gheayrtey maStey (filill) ny ourallyn oc.
[13:2] As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Vel shiuish sheiltyn dy row ny Galileanee shoh nyn beccee erskyn ooilley ny Galileanee, er-y-fa dy duillee ad lheid y baase?
[13:3] Ta mee ginsh diu, Nagh row: agh mannagh gow shiuish arrys, nee shiu ooilley myrgeddin cherraghtyn.
[13:4] Ny yn hoght-jeig shen, orroo ren y toor nyns Siloam tuittym, as ad y varroo, vel shiu smooinaghtyn dy row ad nyn beccee erskyn ooilley cummaltee Yerusalem?
[13:5] Ta mee ginsh diu, Nagh row: agh mannagh gow shiuish arrys, nee shiu ooilley myrgeddin cherraghtyn.
[13:6] Loayr eh myrgeddin yn coraa-dorraghey shoh: va dooinoey dy row va billey-figgagh echey soit ayns e gharey-feeyney, as haink eh dy yeeaghyn row mess er, as cha dooar eh veg.
[13:7] Eisht dooyrt eh rish y ghareyder, Cur-my-ner, ny three bleeaney shoh ta mee er jeet dy yeeaghyn voin mess er y villey-figgagh shoh, as cha vel mee geddyn veg: giare sheese eh, cha vel eh agh goaill seose room hallooin.
[13:8] As dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh rish, Hiarn, lhig da shassoo blein elley, derrey neem's reurey mygeayrt y mysh as lhiassaghey eh.
[13:9] As my nee eh mess y ymmyrkey, s'mie shen: as mannagh jean, foddee oo ny lurg shen y ghiarey sheese eh.
[13:10] As v'eh gynsaghey ayns unnane jeh ny synagogueyn er y doonaght.
[13:11] As cur-my-ner va ben ayns shen seaghnit lesh spyrryd doghanagh rish hoght bleeaney jeig, as v'ee crybbit dy cheilley, as cha dod ee er aght erbee ec hene y yeeraghey.
[13:12] As tra honnick Yeesey ee, deie eh urree huggey, as dooyrt eh r'ee, Ven, t'ou er dty eaysley veih dty ghoghan.
[13:13] As hug eh e laueyn urree; as er-y chooyl v'ee er ny yannoo jeeragh, as ren ee Jee y ghloyraghey.
[13:14] As dreggyr fer-reill yn synagogue lesh jymmoose, er-yn-oyr dy row Yeesey er lheihys er laa yn doonaght, as dooyrt eh rish y pobble, Ta shey laa ayn ry-hoi gobbraghey: er ny laghyn shen er-y-fa shen tar-jee dy ve er nyn lheihys, as cha nee er laa yn doonaght.
[13:15] Eisht dreggyr y Chiarn eh, gra, Er crauee-oalsey, nagh vel dagh fer jiuish er y doonaght feaysley e ghow ny e assyl veih'n staik, as dy chur lesh magh dy ushtaghey eh?
[13:16] As nagh lhisagh y ven shoh ta ny hinneen da Abraham, ee ta satan er chiangley, cur-my-ner ny hoght bleeaney jeig shoh, ve er ny eaysley veih yn vondiaght shoh er laa yn doonaght?
[13:17] As tra v'eh er loayrt ny goan shoh, ghow ooilley e noidyn nearey: agh va ooilley yn pobble ayns ard-voggey son ooilley ny reddyn gloyroil va jeant liorishyn.
[13:18] Eisht dooyrt eh, Cre ta reeriaght Yee goll-rish? as cre gys nee'm y hoylaghey eh?
[13:19] Te goll-rish grine dy rass mustard, ren dooinney y ghoaill, as y hilgey ayns e gharey, as daase eh, as haink eh dy ve ny villey vooar: as ren eeanlee yn aer fastee y ghoaill ayns ny banglaneyn echey.
[13:20] As reesht dooyrt eh, Cre gys nee'm reeriaght Yee y hoylaghey?
[13:21] Te goll-rish soorid, ren ben y ghoaill as follaghey ayns three towseyn dy veinn, derrey va'n clane soorit.
[13:22] As hie eh magh trooid ny ard-valjyn as ny baljyn-cheerey, gynsaghey as goll er e hoshiaght gys Jerusalem.
[13:23] Eisht dooyrt fer rish, Hiarn, nee beggan ta er nyn sauail? As dooyrt eh roo.
[13:24] Streeu-jee shiuush dy gholl stiagh er y ghiat coon: son nee ymmodee, ta mee gra riu, shirrey goll stiagh, agh cha jig eh lhieu.
[13:25] Keayrt dy vel mainshter y thie er n'irree, as y dorrys dooint, as dy jean shiuish toshiaght dy hassoo er cheu-mooie, as dy chronkal ec y dorrys, gra, Hiarn, Hiarn, foshil dooin; as freggyree eshyn as jir eh riu, Cha nione dou shiu, cre veih ta shiu:
[13:26] Eisht gowee shiuish toshiaght dy ghra, Ta shin er n'ee as er n'iu ayns dty enish, as t'ou er n'ynsaghey ayns ny straidyn ain.
[13:27] Agh jir eshyn, Ta mee ginsh diu, nagh nione dou shiu, cre veih ta shiu: ersooyl-jee voym ooilley shiuish ghrogh-yantee.
[13:28] Shen-y-raad vees keayney as snaggeraght feeacklyn, tra hee shiu Abraham, aa Isaac as Jacob as ooilley ny phadeyryn ayns reeriaght Yee, as shiu hene er nyn yioolaey magh.
[13:29] As hig ad veih'n niar, as veih'n neear, as veih'n twoaie as veih'n jiass, as soie-ee ad sheese ayns reeriaght-Yee.
[13:30] As cur-my-ner, ta er-jerrey vees hoshiaght, as ta hoshiaght vees er-jerrey.
[13:31] Yn laa cheddin, haink shiartanse jeh ny Phariseeyn, as dooyrt ad rish, Fow ersooyl, as immee royd veih shoh; son ta Herod sleeuit er dty rioys y ghoaill.
[13:32] As dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee shiuish as insh-jee da'n shynnagh shen, Cur-my-ner, ta mee castey drogh-spyrrydyn, as lheihys doghanyn jiu as mairagh, as y trass laa bee'm er my ghloyraghey.
[13:33] Ny yeih, Shegin dou shooyl jiu as mairagh, as y laa er-giyn: son s'coan oddys phadeyr cherraghtyn agh ayns Jerusalem.
[13:34] O Yerusalem, Yerusalem, ta cur dy baase ny phadeyryn, as dyn glaghey adsyn t'er nyn goyrt er chaghteraght hood: cre cha mennick as va mish aggindagh v'er hagIym dty chloan cooidjagh, myr ta kiark clussaghey e aalagh fo my skianyn, agh cha bailliu shen!
[13:35] Cur-my-ner, ta'n thie eu faagit diu follym-faase: as dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, nagh vaik shiu mish maghey shoh, derrey hig yn traa dy jir shiu, Bannit ta eshyn ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn.
[14:1] As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'eh er gholl stiagh ayns thie fer jeh ny ard Phariseeyn dy ee arran er y doonaght, dy row sooill oc er.
[14:2] As cur-my-ner, va dooinney kionfenish, va'n dropsee er.
[14:3] As dreggyr Yeesey, as loayr eh rish fir-ynsee yn leigh as rish ny Phariseeyn, gra, Vel eh lowal dy lheihys er laayn doonaght?
[14:4] As v'ad nyn-dhost. As ghow eh as laanee eh eh, as lhig eh yn raad da:
[14:5] As dreggyr eh ad, gra, Quoi j'iu vees dow ny assyl echey er huittym ayns jeeg, nagh jean jeeragh y hayrn ass eh er y doonaght?
[14:6] As cha row ansoor erbee oc dy choyrt gys ny goan shoh.
[14:7] As loayr eh coraa-dorraghey rish ny goaldee, tra hug eh tastey kys v'ad reih ny stuill byrjey; gra roo,
[14:8] Tra t'ou cuirt liorish dooinney erbee gys bannish, ny soie sheese er y stoyl syrjey; er-aggle dy bee dooinney s'ooasle na uss er ny chuirrey liorish;
[14:9] As dy jig eshyn ren shiu nyn neesht y chuirrey, as dy jir eh rhyt, Cur raad da'n dooinney shoh; as dy jean oo toshiaght lesh nearey dy ghoaill y stoyl s'inshley.
[14:10] Agh tra vees oo cuirt, immee, as soie sheese er y stoyl s'inshley; tra hig eshyn ren dty chuirrey, dy vod eh gra rhyt, Charrey, gow seose ny syrjey: eisht bee ooashley ayd ayns yn enish ocsyn ta nyn soie ec bee mayrt:
[14:11] Son quoi-erbee ta dy hoiaghey eh-hene seose, bee eh er ny injillaghey; as eshyn ta dy injillaghey eh-hene, bee eh er ny hoiaghey seose.
[14:12] Eisht dooyrt eh rishyn ren y chuirrey eh, Tra t'ou jannoo jinnair ny shibber, ny cuir dty chaarjyn, ny dty vraaraghyn, ny dty gheiney-mooinjerey, ny dty naboonyn berchagh; er-aggle dy jean adsyn oo y chuirrey reesht, as dy bee lhiassaghey er ny yannoo dhyt.
[14:13] Agh tra t'ou jannoo cuirraghyn, eie er ny boghtyn, ny baccee, ny croobee, as ny doail:
[14:14] As bee oo bannit; son cha vod adsyn cooilleeney 'chur dhyt: son bee oo cooilleenit ec irree-reesht y chloan chairagh.
[14:15] As tra cheayll fer jeusyn va nyn soie ec bee marish ny goan shoh, dooyrt eh rish, Bannit ta eshyn ee-ys arran ayns reeriaght Yee.
[14:16] Eisht dooyrt eh rish, Ren dooinney dy row shibber vooar, as chuir eh ymmodee:
[14:17] As hug eh magh e harvaant ec traa shibberagh dy ghra rish ny goaldee, Tar-jee, son ta dy chooilley nhee nish aarloo.
[14:18] As ren ad ooilley toshiaght lesh un aigney dy yannoo leshtalyn. Dooyrt y chied er, Ta mee er chionnaghey peesh dy halloo, as shegin dou goll dy yeeaghyn er: guee-ym ort, jean my leshtal.
[14:19] As dooyrt fer elley, Ta mee er chionnaghey queig chubbil dy ghew, as ta mee goll dy phowal ad: ta mee guee ort jean my leshtal.
[14:20] As dooyrt fer elley, Ta mee er phoosey ben, as er-y-fa shen cha voddym cheet.
[14:21] Myr shen haink y charvaant cheddin, as hoilshee eh da e hiarn ny reddyn shoh. Eisht va mainshter y thie jymmoosagh, as dooyrt eh rish e harvaant, Gow magh dy tappee gys straidyn as raaidyn yn ard-valley, as cur lhiat stiagh ayns shoh ny boghtyn, as ny baccee, as ny croobee, as ny doail:
[14:22] As dooyrt y charvaant, Hiarn, te jeant myr t'ou er harey, as foast ta room.
[14:23] As dooyrt y chiarn rish y charvaant, Gow magh gys ny raaidyn mooarey as ny cleigh, as guee orroo dy heet stiagh, dy vod my hie ve er ny lhieeney.
[14:24] Son ta mee gra riu, nagh jean fer jeh ny deiney va cuirt, blashtyn jeh my hibber,
[14:25] As hie earrooyn mooarey dy leih marish: as hyndaa eh, as dooyrt eh roo,
[14:26] My hig dooinney erbee hym's, as nagh vel graih sloo echey er e ayr as e voir, as e ven, as e chloan, as e vraaraghyn, as e hayraghyn, dy jarroo, as er e vioys hene (na orrym's) cha vod eh dy firrinagh gynsaghey voym's.
[14:27] As quoi-erbee nagh vel gymmyrkey e chrosh, as cheet geiyrt orrym's, cha vod eh ve ny eiyrtyssagh dooys.
[14:28] Quoi jiuish ta kiarail toor y hroggal, nagh vel soie sheese hoshiaght, as coontey yn cost, vel wheesh echey as ver mullagh er?
[14:29] Er-aggle erreish da yn undin y boiaghey, as nagh vel yn fort echey dy chur kione er, dy jean ooilley nee fakin eh toshiaght dy chraidey mysh,
[14:30] Gra, Ren y dooinney shoh toshiaght dy vuildal, as cha row fort echey kione y cur er e obbyr.
[14:31] Ny cre'n ree ragh dy yannoo caggey noi ree elley, nagh soiagh sheese hoshiaght dy ghoaill coyrle, vel eh son goll magh lesh jeih thousaneyn ny whail echeysyn ta cheet n'oi lesh feed thousane?
[14:32] Er-nonney, choud as ta'n ree elley foddey veih, t'eh cur chaghteraght huggey, as chebbal conaantyn shee.
[14:33] Myr shen myrgeddin quoi-erbee jiuish, nagh vel treigeil ooilley ny t'echey, cha vod eh ve ny eiyrtyssagh dooys.
[14:34] Ta sollan mie: agh my ta'n sollan er choayl e vlass, kys hig e vree ayn reesht?
[14:35] Cha vel ymmyd ayn son y thalloo, ny foast son y torran; agh ta deiney dy cheau magh eh. Eshyn ta cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn, lhig da clashtyn.
[15:1] Eisht haink er-gerrey da ooilley ny publicanee as ny peccee dy eaishtagh; rish.
[15:2] As ren ny Phariseeyn as ny scrudeyryn tallagh, gra, Ta'n dooinney shoh goaill rish peccee, as gee maroo.
[15:3] as loayr eh yn coraa-dorraghey shoh roo, gra,
[15:4] Quoi yn dooinney ny mast' euish ta keead keyrrey echey, as coayl unnane jeu nagh vel eh faagail yn chiare-feed as yn nuy jeig ayns yn aasagh, as goll dy hirrey yn cheyrrey chailjey, derrey t'eh dy gheddyn ee?
[15:5] As tra t'eh er gheddyn ee, t'eh dy choyrt ee er e gheayltyn, goaill boggey.
[15:6] As tra t'eh cheet thie, t'eh geamagh er e chaarjyn as e naboonyn cooidjagh, as gra roo, Gow-Jee boggey marym, son ta mee er gheddyn my cheyrrey va caillit.
[15:7] Ta mee gra riu, dy bee boggey myrgeddin ayns niau, jeh un pheccagh ta goaill arrys, ny smoo na jeh kiare-feed as nuy persoonyn jeig cairagh, nagh vel feme arrys.
[15:8] Ny cre'n ven ta jeih peeshyn dy argid eck, as ee dy choayl un pheesh, nagh vel ee foaddey cainle, as sceabey yn thie, as shirrey dy kiaralagh, derrey t'ee dy gheddyn eh?
[15:9] As tra t'ee er gheddyn eh, t'ee geamagh er e caarjyn as e naboonyn cooidjagh, gra, Gow-jee boggey marym, son ta mee er gheddyn yn pheesh ren mee y choayl.
[15:10] Myrgeddin ta mee gra riu, dy vel boggey ayns fenish ainleyn Yee jeh un pheccagh ta goaill arrys.
[15:11] As dooyrt eh, Va daa vac ec dooinney dy row:
[15:12] A s dooyrt y fer saa rish e ayr, Ayr, cur dooys yn ayrn dy chooid ta my chour. As rheynn eh e eh chooid orroo.
[15:13] As laghyn ny lurg shen, hymsee yn mac saa ooilley cooidjagh as ghow eh jurnah gys cheer foddey, as ayns shen hug eh jummal er e chooid liorish baghey rouanagh.
[15:14] As tra va ooilley baarit echey, dirree genney vooar ayns y cheer shen; as ren eh toshiaght dy ve ayns feme.
[15:15] As hie eh as daill eh eh-hene rish cummaltagh jeh'n cheer shen; as hug eshyn eh magh gys ny magheryn echey dy ve son bochilley muickey.
[15:16] As by-vian lesh e volg y lhieeney lesh ny bleaystyn va ny muckyn dy ee: as cha row dooinney erbee hug cooney da.
[15:17] As tra v'eh er jeet huggey hene, dooyrt eh, Nagh nhimmey sharvaant failt t'ec my ayr ta nyn saie arran oc, as fooilliagh, as ta mish goll mow laccal beaghey!
[15:18] Trog-ym orrym, as hem roym gys my ayr, as jir-ym rish, Ayr, ta mee er n'yannoo peccah noi niau, as kiongoyrt rhyt's,
[15:19] rish fer jeh dty harvaantyn sailt.
[15:20] As hrog eh er, as haink eh gys e ayr. Agh tra v'eh foast foddey veih, honnick e ayr eh, as va chymmey echey er, as roie eh, as ghow eh eh ayns e roihaghyn as phaag eh eh.
[15:21] As dooyrt y mac rish, Ayr, ta mee er n'yannoo peccah noi niau, as ayns dty hilley's, as cha vel mee ny-sodjey feeu dy ve enmyssit dty vac.
[15:22] Agh dooyrt yn ayr rish e harvaantyn, Cur-jee lhieu magh yn coamrey share, as cur-jee er eh, as cur-jee fainey er e laue, as braagyn er e chassyn.
[15:23] As cur-jee lhieu ayns shoh yn lheiy beiyht, as marr-jee eh; as lhig dooin gee as ve gennal.
[15:24] Son v'eh shoh my vac marroo, as t'eh bio reesht; v'eh caillit, as t'eh er ny gheddyn reesht. As ren ad toshiaght dy yannoo gien mie.
[15:25] Nish va'n mac shinney mooie 'sy vagher: as tra haink eh er-gerrey da'n thie, cheayll eh kiaulleeaght as daunsin.
[15:26] As deie eh er fer jeh'n vooinjer, as denee eh cre son va shoh.
[15:27] As dooyrt eh rish, Ta dty vraar er jeet thie; as ta dty ayr er varroo yn lheiy beiyht, er-yn-oyr dy vel eh er jeet thie huggey slane follan.
[15:28] As v'eh feer chorree, as cha baillish goll stiagh: shen-y-fa haink e ayr magh, as vreag eh eh.
[15:29] As dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh rish e ayr, Cur-my-ner, ta mish rish whilleen blein shen ayns dty hirveish, chamoo ren mee rieau noi dty aigney, as foast cha dug oo dou rieau wheesh mannan, dy yannoo gien marish my gheiney-mooinjerey:
[15:30] Agh cha leah as v'eh shoh dty vac er jeet, ta er vaarail dty chooid er streebeeyn t'ou er varroo er e hon yn lheiy beiyht.
[15:31] As dooyrt eh rish, Vac, t'ou er ny ve kinjagh marym, as lhiat's ooilley ny t'aym.
[15:32] Ve cooie dooin ve gennal, as boggey y ghoaill: son v'eh shoh dty vraar marroo as t'eh bio reesht: v'eh caillit, as t'eh er ny gheddyn.
[16:1] AS dooyrt eh myrgeddin rish e ostyllyn, Va dooinney berchagh dy row as stiurt echey, va er ny chassid huggey son jummal e chooid.
[16:2] As deie eh er, as dooyrt eh rish, Kys dy vel mee clashtyn shoh jeed? cur coontey jeh dty stiurtys: son cha vod oo ve ny sodjey dty stiurt,
[16:3] Eisht dooyrt y stiurt rish hene, Cre nee'm? son ta my hiarn goaill y stiurtys voym: cha voddym reurey, as dy huill ny dhieyn ta nearey orrym.
[16:4] Shoh ta mee kiarail dy yannoo tra chaill-ym y stiurtys, dy vod paart jeu goaill mee stiagh ayns ny thieyn oc.
[16:5] Er shoh deie eh orroosyn ooilley v'ayns lhiastynys da e hiarn, as dooyrt eh rish y chied er, Cre-woad t'ou uss dy lhiastyn dy my hiarn?
[16:6] As dooyrt eh, Keead towse dy ooil As dooyrt eh rish, Gow dty lioar, as soie sheese-dy tappee, as scrieu jeih as da-eed.
[16:7] As doogrt eh rish fer elley, As cre-woad t'ou uss dy lhiastyn? As dooyrt eh, Keead owse dy churnaght. As dooyrt eh rish,Gow dty lioar as scrieu kiare-feed.
[16:8] As voyll y chiarn y stiurt neu-chairagh, er-y-fa dy row eh er n'yannoo dy creeney: son ta cloan y theihll shoh ayns nyn sheeloghe ny s'creeney na cloan y toilshey.
[16:9] As ta mee gra riu, Jean-jee diu hene caarjyn liorish y mammon molteyragh; tra nee shiu failleil dy vod ad shiu y ghoaill stiagh gys ny ynnydyn vaghee dy bragh farraghtyn.
[16:10] Eshyn ta ynrick ayns yn nhee s'fardalee, t'eh ynrick myrgeddin ayns mooarane: as eshyn ta neu-charragh ayns y nhee s'fadalee, t'eh neu-chairagh myrgeddin ayns mooarane.
[16:11] Mannagh vel shiu er-y-fa shen er ve ynrick ayns y mammon molteyragh, quoi ver yn verchys firrinagh fo nyn gurrym?
[16:12] As mannagh vel shiu er ve firrinagh ayns ny ta lesh dooinney elley, quoi ver diu ny vees lhieu hene?
[16:13] Cha vod sharvaant erbee daa vainshter y hirveish: son eddyr ver eh feoh da'n derrey yeh as graih da'n jeh elley; er nonney cummee eh gys y derrey yeh, as soie-ee eh beg jeh'n jeh elley. Cha vod shiu Jee as mammon y hirveish.
[16:14] As cheayll ny Phariseeyn myrgeddin va sayntoilagh, ooilley ny reddyn shoh: as ren ad gannidys er.
[16:15] As dooyrt eh roo, Shiuish yn vooinjer ta dy heyrey shiu hene kiongoyrt rish deiney: agh ta fys ec Jee er ny creeaghyn eu: son ta shen ta dy mooar soit jeh mastey deiney, feohdoil ayns shilley Yee.
[16:16] Va'n leigh as ny phadeyryn derrey Ean: er-dyn traa shen, ta reeriaght Yee er ny phreacheil, as ta dy chooilley ghooinney chionney stiagh huggey.
[16:17] Agh te ny sassey da'n aer as da'n thalloo dy herraghtyn, na da un floag jeh'n leigh dy ailleil.
[16:18] Quoi-erbee scarrys rish e ven, as phoosys ben elley, t'eh brishey poosey: as quoi-erbee phoosys ish ta scarrit veih e sheshey, t'eh brishey poosey.
[16:19] Va dooinney berchagh dy row va coamrit ayns gorrym-jiarg, as sheeidey, as farrail dy soaillagh dy chooilley laa.
[16:20] As va boght dy row va enmyssit Lazarus, va ny lhie ec y ghiat echey lane dy hingyn,
[16:21] As geearree dy ve jeant magh lesh y vrooillagh va tuittym jeh boayrd y dooinney berchagh: agh haink ny eer moddee as sliee ad ny chingyn echey.
[16:22] As haink eh gy-kione, dy dooar y dooinney boght baase, as dy dug dy ainleyn lhieu eh gys oghrish Abraham: hooar y dooinney berchagh myrgeddin baase, as v'eh er ny oanluckey.
[16:23] As ayns niurin, raad v'eh er ny horchaghey, hrog eh seose e hooillyn, as honnick eh Abraham foddey veih, as Lazarus ayns e oghrish.
[16:24] As deie eh as dooyrt eh, Ayr Abraham, jean myghin orrym, as cur Lazarus, dy vod eh baare e vair y hummey ayns ushtey, as my hengey y eayraghey; son ta mee er my horchaghey ayns y lossey shoh.
[16:25] Agh dooyrt Abrabam, Vac, cooinee uss ayns earish dty vea dy row ayd's dy chooilley nhee mie, as myrgeddin ec Lazarus cha row monney agh seaghyn: agh nish t'eshyn er ny gherjaghey, as t'ou uss er dty horchaghey,
[16:26] As marish shoh ooilley, ta eddyr shinyn as shiuish diunid vooar soit: myr shen adsyn ta aignagh dy gholl yeih shoh hiuish, cha vod ad; chamoo oddys adsyn cheet hooinyn bailliu cheet veih shen.
[16:27] Eisht dooyrt eh, Ta mee guee ort er-y-fa shen, ayr, dy choyrt eh gys thie my ayrey:
[16:28] Son ta queig braaraghyn aym; dy vod eh feanish y ymmyrkey daue, nagh jig adsyn myrgeddin gys y boayl shoh dy horchagh.
[16:29] Dooyrt Abraham rish, Ta Moses as ny phadeyryn oc; lhig daue clashtyn adsyn.
[16:30] As dooyrt eh, Cha nee, O ayr Abraham: agh dy ragh chaghter huc veih ny merriu, ghoghe ad arrys.
[16:31] As dooyrt eh rish, Mannagh der ad geill da Moses as ny phadeyryn, cha greidjagh ad, ga dy n'irragh fer veih ny merriu.
[17:1] Eisht dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Cha vod eh ve, agh dy bee oyryn peccah ayn: agh smerg dasyn liorish hig ad.
[17:2] Veagh eh ny bare dasyn clagh-wyllin ve croghit mysh e wannal, as eh dy ve baiht ayns y cheayn, na eh dy hayrn gys peccah unnane jeh'n vooinjer veggey shoh.
[17:3] Cur-jee twoaie diu hene: My nee dty vraar aggair dhyt, cur oghsan da; us my ghoys eh arrys, leih da.
[17:4] As my nee eh peccah dt'oi shiaght keayrtyn 'sy laa, as shiaght keayrtyn 'sy laa chyndaa reesht hood as gra, Ta mee goaill arrys; te ort leih da.
[17:5] As dooyrt ny ostyllyn rish y Chiarn, Bishee yn credjue ainyn.
[17:6] As dooyrt y Chiarn, Dy beagh credjue eu myr grine dy rass mustard, oddagh shiu gra rish y billey-sycamine shoh, Bee er dty hayrn ass ny fraueyn, as bee er dty hoiaghey ayns y cheayn; as yinnagh eh biallys diu.
[17:7] Agh quoi eu ta sharvaant echey traaue, ny bochillagh ollagh, jirrys rish chelleeragh, tra vees eh er jeet veih'n vagher, Immee as soie gys y voayrd?
[17:8] As nagh jir hoshiaght rish, Fow aarloo my hibber, as kiartee oo hene dy hirveish orrym's, derrey vee'm erreish gee as giu, us ny lurg shen nee uss gee as giu?
[17:9] Vel booise er da'n charvaant shen, Son jannoo myr v'eh oardit? Er-lhiam nagh vel.
[17:10] Myr shen neesht shiuish tra vees shiu er n'yannoo ooilley ny t'er ny harey diu, abbyr jee. She sharvaantyn neu-frioosagh shin: ta shin er n'yannoo ynrycan ny va orrin dy yannoo.
[17:11] As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh er e vurnah gys Jerusalem, dy jimmee eh trooid mean Samaria as Galilee.
[17:12] As myr v'eh goll stiagh ayns balley dy row, haink ny whail jeih deiney va nyn louranee, as hass ad foddey veih:
[17:13] As hrog ad seose nyn goraa, as dooyrt ad, Yeesey, Vainshter, jean myghin orrin.
[17:14] As tra v'eh er jeeaghyn orroo, dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee as jeeagh-jee shiu hene da ny saggyrtyn. As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'ad goll, dy row ad er nyn ghlenney.
[17:15] As hyndaa fer jeu back, tra honnick eh dy row eh er ny laanaghey, as lesh ard choraa hug eh moylley da Jee,
[17:16] As huitt eh sheese er e eddin ec ny cassyn echey, cur booise da: as v'eh ny Samaritan.
[17:17] As dreggyr Yeesey, gra, Nagh row jeih er ny ghlenney? agh cre vel yn nuy?
[17:18] Cha vel er nyn gheddyn t'er jyndaa dy chur gloyr da Jee, agh yn ynrycan joarree shoh.
[17:19] As dooyrt eh rish, Irree, immee royd; ta dty chredjue er dty laanaghey.
[17:20] As tra denee ny Phariseeyn jeh, cre'n traa harragh reeriaght Yee? dreggyt eh ad, gra, Cha jig reeriaght Yee lesh stayd chronnal.
[17:21] Chamoo jir ad, Jeeagh shoh, ny jeeagh shid: son cur-my-ner, ta reeriaght Yee cheu-sthie jeu.
[17:22] As dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Hig y traa dy bee shiu aignagh dy akin unnane jeh laghyn Mac y dooinney, as cha vaik shiu eh.
[17:23] As jir ad riu, jeeagh-jee ayns shoh, as jeeagh-jee ayns shid: ny roie-jee geiyrt orroo, as ny lhian-jee roo.
[17:24] Son myr ta'n tendreil soilshean veih ard dy ard fo yn aer: myr shen myrgeddin vees Mac y dooinney ayns y laa echeysyn.
[17:25] Agh hoshiaght shegin da ymmodee seaghyn y hurranse, as ve beg soit jeh liorish y sheeloghe shoh.
[17:26] As myr ve rish lhing Noe, shen myr vees eh neesht ayns laghyn Mac y dooinney.
[17:27] V'ad gee, v'ad giu, v'ad poosey, v'ad er nyn goyrt ayns poosey, derrey'n laa hie Noe stiagh ayns yn arg: as haink y thooilley as vaih eh ad ooilley.
[17:28] As er yn aght cheddin myr ve ayns laghyn Lot, v'ad gee, v'ad giu v'ad kionnaghey, v'ad creck, v'ad soiaghey biljyn, v'ad troggal thieyn:
[17:29] Agh er yn eer laa hie Lot magh ass Sodom, gheayrt neose orroo aile as brimstone veih niau, as ren eh ad ooilley y stroie:
[17:30] Eer er yn aght cheddin vees eh er y laa vees yn Mac dooinney er ny hoilshaghey.
[17:31] Ayns y laa shen, eshyn vees er mullagh y thie, as e chooid sthie, ny lhig da cheet neose dy chur lesh eh: as eshyn ta ayns y vagher, ny lhig dasyn myrgeddin chyndaa back
[17:32] Cooinee-jee er ben Lot.
[17:33] Quoi-erbee ta shirrey e vioys y hauail caillee eh eh: as quoi-erbee nee e vioys y choayl, saue-ee eh eh.
[17:34] Ta mee ginsh diu, ayns yn oie shen dy bee daa ghooinney ayns un lhiabbee: as bee yn derrey yeh goit, as y jeh elley faagit.
[17:35] Bee daa ven blieh cooidjagh, bee yn derrey yeh goit, as y jeh elley faagit.
[17:36] Bee daa ghooinney ayns y vagher; bee yn derrey yeh goit, as y jeh elley faagit.
[17:37] As dreggyr ad, as dooyrt ad rish, C'raad, Hiarn? As dooyrt eshyn roo, Raad erbee dy vel yn convayrt, shen-y-raad vees ny urlee er nyn jaglym cooidjagh.
[18:1] Aa loayr eh coraa-dorraghey roo, dy lhisagh deiney kinjagh padjer y ghoaill, as gyn ad y ve lhiastey;
[18:2] Gra, Va ayns ard-valley dy row briw nagh row ayns aggle roish Jee, ny soiaghey jeh deiney.
[18:3] As va ben-treoghe ayns yn ard-valley cheddin, haink huggey, gra, Jean cairys dou er my noid.
[18:4] As son tammylt cha dug eh geill jee: agh ny lurg shen dooyrt eh rish hene, Ga nagh vel mee goaill aggle roish Jee, ny jannoo soiaghey jeh dooinney:
[18:5] Ny-yeih er-y-fa dy vel y ven-treoghe shoh dy my voirey, ver-ym cairys jee, er-aggle liorish cheet cha kinjagh dy jean ee skee jee'm.
[18:6] As dooyrt y Chiarn, Clasht-jee cre ta'n briw neu-chairagh dy ghra.
[18:7] As nagh jean Jee cooilleeney ass lieh e chloan reiht hene, ta geamagh huggey oie as laa, ga dy vel eh foddey lhiggey shaghey?
[18:8] Ta mee ginsh diu dy jean eh dy tappee goaill cooilleeney er nyn son. Ny-yeih tra hig Mac y dooinney, vow eh credjue er y thalloo?
[18:9] As loayr eh yn coraa-dorraghey shoh rish shiartanse va treishteil ayndoo hene dy row ad cairagh, agh soiaghey beg jeh feallagh elley:
[18:10] Hie daa ghooinney seose gys y chiamble dy ghoaill padjer; va'n derrey yeh ny Pharisee, as y jeh elley ny Phublican.
[18:11] Hass y Pharisee as ghow eh padjer myr shoh rish hene, Yee, ta mee cur booise dhyt, nagh vel mish myr deiney elley, tranlaasee, neu-chairagh, brishey-poosey, ny foast myr y publican shoh.
[18:12] Ta mee trostey daa cheayrt 'sy chiaghtin, ta mee cur jaghee jeh ooilley ny t'ayns my chummal.
[18:13] As hass y publican foddey veih, as cha b'lhoys da wheesh as e hooillyn y hroggal seose gys niau, agh woaill eh er e chleeau, gra, Dy row Jee myghinagh dooys ta my ghooinney peccoil.
[18:14] Ta mee ginsh diu, dy jagh y dooinney shoh sheese gys e hie er ny heyrey roish y jeh elley: son bee dy chooilley er ta dy hoiaghey eh-hene seose er ny injillaghey as bee eshyn ta dy injillaghey eh-hene, er ny hoiaghey seose.
[18:15] As hug ad lhieu huggey myrgeddin cloan aegey, dy ventyn roo: agh tra honnick e ostyllyn shoh, hooar ad foill.
[18:16] Agh deie Yeesey orroo huggey, as dooyrt eh, Lhig-jee da ny paitchyn cheet hym's, as ny jean-jee ad y lhiettal: son jeh nyn lheid ta reeriaght Yee.
[18:17] Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Quoi-erbee nagh jean goaill-rish reeriaght Yee myr lhiannoo beg, cha jed eh er aght erbee stiagh ayn.
[18:18] As denee fer-reill dy row jeh, gra, Vainshter vie, cre t'orrym dy yannoo dy vod eiraght y ve aym ayns y vea veayn?
[18:19] As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Cre'n-fa t'ou genmys mish mie? cha vel ayn ny ta mie, agh unnane, ynrycan Jee.
[18:20] Shione dhyt ny annaghyn, Ny jean poosey y vrishey, Ny jean dunverys, Ny jean geid, Ny jean feanish foalsey y ymmyrkey, Cur arrym da dty ayr as da dty voir.
[18:21] As dooyrt eh, Ooilley shoh ta mee er vreayll veih my aegid.
[18:22] Nish tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, dooyrt eh rish, Ta foast ort un red y yannoo: creck as rheynn ooilley ny t'ayd er ny boghtyn, as bee berchys ayd ayns niau: as tar, as eiyr orrym's.
[18:23] As tra cheayll eh shoh, daase eh feer trimshagh, son v'eh feer verchagh.
[18:24] As tra honnick Yeesey dy row eh feer trimshagh, dooyrt eh, Cre cha doillee as te dauesyn ta berchys oc, goll stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee!
[18:25] Son te ny sassey da camel goll trooid croae snaidey, na da dooinney berchagh dy gholl stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee.
[18:26] As dooyrt adsyn cheayll eh, Quoi eisht oddys v'er ny hauail?
[18:27] As dooyrt eh, Ta ny reddyn shoh neu phossible da deiney, agh t'ad possible da Jee.
[18:28] Eisht dooyrt Peddyr, Cur-my-ner, ta shinyn er dreigeil ooilley, as er n'eiyrt ort's.
[18:29] As dooyrt eh roo, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Nagh vel dooinney erbee t'er dreigeil thie, ny ayr ny moir, ny braaraghyn, ny ben, ny cloan, er graih reeriaght Yee,
[18:30] Nagh vow ymmodee fillee smoo 'sy traa t'ayn nish, as ayns y theihll ta ry-heet yn vea dy bragh farraghtyn.
[18:31] Eisht ghow eh huggey yn daa ostyl yeig, as dooyrt eh roo, Cur-my-ner ta shin goll seose gys Jerusalem, as bee dy chooilley nhee ta scruit liorish ny phadeyryn, my chione yn Mac dooinney, er ny chooilleeney.
[18:32] Son bee eh er ny vrah gys ny Ashoonee, as nee ad craidey mysh, as dellal dy roonagh rish, as ceau shellaghyn er;
[18:33] As scuitchee ad eh, as ver ad eh gy baase; as y trass laa nee eh girree reesht.
[18:34] As cha hoig ad veg jeh ny reddyn va fys oc er ny reddyn va loayrit.
[18:35] As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'eh er jeet er gerrey da Jericho, dy row dooinney doal dy row ny hoie rish lhiattee yn raad, shirrey jeirk.
[18:36] As tra cheayll eh yn pobble goll shaghey, denee eh cre v'ayn.
[18:37] As dinsh ad da, dy row Yeesey dy Nazateth goll shaghey.
[18:38] As dyllee eh, gra, Yeesey, vac Ghavid, jean myghin orrym.
[18:39] As hug y vooinjer hie roish oghsan da dy ve ny-host: agh dyllee eshyn wheesh shen smoo, Vac Ghavid, jean myghin orrym.
[18:40] As hass Yeesey, as doardee eh yn dooinney dy ve er ny choyrt lesh huggey: as tra v'eh er jeet er-gerrey, denee eh jeh,
[18:41] Gra, Cre bailt mee dy yannoo er dy hon? As dooyrt eh, Hiarn, dy voddym my hoilshey y gheddyn.
[18:42] As doogrt Yeesey rish, Dty hoilshey dy row ayd: ta dty chredjue er dty hauail.
[18:43] As chelleeragh hooar eh e hoilshey, as deiyr eh er, cur gloyr da Jee: ooilley yn pobble, tra honnick ad eh, hug ad moylley da Jee.
[19:1] As hie Yeesey stiagh, as jimmee eh trooid Jericho.
[19:2] As cur-my-ner, va dooinney va enmyssit Zaccheus, va ny ard-ghooinney mastey ny publicanee, as v'eh berchagh.
[19:3] As v'eh shirrey Yeesey y akin quoi v'eh, as cha dod eh kyndagh rish y pobble, son v'eh ny ghooinney giare.
[19:4] As roie eh roish, as hie eh seose er billey-sycamore dy gheddyn shilley jeh; son v'eh dy gholl shaghey yn raad shen.
[19:5] As tra va Yeesey er jeet gys yn ynnyd, yeeagh eh seose, as honnick eh eh, as dooyrt eh rish, Zaccheus, jean siyr, as tar neose; son jiu ta mish dy ghoaill aght ec dty hie.
[19:6] As ren eh siyr, as haink eh neose, as hug eh oltaghey-bea gennal da.
[19:7] As tra honnick ad shoh, v'ad ooilley jymmoosagh, gra, Dy row eh er gholl stiagh dy ee as dy iu marish dooinney dy ghrogh vea.
[19:8] As hass Zaccheus magh, as dooyrt eh rish y Chiarn, Cur-my-ner, Hiarn, yn derrey lieh jeh my chooid ta mee dy choyrt da ny boghtyn: as my ta mee er ghoaill red erbee dy molteyragh veih dooinney erbee, ta mee jannoo lhiassaghey kiare-filley da.
[19:9] As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Jiu ta saualtys er jeet gys y thie shoh, ayns wheesh as dy vel eshyn myrgeddin ny vac da Abraham.
[19:10] Son ta Mac y dooinney er jeet dy hirrey as dy hauail shen ny va caillit.
[19:11] As erreish daue shoh y chlahtyn, hie eh ny sodjey er e hoshiaght, as loayr eh coraa-dorraghey er-y-fa dy row eh er-gerrey da Jerusalem, as liorish dy row ad smooinaghtyn dy beagh reeriaght Yee dy gerrit er ny hoilshaghey:
[19:12] Dooyrt eh er-y-fa shen, Hie dooinney ooasle dy row gys cheer foddey, dy gheddyn da hene reeriaght, as dy heet back reesht.
[19:13] As deie eh er ny jeih sharvaantyn echey, as livrey eh daue jeih puint, as dooyrt eh roo, Jean-jee dellal derrey hig-ym.
[19:14] Agh dirree yn theay shen magh n'oi as hug ad chaghteraght geiyrt er, gra, Cha naill-lhieu yn dooinney shoh dy reill harrin.
[19:15] As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'eh er jeet reesht, erreish da yn reeriaght y gheddyn, dy doardee eh ny sharvaantyn shen dy ve eit huggey, daue v'eh er choyrt yn argid, dy gheddyn fys cre-woad va dy chooilley ghooinney er chosney liorish e ghellal.
[19:16] Eisht haink y chied er, gra, Hiarn, ta dty phunt er chosney jeih puint.
[19:17] As dooyrt eh rish, S'mie shen, harvaant vie: er-yn-oyr dy vel oo er ve firrinagh ayns red feer fardalagh, gow uss yn reill er jeih ard-valjyn.
[19:18] As haink yn nah er, gra, Hiarn, ta dty phunt er chosney queig puint.
[19:19] As dooyrt eh myrgeddin rishyn, Gow uss yn reill neesht er queig ard-valjyn.
[19:20] As haink fer elley, gra, Hiarn, cur-my ner, shoh dty phunt, t'er ny ve aym's tashtit ayns naptin:
[19:21] Son va mee ayns aggle royd, er-y-fa dy nee dooinney creoi oo: t'ou troggal shen nagh dug oo sheese, as buinn shen nagh ren oo cuirr.
[19:22] As dooyrt eh rish, Ass dty veeal hene nee'm oo y vriwnys, uss ghrogh harvaant, Va fys ayd dy row mee my ghooinney creoi, troggal shen nagh dug mee sheese, as buinn shen nagh chuirr mee:
[19:23] Cre'n-fa nagh dug oo my argid magh er use, tra harrin thie, dy voddin v'er droggal my chooid hene lesh bishaghey.
[19:24] As dooyrt eh roosyn,va kionfenish Gow-jee yn punt voishyn as cur-jee eh da fer ny jeih puint.
[19:25] (As dooyrt ad rish, Hiarn, ta jeih puint echey shen.)
[19:26] Son ta mee gra riu, Da dy chooilley unnane ta echey, vees er ny choyrt, as eshyn nagh vel echey, bee shen hene ny ta echey er ny ghoaill veih.
[19:27] Agh ad shen my noidyn nagh bailliu mish dy reill harrystoo, cur-jee lhieu ad ayns shoh, as cur-jee ad gy-baase kiongoyrt rhym.
[19:28] As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, hie eh rhymboo, myr v'ad goll seose gys Jerusalem,
[19:29] As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'ad er jeet er-gerrey da Bethphage as Bethany, ec y chronk va enmyssit cronk ny oliveyn, dy dug eh jees jeh e ostyllyn er chaghteraght,
[19:30] Gra, Gow-jee gys y balley-beg ta rhymbiu; as tra hig shiu gys shen, yiow shiu lhiy er-eistyr, er nagh ren rieau dooinney markiagh: feayshil-jee as cur-jee lhieu eh gys shoh.
[19:31] As my enys dooinney erbee j'iu, Cre'n fa ta shiu dy eaysley eh? Shoh myr nee shiu gra rish, Er-y-fa dy ve feme ec y Chiarn er.
[19:32] As hie ny chaghteryn rhymboo, as hooar ad eh myr v'eh er ghra roo.
[19:33] As myr v'ad feaysley yn lhiy, dooyrt y vooinjer by-liesh eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu feaysley yn lhiy?
[19:34] As dooyrt adsyn, Ta feme ec y Chiarn er.
[19:35] As hug ad lhieu eh gys Yeesey: as hilg ad nyn gharmadyn er y lhiy, as hug ad Yeesey ny hoie orroo.
[19:36] As myr v'eh goll, skeayll ad nyn eaddagh er y raad.
[19:37] As tra v'eh er jeet er-gerrey, eer ec goll-sheese cronk ny oliveyn, ghow yn slane sheshaght jeh e eiyrtyssee toshiaght dy ghoaill boggey, as dy chur moylley da Jee lesh ard-choraa, son ooilley ny obbraghyn mirrillagh v'ad er n'akin,
[19:38] Gra, Bannit dy row yn Ree ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn: shee ayns niau, as gloyr ayns yn yrjid.
[19:39] As dooyrt paart jeh ny Phariseeyn rish veih mastey yn pobble, Vainshter, cur oghsan da dty eiyrtyssee.
[19:40] As dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Ta mee ginsh diu, my chummagh ad shoh nyn jengey, dy jinnagh ny eer claghyn troggal seose nyn goraa.
[19:41] As tra v'eh er jeet er-gerrey, yeeagh eh er yn ard-valley, as cheayn eh harrish.
[19:42] Gra, Dy beagh toiggal er ve ayd's, dy jarroo ayd's, ayns dty laa shoh hene, jeh ny reddyn ta bentyn rish dty hee! agh nish t'ad follit veih dty hooillyn.
[19:43] Son hig ny laghyn ort, tra nee dty noidyn jeeg y yannoo mood, as soie-ee ad ad-hene mygeayrt, as cruinnee ad oo stiagh er dy chooilley heu.
[19:44] As lhieggee ad oo kiart rish y thalloo, as dty chloan cheu-sthie jeed; as cha vaag ad aynyd un chlagh er clagh elley: er-yn-oyr nagh dug oo tastey da'n earish haink mish dy dty yeeaghyn.
[19:45] As hie eh stiagh ayns y chiamble, as ren eh toshiaght dy eiyrt magh yn vooinjer va creck as kionnaghey ayn
[19:46] Gra roo, Te scruit, Ta my hie's thie yn phadjer: agh ta shiuish er n'yannoo eh ny ooig dy vaarlee.
[19:47] As v'eh gynsagh ad gagh laa ayns y chiamble. Agh va ny ard-saggyrtyn, as ny scrudeyryn, as leeideilee yn phobble shirrey eh y stroie,
[19:48] As cha row fys oc kys dy heet my geayrt-y-mysh; son va ooilley yn pobble feer aggindagh er clashtyn eh.
[20:1] AS haink eh gy-kione er unnane jeh ny laghyn shen, myr v'eh gynsaghey yn pobble ayns y chiamble as preacheil y sushtal, dy ren ny ard-saggrtyn as ny scrudeyryn soiaghey er, marish y chanstyr,
[20:2] As loayr ad rish, gra, Insh dooin, Cre'n phooar t'ayd dy yannoo ny reddyn shoh? ny quoi eh hug y phooar shoh dhyt?
[20:3] As dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh roo, Fenyms jiuish myrgeddin un red; as freggyr-jee mee:
[20:4] Bashtey Ean, nee veih niau ve, ny veih deiney?
[20:5] As loayr ad nyn mast' oc hene, gra, My jir mayd, Veih niau; jir eshyn, Cre'n-fa eisht nagh chred shiu eh?
[20:6] Agh my jir mayd, Veih deiney; nee ooilley yn pobble nyn glaghey shin; son t'ad dy shickyr credjal Ean dy ve ny adeyr.
[20:7] As dreggyr ad, nagh voddagh ad ginsh cre voish v'eh.
[20:8] As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Chamoo insh yms diuish cre'n phooar t'aym dy yannoo ny reddyn shoh.
[20:9] Eisht hie eh er e hoshiaght dy loayrt rish y pobble yn coraa-dorraghey shoh: Va dooinney dy row ren garey-feeyney y hoiaghey, as hoie eh eh rish, eirinnee, as hie eh gys cheer foddey son choud shen dy hraa.
[20:10] As ec yn imbagh, hug eh fer-mooinjerey gys ny eirinnee, dy choyrt da jeh mess y gharey-feeyney: agh woaill ny eirinnee eh, as hug ad eh ersooyl follym.
[20:11] As reesht hug eh fer-mooinjerey elley; as woaill ad eshyn myrgeddin, as ghell ad dy scammyltagh rish, as hug ad eh ersooyl follym.
[20:12] As reesht hug eh yn trass; as vroo ad eshyn myrgeddin, as deiyr ad eh ersooyl.
[20:13] Eisht dooyrt chiarn y gharey-feeyney Cre nee'm? Ver-ym huc my vac graihagh foddee dy der ad arrym da tra hee-ys ad eh.
[20:14] Agh tra honnick ny eirinnee eh, loayr ad eddyr ad-hene, gra, Shoh yn eirey: tar-jee, lhig dooin eh y varroo, dy vod yn eiraght ve lhien hene.
[20:15] Myr shen cheau ad eh magh ass y gharey-feeyney, as varr ad eh. Cre nee Chiarn y gharey-feeyney er-y-fa shen roo?
[20:16] Hig eh as stroie-ee eh ny eirinnee shoh, as ver eh yn garey-feeyney da feallagh elley. As tra cheayll ad shen, dooyrt ad, Nar lhig eh Jee.
[20:17] As yeeagh eh orroo, as dooyrt eh, Cre shoh eisht ta scruit, Ta'n chlagh ren ny masoonee y vee-lowal, er jeet dy ve yn ard-chlagh chorneilagh?
[20:18] Quoi-erbee huittys er y chlagh shen, hee eh er ny vroo: agh er quoi-erbee huittys y chlagh shen, nee ee cha meen as joan jeh.
[20:19] As va ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny scrudeyryn ayns yn oor cheddin shirrey eh y ghoaill; agh ghow ad aggle roish y pobble: son dennee ad dy row eh er loayrt yn coraa-dorraghey shoh nyn noisyn.
[20:20] As va sooill oc er, as hug ad magh peeikearyn va dy lhiggey orroo dy ve deiney cairagh, er-chee tayrtyn eh nyns e ghlare, as myr shen dy livrey eh gys pooar as reill y chiannoort.
[20:21] As denee ad jeh, gra, Vainshter, ta fys ain dy vel oo loayrt as gynsaghey cairagh; chamoo t'ou soiaghey jeh persoon erbee, agh gynsaghey raad Yee dy firrinagh
[20:22] Vel eh lowal dooin keesh y eeck da Cesar, mannagh vel?
[20:23] Agh dennee eh yn foalsaght oc, as dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu shirrey da my ghoaill ayns ribbey?
[20:24] Jeeagh-jee dou ping: quoi ta'n jalloo as y scrieu t'er cowraghey? Dreggyr ad as dooyrt ad, Cesar.
[20:25] As dooyrt eh roo, Eeck-jee er-y-fa shen da Cesar shen ny ta bentyn gys Cesar; as da Jee shen ny ta bentyn gys Jee.
[20:26] As cha voddagh ad greme y ghoaill er e ghoan kiongoyrt rish y pobble: as ghow ad yindys jeh'n ansoor echey, as chum ad nyn jengey.
[20:27] Eisht haink huggey shiartanse jeh ny Sadduceeyn (ta gobbal yn irree-seose-reesht veih ny merriu) as denee ad jeh,
[20:28] Gra, Vainshter, ta Moses er scrieu dooin, My ta braar dooinney erbee geddyn baase, as ben echey, as eh dy gheddyn baase gyn chloan, dy vel e vraar dy phoosey yn ven echey, as dy hroggal seose sluight gys e vraar.
[20:29] Va er-y-fa shen shiaght braaraghyn: as hooar y braar shinney, tra v'eh er phoosey ben, baase gyn chloan.
[20:30] As ghow yn nah vraar ee son ben, as hooar eshyn baase dyn chloan.
[20:31] As ghow yn trass ee: as er yn aght cheddin yn chiaght. As cha daag ad cloan, as hooar ad baase.
[20:32] Er-jerrey ooilley hooar y ven ee hene baase myrgeddin.
