[23:29] Son cur-my-ner, ta ny laghyn cheet, tra jir ad, Bannit ta ny mraane gennish, as ny breinyn nagh ren gymmyrkey, as ny keeaghyn nagh dug bainney.
[23:30] Eisht nee ad toshiaght dy ghra rish ny sleityn, Tuitt-jee orrin; as rish ny cruink, Coodee-jee shin.
[23:31] Son my t'ad jannoo ny reddyn shoh rish y billey oor, cre vees er ny yannoo rish y billey creen?
[23:32] As va myrgeddin daa chimmagh elley er nyn leeideil magh marish, dy ve er nyn goyrt gy-baase.
[23:33] As tra v'ad er jeet gys yn ynnyd ta enmyssit Calvary, ayns shen ren ad eshyn y chrossey, as ny kimmee; yn derrey yeh er y laue yesh, as y jeh elley er y laue chiare.
[23:34] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey, Ayr jean leih daue; son cha vel fys oc cre t'ad dy yannoo. As rheynn ad e choamrey, as hilg ad lottyn.
[23:35] As va'n pobble nyn shassoo cur-my-ner: as maroo ren ny fir-reill myrgeddin gannidys er, as gra, Haue eh feallagh elley; lhig da eh-hene y hauail my she Creest fer reiht Yee eh.
[23:36] As va ny sidooryn myrgeddin jannoo faghid er, cheet huggey, as chebbal da vinegar,
[23:37] As gra, My she ree ny Hewnyn oo, saue oo hene.
[23:38] As va'n scrieu shoh myrgeddin soit erskyn e chione, ayns letteryn dy Ghreek as dy Latin, as dy Hebrew, SHOH REE NY HEWNYN.
[23:39] As ren fer jeh ny kimmee v'er nyn groghey loayrt dy lunagh n'oi, gra, My she oo yn Creest, saue oo hene as shinyn.
[23:40] Agh dreggyr y jeh elley, cur oghsan da, as gra, Nagh vel aggle ort roish Jee, fakin dy vel uss fo yn vriwnys cheddin?
[23:41] As shinyn dy jarroo dy cairagh; son ta shin er gheddyn toilchinys cooie yn jannoo ain: agh cha vel y dooinney shoh er n'yannoo aggair erbee.
[23:42] As dooyrt eh rish Yeesey, Hiarn, cooinee orryms tra hig oo gys dty reeriaght.
[23:43] As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Dy bee uss marym's jiu ayns Paradise.
[23:44] As ve mysh y cheyoo oor, as va dorraghys harrish ooilley yn cheer gys yn nuyoo oor.
[23:45] As va'n ghrian dorraghey, as va curtan scarree yn chiamble raipit veih-my cheilley.
[23:46] As tra va Yeesey er n'eamagh lesh ard-choraa, dooyrt eh, Ayr, gys dty laueyn ta mish chymney my spyrryd: as tra v'eh er ghra shoh, phaart eh.
[23:47] Nish tra honnick y centurion cre va er jeet gy-kione, hug eh moylley da Jee, gra, Ayns firrinys v'eh shoh ny ghooinney cairagh.
[23:48] As ooilley yn pobble v'er jeet cooidjagh gys y shilley shen, hug ad my-ner ny reddyn va jeant, as goaill ad nyn gleeau, haink ad rhymboo.
[23:49] As ooilley e ainjyssee, as ny mraane deiyr er veih Galilee, hass ad foddey jeh cur-my-ner ny reddyn shoh.
[23:50] As cur-my-ner va dooinney va enmyssit Joseph, va ny er-coyrlee, as ny ghooinney mie as cairagh:
[23:51] (Cha row ayrt ny paart echey shoh ayns y choyrle ny yn jannoo oc) v'eh veih Arimathea, ard-valley jeh ny Hewnyn, (va myrgeddin eh-hene farkiaght son reeriaght Yee.)
[23:52] Hie yn dooinney shoh gys Pilate, as yeearree eh corp Yeesey,
[23:53] As ghow eh neose eh, as hoiII eh eh ayns aanrit, as doanluck eh eh ayns oaie va cleight ayns creg, raad nagh row rieau dooinney oanluckit roie.
[23:54] As va shen laa yn aarlaghey, as va yn doonaght tayrn er-gerrey.
[23:55] As hie ny mraane myrgeddin haink marish veih Galilee geiyrt er y corp, as hug ad my-ner yn oaie, as kys va'n corp er ny oanluckey.
[23:56] As haink ad rhymboo, as hooar ad aarloo spisyn as ooilyn; as ghow ad fea er laa yn doonaght cordail rish yn anney.
[24:1] Nish er y chied laa jeh'n chiaghtin, eer sy vadran, haink ad gys yn oaie, cur lhieu ny spisyn v'ad er gheddyn aarloo, as mraane elley maroo.
[24:2] As hooar ad y chlagh rowlit ersooyl jeh'n oaie.
[24:3] As hie ad stiagh, as cha dooar ad corp y Chiarn Yeesey.
[24:4] As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'ad ayns imnea mooar son shoh, cur-my-ner hass daa ghooinney lioroo ayns coamrey sollys.
[24:5] As myr v'ad ayns aggle, as croymmey sheese lesh nyn eddin gys y thalloo, dooyrt ad roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu shirrey yn vio mastey ny merriu?
[24:6] Cha vel eh ayns shoh, agh t'eh er n'irree: cooinee-jee cre dooyrt eh-hene riu choud's v'eh foast ayns Galilee,
[24:7] Gra, Shegin da'n Mac dooinney v'er ny lirrey gys laueyn deiney peccoil, as ve er ny chrossey, as girree reesht er y trsss laa.
[24:8] As chooinee ad er e ghoan,
[24:9] As haink ad back veih yn oaie, as dinsh ad ooilley shoh da'n un ostyl yeig, as da ooilley yn vooinjer elley.
[24:10] She Moirrey Malaine, as Joanna as Moirrey moir Yamys, as mraane elley va maroo, dinsh ny reddyn shoh da ny ostjllyn,
[24:11] As ghow ad y ghlare oc myr skeeal branlaadee, a cha dug ad geill daue.
[24:12] Eisht dirree Peddyr as roie eh gys yn oaie, as chroym eh sheese, as honnick eh ny aanrityn nyn lhie er-lheh, as jimmee eh roish, goaill yindys ec ny va er daghyrt.
[24:13] As cur-my-ner hie Jees jeu yn laa cheddin gys balley va enmyssit Emmaus, va mysh shiaght veeilley veih Jerusalem.
[24:14] As v'ad taggloo ry-cheilley mychione dy chooilley nhee v'er daghyrt.
[24:15] As haink eh gy-kione, choud as v'ad taggloo as resooney ry-cheilley, dy daink Yeesey hene er-gerrey, as dy jagh eh maroo.
[24:16] As va ny sooillyn oc er ny lhiettal nagh dug ad enney er.
[24:17] As dooyrt eh roo, Cre ny naightyn shoh ta shiu dy insh yn derrey yeh da'n jeh elley, myr ta shiu shooyll dy trimshagh er y raad?
[24:18] As dreggyr fer jeu, va'n ennym echey Cleopas, as dooyrt eh rish, Vel uss agh joarree ayns Jerusalem, as gyn fys ayd er ny reddyn t'ayns shen er jeet gy-kione er ny laghyn shoh?
[24:19] As dooyrt eh, Cre ny reddyn? As dooyrt adsyn rish, Mychione Yeesey dy Nazareth, va ny adeyr, as pooaral ayns jannoo as goo, kiongoyrt rish Jee; as ooilley yn pobble:
[24:20] As kys ren ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny fir-reill ain y livrey eh dy ve er ny gheyrey gys baase, as t'ad er chrossey eh.
[24:21] Agh va shinyn treishteil dy nee eshyn veagh er chur livrey-ys da Israel: as marish shoh ooilley, jiu yn trass laa neayr as hie ny reddyn shoh er jannoo.
[24:22] Myrgeddin va shiartanse dy vraane jeh'n cheshaght ain, hug orrin lane yindys y ghoaill, liorish dy row ad dy moghey ec yn oaie:
[24:23] As tra nagh dooar ad yn corp echey, haink ad as dooyrt ad, dy row ad er vakin ashlish dy ainleyn dinsh daue dy row eh bio.
[24:24] As hie shiartanse jeusyn va marinyn gys yn oaie, as hooar ad eh eer myr va ny mraane er ghra; agh eh-hene cha vaik ad.
[24:25] Eisht dooyrt eh roo, O shiuish gheiney mee hushtagh, as faase-chredjuagh, nagh vel goaill baght jeh ooilley ny ta ny phadeyryn er loayrt!
[24:26] Nagh beign da Creest ny reddyn shoh y hurranse as goll stiagh ayns e ghloyr?
[24:27] As goaill toshiaght ec Moses, as ooilley ny phadeyryn, hug eh bun daue er ooilley ny scriptyryn jeh dy chooilley nhee va bentyn rish hene.
[24:28] As haink ad er-gerrey da'n balley, raad v'ad goll: as v'eh myr dy beagh eh kiarit dy gholl ny-sodjey.
[24:29] Agh lhie ad er, gra, Fuirree marin, son ta'n fastyr er, as bunnys y laa ceaut. As hie eh stiagh dy uirriaght maroo.
[24:30] As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh ny hoie ec bee maroo, dy ghow eh arran, as vannee eh, as vrish eh, as hirveish eh orroo eh.
[24:31] As va ny sooillyn oc er nyn vosley, as hug ad enney er; as skell eh ersooyl ass nyn shilley.
[24:32] As dooyrt y derrey yeh jeu rish y jeh elley, Nagh row ny creeaghyn ain lossey cheu-sthie j'in, choud as v'eh taggloo rooin er y raad, as choud as v'eh fosley dooin ny scriptyryn?
[24:33] As hrog ad orroo yn oor cheddin, as hyndaa ad gys Jerusalem, as hooar ad yn un ostyl yeig er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, as y cheshaght va maroo.
[24:34] Dooyrt roo, Ta'n Chiarn er n'irree son shickyrys, as v'eh er ny akin liorish Simon.
[24:35] Eisht dinsh adsyn cre ny reddyn va jeant er y raad, as kys hug ad enney er, liorish brishey arran.
[24:36] As myr v'ad myr shoh loayrt, hass Yeesey hene ayns y vean oc, as dooyrt eh roo, Shee dy row hiu.
[24:37] Agh v'ad seaghnit ayns nyn aigney as agglit, as heill ad dy nee scaan v'ad dy akin.
[24:38] As dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu seaghnit, as cre'n-fa ta mee-ourys troggal ayns nyn greeaghyn?
[24:39] Jeeagh-jee er my laueyn as my chassyn dy nee mish mee-hene t'ayn: loaghtee-jee mee, as jeeagh-jee, son cha vel feill as craueyn ec scaan, myr hee shiu aym's.
[24:40] As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, yeeagh eh daue e laueyn as e chassyn.
[24:41] As choud as nagh row ad foast credjal son boggey, agh goaill yindys, dooyrt eh roo, Vel veg y veaghey eu ayns shoh?
[24:42] As hug ad da peesh dy eeast roast as dy chere-volley.
[24:43] As ghow eh, as d'ee eh kiongoyrt roo.
[24:44] As dooyrt eh roo, Shoh ny goan loayr mish riu, choud as va mee foast meriu dy beign da dy chooilley nhee ve cooilleenit va scruit ayns leigh Voses, as ayns ny phadeyryn, as ayns ny psalmyn my-mychione's.
[24:45] Eisht doshil eh yn tushtey oc, dy voddagh ad ny scriptyryn, y hoiggal,
[24:46] As dooyrt eh roo, Shoh myr te scruit, as shoh myr ve kiarit da Creest dy hurranse, as dy irree yn trass laa veih ny merriu:
[24:47] As arrys as leih peccaghyn dy ve er nyn breacheil ayns yn ennym echey, mastey dy chooilley ashoon, goaill toshiaght ec Jerusalem.
[24:48] As ta shiuish nyn veanishyn jeh ny reddyn shoh.
[24:49] As cur-my-ner, ver-yms hiu gialdyn my Ayrey: agh fuirree-jee ayns ard-valley Yerusalem, derrey vees shiu coamrit lesh pooar veih'n yrjid.
[24:50] As hug eh lesh magh ad choud as gys Bethany: as hrog eh seose e laueyn as vannee eh ad.
[24:51] As haink eh gy-kione, choud as v'eh dy vannaghey ad, dy row eh er ny scarrey voue, as er ny hroggal seose gys niau.
[24:52] As hug ad ooashley da, as hyndaa ad gys Jerusalem lesh boggey mooar:
[24:53] As v'ad kinjagh ayns y chiamble, cur moylley as gloyr da Jee.

### John

[1:1] Ayns y toshiaght va'n Goo, as va'n Goo marish Jee, as va'n Goo Jee.
[1:2] Va'n Goo cheddin ayns y toshiaght marish Jee.
[1:3] Liorishyn va dy chooilley nhee er ny yannoo; as n'egooish cha row nhee erbee jeant va er ny yannoo;
[1:4] Aynsyn va bea, as va'n vea soilshey deiney.
[1:5] As ren y soilshey soilshean ayns y dorraghys, as cha ren y dorraghys goaill-rish.
[1:6] Va dooinney er ny choyrt veih Jee va enmyssit Ean.
[1:7] Haink eh shoh son feanish, dy ymmyrkey feanish jeh'n toilshey, liorishyn dy vod dagh dy chooilley ghooinney credjal.
[1:8] Cha nee eh va'n soilshey shen, agh v'eh er ny choyrt dy ymmyrkey feanish jeh'n toilshey shen.
[1:9] Shen va'n soilshey firrinagh, ta soilshean ayns dy chooilley ghooinney ta cheet er y theihll.
[1:10] V'eh ayns y theihll as va'n seihll er ny yannoo liorishyn, as y seihll cha dug enney er.
[1:11] Haink eh gys e vooinjer hene, agh cha ren e vooinjer hene soiaghey jeh.
[1:12] Agh whilleen as ren soiaghey jeh, dauesyn hug eh pooar dy ve nyn mec dy Yee, eer dauesyn ta credjal ayns yn ennym echey:
[1:13] Va er nyn ruggey, cha nee jeh fuill, ny jeh aigney ny foalley, ny jeh aigney dooinney, agh jeh Jee.
[1:14] As ghow yn Goo er dooghys ny foalley, as ren eh baghey nyn mast' ain (as hug shin my-ner yn ghloyr echey, yn ghloyr myr jeh'n ynrycan Mac er-ny-gheddyn jeh'n Ayr) lane dy ghrayse as dy irrinys.
[1:15] (Dymmyrk Ean feanish jeh, as deie eh, gra, Shoh eh jeh ren mish loayrt, T'eshyn ta cheet my yei er ny hoiaghey roym; son v'eh roym)
[1:16] As jeh'n slane towse echey ta shin ooilley er gheddyn ayrn, as grayse er grayse.
[1:17] Son va'n leigh er ny choyrt liorish Moses agh haink grayse as firrinys liorish Yeesey Creest.
[1:18] Cha vel unnane erbee er vakin Jee ec traa erbee; yn ynrycan Mac v'er ny-gheddyn, ta ayns oghrish yn Ayr, eshyn t'er hoilshaghey eh.
[1:19] As shoh feanish Ean, tra hug ny Hewnyn saggyrtyn as Leyiteyn veih Jerusalem dy enaght jeh, Quoi oo hene?
[1:20] As ghow eh rish, as cha dob eh; agh ghow eh rish, Cha nee mish yn Creest.
[1:21] As denee ad jeh, Quoi eisht? Nee oo Elias? As dooyrt eshyn, Cha nee. Nee oo yn phadeyr shen? As dansoor eh, Cha nee.
[1:22] Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Quoi oo? dy vod mayd ansoor y choyrt dauesyn t'er choyrt shin: Cre t'ou gra my-dty-chione hene?
[1:23] Dooyrt eh, Mish coraa fer fockley magh ayns yn aasagh, Kiartee-jee raad y Chiarn, myr dooyrt y phadeyr Esaias.
[1:24] As v'adsyn v'er nyn goyrt, jeh ny Phariseeyn.
[1:25] As denee ad jeh, as dooyrt ad rish, Cre'n-fa t'ou bashtey eisht mannagh nee oo yn Creest, ny Elias, ny'n phadeyr shen?
[1:26] Dreggyr Ean ad, gra, Ta mish bashtey lesh ushtey: agh ta fer shassoo nyn mast' eu, nagh vel enney eu er;
[1:27] Eshyn eh ta cheet my yei, agh t'er ny hoiaghey roym, kiangley ny braagyn echey cha vel mish feeu dy eaysley.
[1:28] Va ny reddyn shoh jeant ayns Bethabara er cheu elley jeh Jordan, raad va Ean bashtey
[1:29] Yn nah laa honnick Ean Yeesey cheet ny whail, as dooyrt eh, Cur-my-ner Eayn Yee, ta goaill ersooyl peccah yn theihll.
[1:30] Shoh eshyn mychione dooyrt mee, My yei ta dooinney cheet, t'er ny hoiaghey roym; son v'eh roym.
[1:31] As cha row enney aym's er: agh dy beagh eh er ny hoilshaghey da Israel, shen-y-fa haink mish bashtey lesh ushtey.
[1:32] As dymmyrk Ean feanish, gra, Honnick mee yn Spyrryd cheet neose veih niau myr calmane, as tannaghtyn er.
[1:33] As cha dug mish enney er: agh eshyn ren mish y choyrt dy vashtey lesh ushtey, dooyrt eh shen rhym, Ersyn hee oo yn Spyrryd cheet neose as tannaghtyn er, shen eh ta bashtey lesh y Spyrryd Noo.
[1:34] As honnick mee eh, as dymmyrk mee feanish, dy nee shoh Mac Yee.
[1:35] Yn nah laa reesht va Ean ny hassoo, as jees jeh e ynseydee:
[1:36] As yeeagh eh er Yeesey, myr v'eh shooyl, as dooyrt eh, Cur-my-ner Eayn Yee.
[1:37] As cheayll yn daa ynseydagh eh loayrt, as deiyr ad er Yeesey.
[1:38] Eisht hyndaa Yeesey, as honnick eh ad geiyrt er, as dooyrt eh roo, Cre ta shiu dy hirrey? Dooyrt adsyn rish, Rabbi (ta shen dy ghra, 'sy ghlare ainyn,Vainshter) cre raad t'ou baghey?
[1:39] Dooyrt eh roo, Tar-jee as hee shiu. Haink ad as honnick ad c'raad v'eh baghey, as duirree ad marish yn laa shen: son ve mysh y jeihoo oor.
[1:40] Eer jeh'n jees cheayll Ean loayrt, as deiyr er, va Andreays, braar Simon Peddyr.
[1:41] Hooar eshyn hoshiaght e vraar hene Simon, as dooyrt eh rish, Ta shin er gheddyn yn Messias ta shen dy ghra, Yn Creest.
[1:42] As hug eh lesh eh gys Yeesey. As tra honnick Yeesey eh, dooyrt eh, Uss Simon mac Jona: bee oo enmyssit Cephas, ta shen dy ghra Peddyr.
[1:43] Yn laa er-giyn she aigney Yeesey ve dy gholl magh gys Galilee, as hooar eh Philip, as dooyrt eh rish, Eiyr orrym.
[1:44] Nish va Philip veih Bethsaida, ard valley Andreays as Peddyr.
[1:45] Veeit Philip rish Nathanael, as dooyrt eh rish, Ta shin er gheddyn eshyn, jeh ren Moses ayns y leigh, as ny phadeyryn scrieu, Yeesey dy Nazareth, mac Yoseph.
[1:46] As dooyrt Nathanael rish, Vod nhee erbee mie cheet magh ass Nazareth? Dooyrt Philip rish, Tar royd as hee oo.
[1:47] Honnick Yeesey Nathanael cheet ny whail, as dooyrt eh jehsyn, Cur-my-ner Israelite firrinagh, ayn nagh vel molteyrys erbee.
[1:48] Dooyrt Nathanael rish, Cre'n enney t'ayd orrym's? Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Roish my deie Philip ort, tra v'ou fo yn villey-figgagh, honnick mee oo.
[1:49] Dreggyr Nathanael as dooyrt eh rish, Rabbi, oo mac Yee, oo ree Israel.
[1:50] Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Er-y-fa dy dooyrt mee rhyt, dy vaik mee oo fo'n villey-figgagh, vel oo credjal? hee oo reddyn smoo na ad shoh.
[1:51] As dooyrt eh rish, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Ny lurg shoh hee shiu niau foshlit, as ainleyn Yee goll seose as cheet neose er Mac y dooinney.
[2:1] AS er y trass laa va poosey ayns Cana dy Ghalilee; as va moir Yeesey ayns shen.
[2:2] As va chammah Yeesey cuirt, as e ynseydee, gys y vannish.
[2:3] As tra v'ad laccal feeyn, dooyrt moir Yeesey rish, Cha vel feeyn oc.
[2:4] Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Ven, cre t'ain dy yannoo rish shen? cha vel my oor foast er jeet.
[2:5] Dooyrt e voir rish y vooinjer, Jean-jee shiuish cre-erbee jir eh riu.
[2:6] As va soit ayns shen shey siyn cloaie ry-hoi ushtey, lurg cliaghtey ny Hewnyn son glenney, cummal ghaa ny three dy firkinyn y pheesh.
[2:7] Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Lhieen-jee ny siyn lesh ushtey. As lhieen ad ad seose gys yn oirr.
[2:8] As dooyrt eh roo, Tayrn-jee nish, as cur-jee lhieu gys mainshter ny cuirraghyn. As hug ad lhieu eh.
[2:9] Tra va mainshter ny cuirraghyn er vlashtyn er yn ushtey va chyndait gys, feeyn, as nagh row fys echey cre voish ve (agh va fys ec ny sharvaantyn va tayrn yn ushtey~ deie mainshter ny cuirraghyn er y dooinney phoosee
[2:10] As dooyrt eh rish, Ta dy chooilley ghooinney ec y toshiaght soiaghey magh feeyn mie; as tra ta deiney er n'iu dy mie, eisht feeyn smessey: agh t'ou uss er vreayll y feeyn mie derrey nish.
[2:11] Yn toshiaght shoh dy virrilyn ren Yeesey ayns Cana dy Ghalilee, as hoilshee eh magh e ghloyr; as ren e ynseydee credjal ayn.
[2:12] Ny lurg shen, hie eh-hene, as e voir, as e vraaraghyn, as e ynseydee sheese gys Capernaum; as cha nhimmey laa duirree ad ayns shen.
[2:13] As va Caisht ny Hewnyn er-gerrey, as hie Yeesey seose gys Jerusalem,
[2:14] As hooar eh ayns y chiamble feallagh va creck dew, as kirree, as calmaneyn, as y vooinjer va caghlaa argid nyn soie:
[2:15] As tra v'eh er n'yannoo kip dy choyrdyn keylley, deiyr eh ad ooilley ass y chiamble, as ny kirree, as ny dew; as spreih eh magh yn argid ocsyn va caghlaa, as hilg eh harrish ny buird;
[2:16] As dooyrt eh roosyn va creck calmaneyn, Ersooyl-jee lesh ny reddyn shoh, ny jean-jee thie my Ayrey ny hie margee.
[2:17] As chooinee e ynseydee dy row eh scruit, Ta graih jeean dty hie er my chur mow.
[2:18] Eisht dreggyr ny Hewnyn, as dooyrt ad rish, Cre'n cowrey t'ou dy yeeaghyn dooin, fakin dy vel oo jannoo ny reddyn
[2:19] Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Lhieg-jee yn chiamble shoh, as trog-yms eh reesht ayns three laa.
[2:20] Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn, Shey bleeaney as da-eed va'n chiamble shoh dy hroggal, as Jean uss troggal eh ayns three laa?
[2:21] Agh mychione chiamble e chorp hene loayr eshyn.
[2:22] Shen-y-fa tra v'eh er n'irree veih ny merriu, chooinee ny ynseydee dy row eh er ghra shoh roo: as chred ad yn scriptyr, as y raa va Yeesey er loayrt.
[2:23] Nish tra v'eh ec Jerusalem ec y chaisht, rish earish ny feailley, ren ymmodee credjal ayns yn ennym echey, tra honnick ad y mirrilyn v'eh er n'yannoo.
[2:24] Agh cha hreisht Yeesey eh-hene orroo, er-yn-oyr dy row enney echey er dy chooilley ghooinney,
[2:25] As nagh row feme echey er unnane erbee dy ymmyrkey feanish jeh dooinney: son va ys echey cre va ayns dooinney.
[3:1] VA dooinney jeh ny Phariseeyn enmyssit Nicodemus, Dy ard-ghooinney mastey ny Hewnyn:
[3:2] Haink eh shoh gys Yeesey ayns yn oie, as dooyrt eh rish, Rabbi, ta fys ain dy nee fer-ynsee as t'er jeet veih Jee: son cha vod dooinney erbee ny mirrilyn shen y yannoo t'ou uss dy yannoo, mannagh bee Jee marish.
[3:3] Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Mannagh bee dooinney er ny ruggey reesht, cha vod eh reeriaght Yee y akin.
[3:4] Dooyrt Nicodemus rish, Kys oddys dooinney v'er ny ruggey tra t'eh shenn? vod eh goll stiagh yn nah cheayrt ayns brein, e vayrey, as cheet er y theihll?
[3:5] Dreggyr Yeesey, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Mannagh bee dooinney er ny ruggey jeh ushtey as jeh'n spyrryd, cha vod eh goll stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee.
[3:6] Shen t'er ny ruggey jeh'n eill, te foalley; as shen t'er ny ruggey jeh'n Spyrryd, te spyrrydoil.
[3:7] Ny gow yindys dy dooyrt mee rhyt, Shegin diu v'er nyn ruggey reesht.
[3:8] Ta'n gheay sheidey raad saillee, as t'ou clashtyn y sheean eck, agh cha s'ayd cre voish t'ee cheet, ny cre'n raad t'ee goll: myr shen ta dy chooilley unnane t'er ny ruggey Jeh'n Spyrryd.
[3:9] Dreggyr Nicodemus as dooyrt eh rish, Kys oddys ny reddyn shoh y ve?
[3:10] Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Vel uss dty er-ynsee ayns Israel, as nagh vel toiggal ayd jeh ny reddyn shoh?
[3:11] Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, ta shin loayrt shen ta fys ain er, as gymmyrkey feanish Jeh ny ta shin er vakin; as cha vel shiu soiaghey jeh'n eanish ain.
[3:12] My ta mish er loayrt riu jeh reddyn seihltagh, as nagh vel shiu dy my chredjal, kys nee shiu my chredjal my loayr-ym riu jeh reddyn flaunyssagh?
[3:13] As cha vel dooinney erbee er gholl seose gys niau, agh eshyn haink neose veih niau, eer yn Mac dooinney ta ayns niau.
[3:14] As myr ren Moses yn ard-nieu y hroggal seose ayns yn aasagh, myr shen shegin da Mac y dooinney v'er ny hroggal seose:
[3:15] Nagh jean quoi-erbee ta credjal ayn cherraghtyn, agh dy bee yn vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn echey.
[3:16] Son lheid y ghraih shen hug Jee da'n theihll, dy dug eh e ynrycan Vac v'er ny gheddyn, nagh jinnagh quoi-erbee chred jagh aynsyn cherraghtyn, agh yn vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn y chosney.
[3:17] Son cha dug Jee e vac gys y theihll, dy gheyrey yn seihll; agh dy voddagh y seihll liorishyn v'er ny hauail.
[3:18] Eshyn ta credjal ayn, cha vel eh er ny gheyrey: agh eshyn nagh vel credjal ayn, t'eh er ny gheyrey hannah, er-yn-oyr nagh vel eh er chredjal ayns ennym yn ynrycan Mac v'er ny gheddyn dy Yee.
[3:19] As shoh yn vriwnys, dy vel soilshey er jeet gys y theihll, as dy row deiney ny s'graihee er y dorraghys (na er y toilshey, er-y fa dy row nyn obbraghyn olk.
[3:20] Son ta dy chooilley unnane ta jannoo dy holk, cur feoh da'n toilshey, chamoo t'eh cheet gys y toilshey, son nagh jig brah er ny obbraghyn echey.
[3:21] Agh eshyn ta jannoo firrinys, t'eh cheet gys y toilshey, dy vod e obbraghyn v'er nyn soilshaghey magh, dy vel ad er nyn obbraghey ayns Jee.
[3:22] Ny lurg shoh haink Yeesey as e ynseydee gys cheer Yudea, as duirree eh ayns shen maroo, as ren eh bashtey.
[3:23] As va Ean myrgeddin bashtey ayns Enon, er-gerrey da Salem, er-y-fa dy row palchey dy ushtey ayns shen: as haink ad as v'ad er nyn mashtey.
[3:24] Son cha row Ean foast tilgit ayns pryssoon.
[3:25] Eisht dirree question eddyr paart jeh ynseydee Ean as ny Hewnyn, mychione bashtey.
[3:26] As haink ad gys Ean, as dooyrt ad rish Rabbi, eshyn va mayrt er cheu elley dy Yordan, da ren oo feanish y ymmyrkey, cur my-ner, t'eshyn bashtey, as ta dy chooilley ghooinney cheet huggey.
[3:27] Dreggyr Ean as dooyrt eh, Cha vod dooinney nhee erbee y ghoaill er hene, mannagh bee eh er ny choyrt da veih niau.
[3:28] Ren shiuish shiu hene feanish y ymmyrkey lhiam, dy dooyrt mee, Cha nee mish yn Creest, agh dy vel mee er my choyrt roish.
[3:29] Eshyn dooinney yn phoosee ta ben y phoosee echey: agh ta carrey dooinney yn phoosee ta ny hassoo as geaishtagh rish, goaill boggey mooar jeh coraa yn dooinney poosee: ta shoh my voggey's er-y-fa shen jeant magh.
[3:30] Shegin dasyn bishaghey, agh shegin dooys parail.
[3:31] Eshyn ta cheet veih'n yrjid, t'eh er skyn ooilley: eshyn ta jeh yn thalloo, t'eh thallooinagh, as loayrt jeh'n thalloo: eshyn ta cheet veih niau, t'eh erskyn ooilley.
[3:32] As y red t'eh er vakin as er chlashtyn, shen t'eh gymmyrkey feanish jeh; as cha vel dooinney erbee soiaghey jeh'n eanish echey.
[3:33] Eshyn t'er n'yannoo soiaghey jeh'n eanish echey, t'eh er chur y seal echey huggey, dy vel Jee firrinagh.
[3:34] Son t'eshyn ta Jee er choyrt, loayrt goan Yee: son cha nee liorish towse ta Jee cur y Spyrryd da.
[3:35] Ta'n Ayr graihagh er y Mac, as t'eh er chur dy chooilley nhee fo yn laue echey.
[3:36] Eshyn ta credjal ayns y Mac, ta'n vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn echey: as eshyn nagh vel credjal yn Mac, cha vaik eh yn vea, agh nee Jymmoose Yee tannaghtyn er.
[4:1] TRA va fys ec y Chiarn er-y-fa shen, kys va ny Phariseeyn er chlashtyn dy row Yeesey jannoo as bashtey ny sliee dy eiyrtyssee na va Ean.
[4:2] (Ga nagh row Yeesey hene bashtey, agh e ynseydee)
[4:3] Daag eh Judea, as jimmee eh reesht gys Galilee.
[4:4] As beign da goll trooid Samaria.
[4:5] Eisht haink eh gys ard-valley dy Samaria, ta enmyssit Sychar, er-gerrey da'n pheesh dy halloo hug Jacob da e vac Joseph.
[4:6] Nish va chibbyr Yacob ayns shen. Myr va Yeesey er-y-fa shen skee lesh e yurnah, hoie eh sheese ayns shen liorish y chibbyr: as ve mysh y cheyoo oor.
[4:7] Haink ben dy Samaria dy hayrn ushtey: dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Cur dou jough.
[4:8] Son va ny ostyllyn er n'gholl gys y valley dy chionnaghey beaghey.
[4:9] Eisht dooyrt y ven dy Samaria rish,Kys dy vel uss, ta dty Hew, shirrey jough orrym's, ta my ven dy Samaria? son cha vel veg y dellal ec ny Hewnyn rish ny Samaritanee.
[4:10] Dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh r'ee, Dy beagh fys ayd's er gioot Yee, as quoi eh ta gra rhyt, Cur jough dou! veagh oo er hirrey ersyn, as veagh eh er chur dhyt ushtey bio.
[4:11] Dooyrt y ven rish, Vainshter, cha vel red erbee ayd dy hayrn lesh, as ta'n chibbyr dowin: cre voish eisht ta'n ushtey bio shen ayd?
[4:12] Vel uss ny s'ooasle na'n ayr ain Jacob, hug dooin y chibbyr shoh, as diu j'ee eh hene, as e chloan, as y maase echey?
[4:13] Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh r'ee, Quoi-erbee iu-ys jeh'n ushtey shoh bee eh paagh reesht:
[4:14] Agh quoi-erbee iu-ys jeh'n ushtey ver-yms da, cha bee eh dy bragh paagh: agh bee yn ushtey ver-ym da ny farrane ushtey ayn nee geill gys y vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn.
[4:15] Dooyrt y ven rish, Vainshter, cur dooys yn ushtey shoh, nagh bee'm paagh, as nagh jig-ym ayns shoh dy hayrn.
[4:16] Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Immee as eie er dty heshey, as tar ayns shoh.
[4:17] Dreggyr y ven as dooyrt ee, Cha vel sheshey aym. Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, t'ou er ghra dy mie, Cha vel sheshey aym:
[4:18] Son ta queig deiney er ny ve ayd, as eshyn t'ayd nish, cha nee dty heshey-poost eh: ayns shen t'ou er ghra yn irriney,
[4:19] Dooyrt y ven rish, Vainshter, ta mee cur tastey dy nee phadeyr oo.
[4:20] Ren ny ayraghyn ain ooashlaghey Jee er y clieau shoh; as ta shiuish gra, dy nee ayns Jerusalem ta'n boayl raad lhisagh sleih ooashlaghey.
[4:21] Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Ven, cred mish, ta'n oor cheet tra nagh jean shiu er y clieau shoh, ny foast ec Jerusalem ooashley 'choyrt da'n Ayr.
[4:22] Ta shiuish cur ooashley da, cha s'eu cre: ta fys ainyn cre ta shin cur ooashley da; son ta saualtys jeh ny Hewnyn.
[4:23] Agh ta'n oor cheet, as nish ayn dy jean ny ooashleyderyn firrinagh ooashlaghey yn Ayr ayns Spyrryd as ayns firrinys: son ta'n Ayr shirrey nyn lheid oc shoh dy chur ooashley da.
[4:24] Ta Jee ny Spyrryd, as shegin dauesyn ta ooashlaghey eh, ooashley y choyrt da ayns Spyrryd as ayns firrinys.
[4:25] Dooyrt y ven rish, Ta fys aym dy vel Messias cheet ta enmyssit Creest: tra hig eshyn, inshee eh dooin dy chooilley nhee.
[4:26] Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, She mish ta loayrt rhyt eh shen.
[4:27] As er shen haink e ostyllyn, as ghow ad yindys dy row eh taggloo rish y ven: foast cha dooyrt dooinney erbee, Cre t'ou dy hirrey? ny, Cre'n-fa t'ou taggloo r'ee?
[4:28] Daag yn ven eisht yn saagh-ushtey eck, as hie ee rhymbee gys y valley, as dooyrt ee rish ny deiney
[4:29] Tarjee as hee shiu dooinney t'er n'insh dou ooilley ny ren mee rieau: nagh nee shoh yn Creest?
[4:30] Eisht hie ad magh ass y valley as haink ad huggey.
[4:31] Ayns y traa shen ghuee e ostyllyn er, gra, Vainshter, gow beaghey.
[4:32] Agh dooyrt eshyn roo, Ta bee aym's dy ee nagh vel fys euish er.
[4:33] Shen-y-fa dooyrt ny ostyllyn yn derrey yeh rish y jeh elley, Vel dooinney erbee er chur lesh nhee erbee huggey dy ee?
[4:34] Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Yn beaghey aym's eh, dy yannoo yn aigney echeysyn t'er my choyrt, as dy chooilleeney yn obbyr echey.
[4:35] Nagh vel shiu gra, dy vel kiare meeghyn foast, as eisht ta'n fouyr cheet? cur-my ner ta mish gra riu, Trog-jee seose nyn sooillyn, as jeeagh-jee er ny magheryn; son t'ad bane hannah son y fouyr.
[4:36] As ta'n beaynee geddyn faill, as chaglym mess gys y vea veayn: dy vod chammah yn correyder as y beaynee boggey y ghoaill cooidjagh.
[4:37] As ayns shoh ta'n raa shen firrinagh, Ta fer cuirr, as fer elley buinn.
[4:38] Hug mish shiu magh dy vuinn cooid nagh ren shiu y laboragh: ta deiney elley er laboragh, as ta shiuish er gholl stiagh er y laboraght oc.
[4:39] As ren ymmodee jeh Samaritanee yn ard-valley shen credjal ayn, kyndagh rish raa yn ven, ren feanish y ymmyrkey, Dinsh eh dou ooilley ny ren mee rieau.
[4:40] Myr shoh tra va ny Samaritanee el jeet huggey, ghuee ad er, eh dy uirriaght maroo: as duirree eh ayns shen daa laa.
[4:41] As ren ymmodee elley credjal ayn e coontey e ghoo hene;
[4:42] As dooyrt ad rish y ven, Nish ta shin credjal, cha nee son y raa ayd's; son ta shiu hene er chlashtyn eh, as ta fys ain, dy nee shoh dy jarroo yn Creest Saualtagh y theihll.
[4:43] Nish lurg daa laa jimmee eh veih shen, as hie eh roish gys Galilee:
[4:44] Son ren Yeesey hene feanish y ymmyrkey, nagh vel ooashley ec phadeyr ayns e heer hene,
[4:45] Tra v'eh eisht er jeet gys Galilee, ren ny Galileanee mooar jeh, liorish dy row ad er vakin ooilley ny ren eh ec Jerusalem, ec y feailley: son v'adsyn er ve ec y feailley.
[4:46] Myr shen haink Yeesey reesht gys Cana ayns Galilee, raad v'eh er hyndaa yn ushtey gys feeyn. As va chiarn dy row, va'n mac echey ching ec Capernaum.
[4:47] Tra cheayll eh dy row Yeesey er jeet veih Judea gys Galilee, hie eh huggey, as ghuee eh er, eh dy heet neose dy lheihys e vac: son v'eh raad y vaaish.
[4:48] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish, Mannagh vaik shiu cowraghyn as yindyssyn, cha jean shiu credjal.
[4:49] Dooyrt y chiarn rish, Vainshter, tar neose roish my vow my lhiannoo baase.
[4:50] Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Immee royd; ta dty vac bio. As chred y dooinney yn ockle va Yeesey er loayrt rish, as hie eh roish.
[4:51] As tra v'eh nish goll sheese, haink ny sharvaantyn echey ny whail, as dinsh ad da, gra, Ta dty vac bio.
[4:52] Eisht denee eh jeu cre'n oor ren eh toshiaght dy choural: as dooyrt ad rish, Jea ec y chiaghtoo oor daag y chiassaghey eh.
[4:53] Myr shen va fys ec yn ayr dy nee ayns yn oor cheddin va Yeesey er ghra rish, Ta dty vac bio; as ren eh-hene credjal as ooilley e hie.
[4:54] Shoh neesht yn nah virril ren Yeesey, tra v'eh er jeet veih Judea gys Galilee.
[5:1] NY lurg shoh va feailley ny Hewnyn, as hie Yeesey seose gys Jerusalem.
[5:2] Nish ta ec Jerusalem liorish giat ny geyrragh, loghan, ta enmyssit ayns y ghlare Hebrewnagh Bethesda, ta queig porchyn er.
[5:3] Ayndoo shoh va nyn lhie ymmodee dy leih dourinagh, doail, baccee, shirgeydee, as v'ad fieau er gleashaght yn ushtey.
[5:4] Son va ainle goll sheese ec lheid y traa shen ayns yn ushtey, as seiy yn ushtey: quoi erbee eisht va hoshiaght goll sheese lurg seiy yn ushtey, v'eh er ny laanaghey jeh doghan erbee dy row er.
[5:5] As va ayns shen dooinney dy row, va doghan er ve er rish hoght bleeaney jeig as feed.
[5:6] Tra honnick Yeesey eh ny lhie, as fys echey dy row eh er ve myr shen ry-foddey dy hraa, dooyrt eh rish, Nailt ve er dty laanaghey?
[5:7] Dreggyr yn annooinagh eh, Vainshter, cha vel dooinney erbee aym, tra ta'n ushtey seiyt, dy my cur sheese ayns y loghan: agh choud as ta mee cheet, ta fer elley goll sheese roym.
[5:8] Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Trog ort, gow seose dty lhiabbee as jean shooyll.
[5:9] As er-y-chooyl va'n dooinney er ny lheihys, as ghow eh seose e lhiabbee, as huill eh: as er y laa shen va'n doonaght.
[5:10] Dooyrt ny Hewnyn er-y-fa shen rishyn v'er ny lheihys, She laa yn doonaght t'ayn; cha vel eh lowal dhyt gymmyrkey dty lhiabbee.
[5:11] Dreggyr eshyn ad, Eshyn ren m'y laanaghey, dooyrt eh shen rhym, Trog dty lhiabbee as shooill.
[5:12] Eisht denee ad jeh, Quoi va yn dooinney shen dooyrt rhyt, Trog dty lhiabbee as shooill?
[5:13] As cha row fys echeysyn v'er ny lheihys, quoi v'eh: son va Yeesey er gholl dy lhiattee, liorish dy row chaglym mooar dy leih ayns y voayl shen.
[5:14] Ny lurg shen hooar Yeesey eh ayns y chiamble, as dooyrt eh rish, Cur-my-ner, t'ou er dty laanaghey: ny jean peccah ny smoo, er-aggle dy jig red smessey ort.
[5:15] Jimmee yn dooinney roish, as dinsh eh da ny Hewnyn dy nee Yeesey v'er laanaghey eh.
[5:16] As er-yn-oyr shen ren ny Hewnyn tranlaase er Yeesey, as v'ad shirrey eh y choyrt gy-baase, er-y-fa dy row eh er n'yannoo ny red dyn shoh er laa yn doonaght.
[5:17] Agh dreggyr Yeesey ad, Ta my Ayr gobbraghey derrey nish: as ta mish gobbraghey.
[5:18] Shen-y-fa va ny Hewnyn wheesh shen smoo shleeuit er cur dy baase eh; er-yn-oyr dy row eh cha nee ynrycan er vrishey yn doonaght, agh er ghra myrgeddin dy nee Jee va'n Ayr echey, jannoo eh-hene corrym rish Jee.
[5:19] Eisht dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh roo, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cha vod y Mac nhee erbee y yannoo jeh hene, agh ny t'eh fakin yn Ayr dy yannoo: son cre-erbee t'eshyn dy yannoo, ta'n Mac jannoo myrgeddin.
[5:20] Son ta'n Ayr graihagh er y Mac, as t'eh soilshaghey da dy chooilley nhee t'eh hene dy yannoo: as soilshee eh da obbragh yn smoo na ad shoh, dy vod shiu yindys y ghoaill.
[5:21] Son myr ta'n Ayr troggal seose, as cur bioys da ny merriu: eer myr shen ta'n Mac bioghey yn vooinjer saillish.
[5:22] Son cha vel yn Ayr briwnys dooinney erbee; agh t'eh er livrey dy chooilley vriwnys gys y Mac:
[5:23] Dy voddagh dy chooilley ghooinney ooashley y choyrt da'n Mac, myr t'ad cur ooashley da'n Ayr. Eshyn nagh vel cur ooashley da'n Mac, cha vel eh coyrt ooashley da'n Ayr ren y choyrt eh.
[5:24] Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Eshyn ta clashtyn my ghoo's, as credjal ayn syn t'er my choyrt, ta'n vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn echey, as cha jig eh gys coayl-anmey: agh t'eh er gholl veih baase gys bea.
[5:25] Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Ta'n oor cheet, as nish ayn, tra nee ny merriu clashtyn coraa Mac Yee: as bee adsyn chlinnys er nyn mioghey.
[5:26] Son 'naght myr ta ec yn Ayr bioys ayn hene; myr shen t'eh er choyrt da'n Mac bioys y ve echey ayn hene;
[5:27] As t'eh er choyrt da pooar dy yannoo briwnys myrgeddin, er-y-fa dy nee Mac y dooinney eh.
[5:28] Ny gow-jee yindys jeh shoh: son ta'n oor cheet, tra chlinnys ooilley ny t'ayns ny oaiaghyn e choraa,
[5:29] As hig ad magh; adsyn t'er n'yannoo dy mie, gys irree-seose-reesht y vea; as adsyn t'er n'yannoo dy olk, gys irree-seose reesht y choayl-anmey.
[5:30] Cha voddym jee'm pene nhee erbee y yannoo: myr ta mee clashtyn, ta mee briwnys: as ta my vriwnys cairagh, er-yn-oyr nagh vel mee shirrey my aigney hene, agh aigney yn Ayr t'er my choyrt.
[5:31] My ta mee gymmyrkey feanish jee'm pene, cha vel my eanish firrinagh.
[5:32] Ta fer elley ta gymmyrkey feanish jee'm, as ta fys aym dy vel yn eanish t'eh dy ymmyrkey jee'm firrinagh.
[5:33] Hug shiuish fys gys Ean, as dymmyrk eh feanish gys yn irriney.
[5:34] Agh cha vel mish goaill fenish veih dooinney: agh shoh ta mee dy ghra, dy vod shiu v'er nyn sauail.
[5:35] V'eshyn ny hoilshey gial as sollys: as va shiu booiagh son earish boggey 'ghoaill ayns y soilshey echey.
[5:36] Agh ta feanish stroshey aym's na Ean: son ny obbraghyn hug my Ayr dou dy chooilleeney, ny obbraghyn cheddin ta mee dy yannoo, t'ad gymmyrkey feanish jee'm, dy vel yn Ayr er my choyrt.
[5:37] As ta'n Ayr hene t'er my choyrt, er n'ymmyrkey feanish jee'm. Cha vel shiuish er chlashtyn e choraa ec traa erbee, ny er vakin e chaslys.
[5:38] As cha vel eu yn goo echeysyn tannaghtyn ayndiu: son eshyn t'eh er choyrt, aynsyn cha vel shiu credjal.
[5:39] Ronsee-jee ny scriptyryn, son ayndoosyn ta shiu smooinaghtyn dy vel y vea veayn eu, as she ad shen ta gymmyrkey feanish jeem's.
[5:40] As cha vel shiu booiagh cheet hym's, dy vod yn vea y ve eu.
[5:41] Cha vel mish soiaghey jeh ooashley deiney.
[5:42] Agh ta toiggal aym jiuish, nagh vel graih Yee ayndiu.
[5:43] Ta mish er jeet ayns ennym my Ayrey, as cha vel shiu goaill rhym: my hig fer elley ayns e ennym hene, rishyn nee shiu goaill.
[5:44] Kys oddys shiuish credjal ta geddyn ooashley yn derrey yeh veih yn jeh elley, as nagh vel shirrey yn ooashley ta veih Jee ny lomarcan?
[5:45] Ny smooinee-jee dy jean-yms plaiynt erriu gys yn Ayr: ta ayn ta plaiynt nyn 'oi eu, eer Moses, ayn ta shiu treishteil.
[5:46] Son dy beagh shiu er chredjal Moses, veagh shiu er chredjal aynym's; son scrieu eh jeem's.
[5:47] Agh mannagh gred shiu ny screeuyn echeysyn, kys nee shiu credjal ny goan aym's?
[6:1] NY lurg shoh hie Yeesey harrish faarkey Ghalilee, ny Tiberias.
[6:2] As deiyr earroo mooar dy leih er, er-y-fa dy vaik ad ny mirrilyn ren eh orroosyn va doghanit.
[6:3] As hie Yeesey seose er slieau, as hoie eh ayns shen marish e ostyllyn.
[6:4] As va'n Chaisht, feailley ny Hewnyn er gerrey.
[6:5] Tra va Yeesey eisht er hroggal seose e hooillyn, as fakin earroo mooar dy leih cheet huggey, dooyrt eh rish Philip, Cre-voish oddys mayd arran y chionnaghey, dy yannoo magh ad shoh?
[6:6] (As shoh dooyrt eh dy phrowal eh: son v'eh hene kiarit cre dy yannoo.)
[6:7] Dreggyr Philip eh, Cha bee feeagh daa cheead ping dy arran dy liooar daue, dy vod dagh unnane oc kuse y ghoaill.
[6:8] Dooyrt fer jeh ny ostyllyn echey, Andreays, braar Simon Peddyr, rish,
[6:9] Ta scollag ayns shoh ta queig bwilleenyn oarn echey, as daa eeast veggey; agh cre t'ad shen mastey whilleen?
[6:10] As dooyrt Yeesey, Cur-jee er ny deiney soie sheese. Nish va lane faiyr ayns yn ynnyd. Myr shen hoie ny deiney sheese ayns earroo mysh queig thousaneyn.
[6:11] As ghow Yeesey ny bwilleenyn, as tra v'eh er chur booise, rheynn eh ad er e ostyllyn, as rheynn adsyn ad orroosyn myr v'ad soie; as myrgeddin jeh ny eeastyn wheesh as bailloo.
[6:12] Tra v'ad jeant magh, dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Jean-jee yn vrooilliagh ta er-mayrn y haglym cooidjagh nagh bee nhee erbee caillit.
[6:13] Er shen ren ad eh y haglym, as lhieen ad daa vaskad jeig lesh fooilliagh ny queig bwilleenyn oarn, va er-mayrn erreish daue v'er n'ee.
[6:14] Eisht dooyrt ny deiney shen, tra v'ad er vakin y mirril va Yeesey er n'yannoo. She shoh ayns firrinys yn phadeyr shen va ry-hoi cheet gys y theihll.
[6:15] Tra dennee Yeesey er-y-fa shen dy darragh ad, as dy goghe ad eh er-niart, dy yannoo eh ny ree, hie eh seose reesht er slieau eh-hene ny-lomarcan.
[6:16] As tra va'n fastyr er, hie e ostyllyn sheese gys y cheayn.
[6:17] As ghow ad lhuingys, as haink ad harrish y cheayn gys Capernaum: as ve nish dorraghey, as cha row Yeesey er jeet huc.
[6:18] As dhatt y keayn lesh niart stermagh ny geayee.
[6:19] Myr shen tra v'ad er n'ymmyrt mysh kiare veeilley, honnick ad Yeesey shooyl er y cheayn, as tayrn er-gerrey da'n lhong: as ghow ad aggle.
[6:20] Agh dooyrt eshyn roo, She mish t'ayn, ny bee aggle erriu.
[6:21] Eisht ghow ad eh dy arryltagh stiagh ayns y lhong: as chelleeragh va'n lhong ec y thalloo raad v'ad goll.
[6:22] Yn laa er-giyn, tra honnick yn pobble va nyn shassoo cheu elley jeh'n cheayn nagh row baatey erbee elley ayns shen, cheu-mooie jeh'n un vaatey shen va ny ostyllyn er n'ghoaill, as nagh jagh Yeesey maroosyn ayns y vaatey, agh dy row ny ostyllyn er n'gholl ersooyl nyn-lomarcan:
[6:23] (Ny-yeih va baatyn elley er jeet veih Tiberias, er-gerrey da'n boayl ren ad arran y ee ayn, erreish da'n Chiarn v'er chur booise.)
[6:24] Tra honnick y pobble er-y-fa shen nagh row Yeesey ayns shen, ny e ostyllyn, ghow adsyn myrgeddin lhuingys, as haink ad gys Capernaum, briaght son Yeesey.
[6:25] As tra hooar ad eh er y cheu elley jeh'n cheayn, dooyrt ad rish, Rabbi, cuin haink oo ayns shoh?
[6:26] Dreggyr Yeesey ad, as dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Ta shiu dy my hirrey's, cha nee er-yn-oyr dy vaik shiu ny mirrilyn, agh son dy d'ee shiu jeh ny bwilleenyn, as dy row shiu jeant magh.
[6:27] Ny bee-jee imneagh son y beaghey ta cherraghtyn, agh son y beaghey shen ta tannaghtyn gys y vea veayn, nee yn Mac dooinney y choyrt diu: son eshyn ta Jee yn Ayr er chowraghey.
[6:28] Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cre nee mainyn, dy vod mayd obbraghyn Yee y yannoo?
[6:29] Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Shoh obbyr Yee, shiu dy chredjal aynsyn t'eh er choyrt.
[6:30] Dooyrt ad er-y-fa shen rish, Cre'n cowrey t'ou dy yeeaghyn eisht, dy vod mayd fakin as credjal aynyd? cre ta dty obbyr?
[6:31] D'ee ny ayraghyn ain manna ayns yn aasagh; myr te scruit, Hug eh daue arran veih niau dy ee.
[6:32] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cha dug Moses diu yn arran shen veih niau, agh my Ayr ta coyrt diu yn arran firrinagh veih niau.
[6:33] Son arran Yee eshyn ta cheet neose veih niau, as ta cur e vioys son y theihll.
[6:34] Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cur dooinyn dy bragh yn arran shoh.
[6:35] As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Mish arran y vea: eshyn ta cheet hym's, cha bee eh dy bragh accryssagh; as eshyn ta credjal aynym, cha bee eh dy bragh paagh.
[6:36] Agh ta mish er ghra riu, dy vel shiu myrgeddin er my akin's, as nagh vel shiu credjal.
[6:37] Hig adsyn ooilley hym's ta'n Ayr dy chur dou; as eshyn ta cheet hym, cha jeanym er aght erbee y yiooldey voym.
[6:38] Son haink mish neose veih niau, cha nee dy yannoo my aigney hene, agh yn aigney echeysyn ren m'y choyrt.
[6:39] As shoh aigney yn Ayr ta er my choyrt, jeh ooilley ny hug eh dou nagh gaillin veg, agh dy droggin eh seose reesht ec y laa jerrinagh.
[6:40] As shoh yn aigney echeysyn ta er my choyrt, dy chooilley unnane ta fakin y Mac as credjal ayn, yn vea dy bragh farraghtyn dy ve echey: as trog-yms seose eh ec y laa jerrinagh.
[6:41] Eisht va ny Hewnyn jymmoosagh rish, er-y-fa dy dooyrt eh, Mish arran y vea haink neose veih niau.
[6:42] As dooyrt ad, Nagh nee shoh Yeesey Mac Yoseph, yn ayr as y voir echey shione dooin? kys eisht dy vel eh gra, Haink mee neose veih niau?
[6:43] Dreggyr Yeesey er-y-fa shen as dooyrt eh roo, Ny lhig da jymmoose ve ny mast' eu.
[6:44] Cha vod dooinney erbee cheet hym's, mannagh jean yn Ayr t'er my choyrt y hayrn eh: as trog-yms seose eh ec y laa jerrinagh.
[6:45] Te scruit ayns ny phadeyryn, As bee ad ooilley ynsit liorish Jee. Dy chooilley ghooinney er-y-fa shen t'er chlashtyn, as er n'ynsaghey veih yn Ayr, t'eh cheet hym's.
[6:46] Cha nee dy vel dooinney erbee er va kin yn Ayr, cheu-mooie jehsyn ta veih Jee, t'eh shen er vakin yn Ayr.
[6:47] Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Eshyn ta credjal ayn-yms ta'n vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn echey.
[6:48] Mish arran y vea.
[6:49] D'ee ny ayraghyn euish manna ayns yn aasagh, as t'ad marroo.
[6:50] Shoh yn arran ta cheet neose veih niau, dy vod dooinney gee jeh, as gyn baase y gheddyn.
[6:51] Mish yn arran bio, haink neose veih niau: my ee-ys dooinney erbee jeh'n arran shoh, bee eh bio son dy bragh: as yn arran neem's y choyrt, she my eill eh, ver-yms son bioys y theihll.
[6:52] Va ec ny Hewnyn er-y-fa shen argane nyn mast oc hene, gra, Kys oddys y dooinney shoh cur dooin e eill dy ee?
[6:53] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy firrinagh focklagh ta mee gra riu, Mannagh jean shiu feill yn Mac dooinney y ee, as e uill y iu, cha vel y vea eu ayndiu.
[6:54] Eshyn ta gee my eill, as giu my uill, ta'n vea veayn echey, as trog-yms seose eh ec y laa jerrinagh.
[6:55] Son dy firrinagh she bee my eill, as dy firrinagh she jough my uill.
[6:56] Eshyn ta gee my eill as giu my uill, t'eh baghey aynym's, as mish aynsyn
[6:57] Myr ta'n Ayr bio er my choyrt's, as ta mee bio liorish yn Ayr: myr shen neesht vees eshyn ta dy my ee's, bio liorym.
[6:58] Shoh yn arran haink neese veih niau; cha nee myr ren ny ayraghyn eu manna y ee, as t'ad marroo: bee eshyn ta gee jeh'n arran shoh, bio son dy bragh.
[6:59] Ny goan shoh loayr eh ayns y synagogue, myr v'eh gynsaghey ayns Capernaum.
[6:60] Dooyrt ymmodee er-y-fa shen jeh e eiyrtee, tra cheayll ad shoh, Shoh raa creoi, quoi oddys y chlashtyn eh?
[6:61] Tra va fys ec Yeesey ayn hene dy row e eiyrtee jymmoosagh son shoh, dooyrt eh roo, Vel shoh cheet ayns raad y chredjue eu?
[6:62] Cre my hee shiu Mac y dooinney goll seose raad v'eh roie?
[6:63] She yn spyrryd ta bioghey, cha vel yn eill jannoo veg y vie: ny goan ta mish dy loayrt riu, t'ad spyrryd as t'ad bea.
[6:64] Agh ta paart jiuish nagh vel credjal. Son va fys ec Yeesey er-dyn toshiaght, quoi v'ad nagh row credjal, as quoi yinnagh eh y vrah.
[6:65] As dooyrt eh, Shen-y-fa dooyrt mish riu, nagh vod dooinney erbee cheet hym's mannagh bee eh er ny choyrt da liorish my Ayr.
[6:66] Veih yn traa shen hie ymmodee jeh e eiyrtee back, as cha huill ad arragh marish.
[6:67] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish y daa ostyl yeig, Jed shiuish myrgeddin reue?
[6:68] Eisht dreggyr Simon Peddyr eh, Hiarn, quoi gys hem mayd? ayd's ta goan y vea veayn.
[6:69] As ta shin credjal, as shickyr jeh dy nee uss yn Creest, Mac y Jee bio.
[6:70] Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Nagh vel mish er reih shiuish yn ghaa-yeig, as ta fer j'iu ny youyl?
[6:71] Loayr eh jeh Yuaase Iscariot mac Simon: son eshyn eh va dy vrah eh, as v'eh fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig.
[7:1] NY lurg shoh duirree Yeesey ayns Galillee: son cha row eh booiagh cummal ayns Judea, er-yn-oyr dy row ny Hewnyn shirrey eh y varroo.
[7:2] Nish va feailley cabbaneyn ny Hewnyn er-gerrey.
[7:3] Dooyrt e vraaraghyn er-y-fa shen rish, Faag y voayl shoh, as immee gys Judea, dy vod ny eiyrtee t'ayd ayns shen myrgeddin fakin ny obbraghyn t'ou dy yannoo.
[7:4] Son cha vel dooinney erbee freayll e obbraghyn follit, as eh-hene shirrey dy ve cronnal: My t'ou jannoo ny reddyn shoh soilshee oo hene da'n theihll.
[7:5] Son chamoo ren e vraaraghyn hene credjal ayn.
[7:6] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Cha vel my hraa's foast er jeet: agh ta'n traa euish dy kinjagh jesh diu.
[7:7] Cha vod y seihll dwoaie y chur diuish, agh dooys te cur dwoaie; er-yn-oyr dy vel mee gymmyrkey feanish jeh, dy vel ny obbraghyn echey olk.
[7:8] Immee-jee shiuish seose gys y feailley shoh: cha vel mish son goll seose foast gys y feailley shoh, er-yn-oyr nagh vel my hraa foast er jeet.
[7:9] Tra v'eh er ghra ny goan shoh roo duirree eh myr v'eh ayns Galilee.
[7:10] Agh tra va e vraaraghyn er gholl seose, eisht hie eshyn myrgeddin seose gys y feailley, cha nee dy foshlit, agh myr dy beagh eh dy follit.
[7:11] Eisht va ny Hewnyn briaght er e hon ec y feailley, as dooyrt ad, Cre vel eh?
[7:12] As va lane argane mastey yn pobble mychione echey: son va paart gra, She dooinney mie eh: as feallagh elley gra, Cha nee; agh t'eh molley yn pobble.
[7:13] Ny-yeih, cha loayr dooinney erbee dy foshlit jeh, goaill aggle roish ny Hewnyn.
[7:14] Nish mysh mean y feailley, hie Yeesey seose gys y chiamble, as dynsee eh.
[7:15] As ghow ny Hewnyn yindys, gra, Kys ta lheid yn ynsagh ec y dooinney shoh, nagh row eh-hene rieau ynsit?
[7:16] Dreggyr Yeesey ad, as dooyrt eh, Cha vel my ynsagh lhiam pene, agh leshyn t'er my choyrt.
[7:17] My vees dooinney erbee aggindagh yn aigney echeysyn y yannoo, yiow eh toiggal jeh'n ynsagh, nee veih Jee te, ny vel mee loayrt jee'm pene.
[7:18] Eshyn ta loayrt jeh hene, t'eh shirrey e ooashley hene: agh eshyn ta shirrey yn ooashley echeysyn t'er choyrt eh, t'eh shen firrinagh, as cha vel neu-chairys erbee ayn.
[7:19] Nagh dug Moses yn leigh diu, as cha vel fer j'iu freayll yn leigh? Cre'n-fa ta shiu shirrey my vioys y ghoaill?
[7:20] Dreggyr y pobble eh, as dooyrt ad, Ta drogh-spyrryd breagagh aynyd: Quoi ta shirrey dty vioys y ghoaill?
[7:21] Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Ta mish er n'yannoo yn un obbyr shoh, as ta shiu ooilley goaill yindys.
[7:22] Hug Moses er-y-fa shen yn giarey chymmylt diu, (cha nee son dy vel eh jeh Moses, agh jeh ny ayraghyn) as ta shiu er laa yn doonaght giarey-chymmylt dooinney.
[7:23] My ta dooinney er y doonaght goaill giarey chymmylt, son nagh bee leigh Voses er ny vrishey; vel shiuish jymmoosagh rhym's, son dy vel mee er n'yannoo dooinney ooilley magh slane er y doonaght?
[7:24] Ny jean-jee briwnys rere yn caslys, agh jean-jee briwnys cairagh.
[7:25] Eisht dooyrt paart jeusyn va veih Jerusalem, Nagh nee shoh eh t'ad shirrey dy varroo?
[7:26] Agh cur-my-ner, t'eh loayrt dy foshlit, as cha vel ad gra veg n'oi: vel dy jarroo fys ec ny firreill dy nee shoh yn Creest firrinagh?
[7:27] Ny-yeih ta enney ain er y dooinney shoh cre-voish t'eh: agh tra hig Creest, cha bee fys ec dooinney erbee cre-voish t'eh.
[7:28] Eisht deie Yeesey ayns y chiamble myr v'eh gynsaghey, gra, Ta chammah enney eu orrym's, aa ta fys eu cre-voish ta mee: as cha vel mish er jeet jee'm pene, agh t'eshyn t'er ny choyrt firrinagh, eshyn cha nione diu.
[7:29] Agh shione dooys eh, son ta mee veih, as t'eh er my choyrt.
[7:30] Eisht v'ad shirrey y ghoaill eh: agh cha dug dooinney erbee laue er, son nagh row yn oor echey foast er jeet.
[7:31] As ren ymmodee jeh'n pobble credjal ayn, as dooyrt ad, Tra hig Creest, jean eh ny shlee mirril na ad shoh ta'n dooinney shoh er n'yannoo?
[7:32] Cheayll ny Phariseeyn dy row yn pobble tallagh myr shoh my-e-chione: as hug ny Phariseeyn as ny ard-saggyrtyn magh sidooryn dy ghoaill eh.
[7:33] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Foast tammylt beg ta mish meriu, as eisht ta mee goll huggeysyn t'er my choyrt.
[7:34] Shirree shiu mee agh cha vow shiu mee: as y raad ta mish, cha vod shiuish cheet.
[7:35] Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn nyn mast' oc hene, C'raad hed eh, nagh vow mayd eh? jed eh gys ny Hewnyn t'er nyn skeayley mastey ny Ashoonee, as adsyn y ynsaghey .
[7:36] Cre'n monney dy raa shoh t'eh er loayrt, Shirree shiu mee, agh cha vow shiu mee: as y raad ta mish cha vod shiuish cheet?
[7:37] Er y laa s'jerree, laa mooar ny feailley, hass Yeesey, as deie eh, gra, My ta dooinney erbee paagh, lhig da cheet hym's as giu.
[7:38] Eshyn ta credjal aynym's, myr ta'n scriptyr er ghra, Ass y chree echeysyn roieys strooanyn dy ushtey bio.
[7:39] (Agh shoh loayr eh jeh'n Spyrryd, v'adsyn va credjal ayn ry-hoi gheddyn: son cha row yn Spyrryd Noo foast er ny choyrt, er yn-oyr nagh row Yeesey foast er ny ghloyraghey.)
[7:40] Dooyrt ymmodee jeh'n phobble er-y fa shen, tra cheayll ad y raa shoh, Ayns firrinys shoh yn phadeyr.
[7:41] Dooyrt feallagh elley, She shoh yn Creest. Agh dooyrt paart, Jig Creest ass Galilee?
[7:42] Nagh vel y scriptyr er ghra, dy vel Creest dy heet jeh sluight Ghavid, as ass y balley Bethlehem, raad ruggyr David?
[7:43] Myr shen va streeu mastey'n pobble mychione echey.
[7:44] As va paart jeu son goaill eh; agh cha dug dooinney jeu laue er.
[7:45] Eisht haink ny sidooryn gys ny ard saggyrtyn as ny Phariseeyn, dooyrt roo, Cre'n-fa nagh dug shiu lhieu eh?
[7:46] Dreggyr ny sidooryn, Cha ren rieau dooinney loayrt myr y dooinney shoh.
[7:47] Eisht dreggyr ny Phariseeyn ad, Vel shiuish myrgeddin er nyn molley?
[7:48] Vel veg jeh ny fir-reill, as jeh ny Phariseeyn er chredjal ayn?
[7:49] Agh ta'n pobble shoh, nagh vel toiggal yn leigh, fo mollaght.
[7:50] Dooyrt Nicodemus roo (eh haink gys Yeesey ayns yn oie, v'eh fer jeusyn.)
[7:51] Vel y leigh ainyn deyrey dooinney erbee roish clashtyn y choyrt da, as prowal oc n'oi cre t'eh er n'yannoo?
[7:52] Dreggyr adsyn, as dooyrt ad rish, Nee ass Galilee t'ou uss myrgeddin? jean-jee ronsaghey as jeeaghyn: son cha vel phadeyr erbee er droggal ayns Galilee.
[7:53] As jimmee dy chooilley ghooinney roish gys e hie hene.
[8:1] HIE Yeesey gys cronk ny Oliveyn.
[8:2] As dy moghey laa-ny-vairagh hie eh reesht gys y chiamble, as haink ooilley yn phobble huggey; as hoie eh sheese, as dynsee eh ad.
[8:3] As hug ny scrudeyryn as ny Phariseeyn lhieu huggey ben va goit ayns brishey-poosey; as tra v'ad er hoiaghey ee kiongoyrt rish,
[8:4] Dooyrt ad rish, Vainshter, va'n ven shoh goit ayns brishey-poosey, ayns yn eer peccah.
[8:5] Nish ta Moses ayns y leigh er chur sarey dooin, e lheid dy ve er ny claghey, agh cre t'ou uss dy ghra?
[8:6] Shoh dooyrt ad dy phrowal eh, dy vod dagh cooish chassid y ve oc n'oi. Agh chroym Yeesey sheese, as lesh e vair scrieu eh er y laare, myr nagh beagh eh dy nyn glashtyn.
[8:7] As myr lhie ad er son ansoor, hrog eh eh-hene seose, as dooyrt eh roo, Lhig dasyn ta fegooish peccah nyn mast'eu tilgey yn chied chlagh urree.
[8:8] As chroym eh sheese reesht, as scrieu eh er y laare.
[8:9] As v'adsyn cheayll eh, er nyn gheyrey liorish nyn gooin-sheanse hene, as hie ad magh fer lurg fer jeu, goaill toshiaght veih yn er-shinney gys yn er-saa: as va Yeesey faagit ny-lomarcan, as y ven ny shassoo kiongoyrt rish.
[8:10] Tra hrog Yeesey eh-hene seose, as nagh vaik eh unnane erbee agh y ven, dooyrt eh r'ee, Ven, cre vel ad shen dty chassidee? vel dooinney erbee er dty gheyrey?
[8:11] Dooyrt ish, Cha vel dooinney erbee, Hiarn. As dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Chamoo ta mish dy dty gheyrey: immee royd, as ny jean peccah arragh.
[8:12] Eisht loayr Yeesey roo reesht, gra, Mish soilshey yn theihll: eshyn ta geiyrt orrym's, cha shooyllee eh ayns y dorraghys, agh bee echeysyn soilshey yn vea,
[8:13] Dooyrt ny Phariseeyn er-y-fa shen rish, T'ou gymmyrkey feanish jeed hene; cha vel dty eanish firrinagh.
[8:14] Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Ga dy vel mee gymmyrkey feanish jee'm pene, foast ta'n eanish firrinagh: son ta fys aym cre-voish haink mee, as c'raad ta mee goll; agh cha s'euish cre-voish haink mee ny c'raad ta mee goll.
[8:15] Ta shiuish briwnys lurg briwnys ny foalley; cha vel mish briwnys dooinney erbee.
[8:16] As foast my ta mee briwnys, ta my vriwnys firrinagh: son cha vel mish my lomarcan, agh mish as yn Ayr t'er my choyrt, t'eh marym.
[8:17] Eer ayns y leigh eu hene te scruit, dy vel feanish daa ghooinney firrinagh.
[8:18] Ta mish gymmyrkey feanish dou hene, as ta'n Ayr t'er my choyrt gymmyrkey feanish dou.
[8:19] Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cre vel dty Ayr? Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha vel enney eu orrym's, ny er my Ayr: dy beagh enney er ve eu orrym s, veagh enney er ve eu er my Ayr myrgeddin.
[8:20] Ny goan shoh loayr Yeesey 'sy room tashtee, myr v'eh gynsaghey ayns y chiamble: as cha dug dooinney erbee laue er, son cha row yn oor echey foast er jeet.
[8:21] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo reesht, Ta mee goll roym, as nee shiu my hirrey, as yiow shiu baase ayns nyn beccaghyn: raad ta mish goll, cha vod shiuish cheet.
[8:22] Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn, Jean eh eh hene y varroo? er-yn-oyr dy vel eh gra, raad ta mish goll, cha vod shiuish cheet.
[8:23] As dooyrt eh roo, Ta shiuish veih heese ta mish veih heose: ta shiuish jeh'n theihll shoh, cha vel mish jeh'n theihll shoh.
[8:24] Dooyrt mee er-y-fa shen riu, dy voghe shiu baase ayns nyn beccaghyn: son mannagh vel shiu credjal dy nee mish eh, yiow shiu baase ayns nyn beccaghyn.
[8:25] Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Quoi oo hene? As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Yn fer cheddin dooyrt mee riu er-dyn toshiaght.
[8:26] Ta ymmodee reddyn aym's dy ghra as dy vriwnys jiuish: agh ta eshyn t'er my choyrt firrinagh as ta mee loayrt rish y theihll shen ta mee er chlashtyn veihsyn.
[8:27] Cha hoig ad dy row eh loayrt roo my chione yn Ayr.
[8:28] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Tra vees shiu erreish yn Mac dooinney y hroggal seose, eisht bee fys eu dy nee mish eh, as nagh vel mee jannoo nhee erbee jee'm pene; agh dy vel mee loayrt ny reddyn shen ta my Ayr er chur roym.
[8:29] As ta eshyn t'er my choyrt marym: cha vel yn Ayr er my aagail my lomarcan: son ta mee dy kinjagh jannoo ny reddyn shen ta dy wooiys eh.
[8:30] Choud as v'eh loayrt ny goan shoh ren ymmodee credjal ayn.
[8:31] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish ny Hewnyn shen va credjal ayn, My nee shiu tannaghtyn ayns my ghoo, eisht bee shiu dy jarroo ny ynseydee ayms;
[8:32] As bee toiggal eu jeh'n irriney, as nee yn irriney shiu y heyrey.
[8:33] Dreggyr adsyn eh, She sluight Abraham shin, as cha row shin rieau ayns bondiaght da dooinney erbee: cre'n aght t'ou gra eisht, Bee shiu er nyn yannoo seyr?
[8:34] Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Dy firrinagh-focklagh ta mee gra riu, Quoi-erbee ta cur-rish peccah, t'eh ayns bondiaght peccah.
[8:35] As cha vel y charvaant tannaghtyn kinjagh ayns y thie: agh ta'n Mac tannaght yn kinjagh.
[8:36] My nee yn Mac er-y-fa shen shiuish seyr, bee shiu seyr dy jarroo.
[8:37] Ta fys aym dy nee sluight Abraham shiu; agh ta shiu shirrey mish y varroo, er-y-fa nagh vel my ghoo er ghoaill greme erriu.
[8:38] Ta mish loayrt shen ny ta mee er n'akin ec my Ayr's: as ta shuish jannoo shen ny ta shiu er vakin ec yn ayr euish.
[8:39] Dreggyr ad as dooyrt ad rish, Abraham yn ayr ainyn. Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy beagh shiuish nyn gloan da Abraham, yinnagh shiu obbraghyn Abraham.
[8:40] Agh nish ta shiu shirrey mish y varroo, dooinney t'er n'insh diu yn irriney, ta mee er chlashtyn veih Jee: shoh cha ren Abraham.
[8:41] Ta shiuish cur-rish obbraghyn nyn ayrey hene. Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cha ruggyr shinyn ayns maarderys; cha vel agh un Ayr ain, ta shen, Jee.
[8:42] Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy beagh Jee yn Ayr eu, veagh shiu graihagh orrym's; son hie mee magh, as haink mee veih Jee; as cha daink mee jee'm pene, agh eshyn t'er my choyrt.
[8:43] Cre'n-fa nagh vel shiu toiggal my ghlare? te son nagh vel shiu cur geill da my ghoo.
[8:44] Ta shiuish jeh'n ayr eu yn drogh spyrryd, as saynt nyn ayrey ver shiu rish: v'eshyn ny ghunver er-dyn toshiaght, as cha ren eh tannaghtyn 'syn ynrickys, son nagh vel yn irriney ayn. Tra t'eh loayrt breg, t'eh loayrt jeh e chooid hene : son t'eh ny vreagerey, as ayr ny breagey.
[8:45] As ga dy vel mee ginsh diu yn irriney, cha vel shiu dy my chredjal.
[8:46] Quoi jiuish ta cur peccah my lieh? as my ta mee gra yn irriney, cre'n-fa nagh vel shiu dy my chredjal?
[8:47] Eshyn ta veih Jee, t'eh cur geill da goan Yee: agh cha vel shiuish cur geill daue, son nagh vel shiu veih Jee.
[8:48] Eisht dreggyr ny Hewnyn, as dooyrt ad rish, Nagh vel shin gra yn irriney, dy nee Samaritan oo, as dy vel drogh-spyrryd aynyd.
[8:49] Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha vel drogh-spyrryd aynym's; agh ta mee cur ooashley da my Ayr, as ta shiuish cur mee-ooashley dooys.
[8:50] As cha vel mee shirrey my ghloyr hene: ta fer ayn ta shirrey as briwnys.
[8:51] Dy firrinagh-focklagh ta mee gra riu, My ta dooinney freayll my raa's, cha vaik eh yn baase dy bragh beayn.
[8:52] Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn rish, Nish ta fys ain dy vel drogh-spyrryd aynyd. Ta Abraham marroo as ny phadeyryn; as t'ou uss gra, My ta dooinney freayll my raa's, cha jean eh blashtyn er y baase dy bragh beayn.
[8:53] Vel uss ny s'ooasle na'n ayr ain Abraham, ta marroo? as ta ny phadeyryn marroo: quoi t'ou jannoo jeed hene?
[8:54] Dreggyr Yeesey, My ta mee cur ooashley dou hene, cha vel my ooashley agh beggan feeu: she my Ayr ta cur ooashley dou, jehsyn ta shiuish loayrt, dy nee yn Jee eu eh:
[8:55] Ny-yeih cha nione diuish eh; agh shione dooys eh: as dy n'yiarrin nagh nione dou eh, veign my vreagerey goll riuish: agh shione dooys eh, as ta mee freayll yn raa echey.
[8:56] Ghow yn ayr eu Abraham foddiaght dy akin yn laa aym's: as honnick eh eh, as ghow eh boggey.
[8:57] Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn rish, Cha vel uss foast jeih bleeaney as da-eed dy eash, as vel oo er vakin Abraham?
[8:58] Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Roish my row Abraham, Ta mish.
[8:59] Eisht hrog ad claghyn dy cheau er: agh cheill Yeesey eh-hene voue, as hie eh magh ass y chiamble, goll trooid y cheeid oc as myr shen hie eh shaghey.
[9:1] AS myr va Yeesey goll shaghey, honnick eh dooinney v'er ny ruggey doal.
[9:2] As denee e ostyllyn jeh, gra, Vainshter quoi ren peccah, eh shoh ny e ayr as e voir, dy row eh er ny ruggey doal?
[9:3] Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha nee son peccah dy ren eh shoh, ny e ayr as e voir: agh dy vod dagh obbraghyn Yee v'er nyn soilshaghey magh ayn.
[9:4] Shegin dooys gobbraghey ny obbraghyn echeysyn t'er my choyrt, choud as ta'n laa ayn: ta'n oie cheet tra nagh vod dooinney erbee gobbraghey.
[9:5] Choud as ta mee ayns y theihll, mee soilshey yn theihll.
[9:6] Tra v'eh erreish shoh y loayrt, cheau eh shelley er y thalloo, as ren eh cray jeh'n shelley, as hug eh yn chray rish sooillyn y dooinney doal.
[9:7] As dooyrt eh rish, Immee as oonlee oo hene ayns poyll Siloam (ta shen 'sy ghlare ainyn, Er ny choyrt) Hie eh roish er-y-fa shen, as doonlee eh eh-hene, as haink eh as e hoilshey echey.
[9:8] Dooyrt ny naboonyn er-y-fa shen, as adsyn va roie er vakin eh dy row eh doal, Nagh nee shoh eshyn boallagh soie shirrey jeirk ?
[9:9] Dooyrt paart, She shoh eh: dooyrt feallagh elley, T'eh goll-rish: agh dooyrt eh hene, She mish eh.
[9:10] Shen y fa dooyrt aa rish, Kys va dty hooillyn er nyn vosley?
[9:11] Dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh, Ren dooinney va enmyssit Yeesey, cray, as hug eh rish my hooillyn eh, as dooyrt eh rhym, Immee gys poyll Siloam, as oolee oo hene: as hie mee, as doonlee mee mee-hene, as hooar mee my hoilshey.
[9:12] Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cre vel eh? Dooyrt eshyn, Cha s'aym.
[9:13] Hug ad lhieu gys ny Phariseeyn eshyn va roish shen doal.
[9:14] As she er y doonaght va Yeesey er n'yannoo yn chray, as er vosley ny sooillyn echey.
[9:15] Eisht denee ny Phariseeyn jeh reesht, kys v'eh er gheddyn e hoilshey. Dooyrt eh roo, Hug eh cray er my hooillyn, as doonlee mee, as ta mee fakin.
[9:16] Shen-y-fa dooyrt paart jeh ny Phariseeyn, Cha vel y dooinney shoh veih Jee, er-yn-oyr nagh vel eh freayll yn doonaght. Dooyrt feallagh elley, Kys oddys dooinney ta ny ghrogh-yantagh lheid ny mirrilyn y yannoo? As va streeu nyn mast' oc.
[9:17] Dooyrt ad rish y dooinney doal reesht, Cre t'ou uss dy ghra my-e-chione, dy doshil eh dty hooillyn? Dooyrt eh, She phadeyr eh.
[9:18] Agh cha ren ny Hewnyn credjal mychione echey, dy row eh er ve doal, as dy dooar eh e hoilshey reesht, derrey deie ad er yn ayr as yn voir echeysyn v'er gheddyn e hoilshey.
[9:19] As denee ad jeu, gra, Nee shoh yn mac euish, ta shiu gra va er ny ruggey doal? kys eisht t'eh nish fakin?
[9:20] Dreggyr e ayr as e voir ad, gra, Ta fys ain dy nee shoh yn mac ain, as dy row eh er ny ruggey doal:
[9:21] Agh kys t'eh nish fakin, cha s'ain; ny quoi t'er vosley ny sooillyn echey, cha vel fys ain: t'eh ec eash, fenee-jee jehsyn, loayree eh er e hon hene.
[9:22] Ny goan shoh loayr e ayr as e voir, son dy row ad ayns aggle roish ny Hewnyn: son va ny Hewnyn er choardail hannah, my ghoghe dooinney erbee rish dy nee eh va'n Creest, dy beagh eh er ny ghiarey magh ass y synagogue.
[9:23] Shen-y-fa dooyrt yn ayr as y voir echey, T'eh ec eash, fenee-jee jeh hene.
[9:24] Eisht deie ad reesht er y dooinney v'er ny ve doal, as dooyrt ad rish, Cur y moylley da Jee: ta fys ain dy nee drogh-ghooinney eh shoh.
[9:25] Dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh, Cha s'aym's dy nee drogh-ghooinney eh: un red ta fys aym er, dy row mee doal, as nish dy vel my hoilshey aym.
[9:26] Eisht dooyrt ad rish reesht, Cre ren eh rhyt? kys doshil eh dty hooillyn?
[9:27] Dreggyr eshyn ad, Ta mee er n'insh diu hannah, as cha dug shiu geill: cre'n-fa bailliu y chlashtyn reesht eh? vel shiuish myrgeddin son goaill-rish yn ynsagh echeysyn?
[9:28] Eisht doltooan ad eh, as dooyrt ad, T'ou uss 'syn ynsaghey echeysyn: agh ta shinyn ayns ynsaghey Voses.
[9:29] Ta fys ain dy loayr Jee rish Moses: agh son eh shoh, cha s'ain cre veih t'eh.
[9:30] Dreggyr y dooinney as dooyrt eh roo, Ta shen red yindyssagh, nagh s'eu cre veih t'eh? as ny-yeih dy vel eh er vosley my hooillyn's.
[9:31] Nish ta fys ain nagh vel Jee cur clashtyn da drogh-yantee: agh my ta dooinney erbee cur ooashley da Jee, as jannoo e aigney, dasyn t'eh cur clashtyn.
[9:32] Er-dy hoshiaght y theihll cha row eh er ny chlashtyn dy doshil dooinney erbee sooillyn fer va er ny ruggey doal.
[9:33] Er-be dy vel y dooinney shoh veih Jee, cha voddagh eh nhee erbee y yannoo.
[9:34] Dreggyr ad as dooyrt ad rish, V'ou uss er dty ruggey ooilley cooidjagh ayns peccaghyn, as vel oo goaill ort dy ynsaghey shinyn? As ghiare ad magh eh.
[9:35] Cheayll Yeesey dy row ad er yiarey magh eh; as tra v'eh er gheddyn eh, dooyrt eh rish, Vel oo credjal ayns Mac Yee?
[9:36] Dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh, Quoi eh, Hiarn, dy voddym credjal ayn?
[9:37] As dooyrt Yeesey rish, T'ou chammah er vakin eh, as she eshyn eh ta taggloo rhyt.
[9:38] As dooyrt eh, Hiarn, ta mee credjal. As hug eh ooashley da.
[9:39] As dooyrt Yeesey, Son briwnys haink mish gys y theihll shoh: dy vod adsyn nagh vel fakin, fakin; as adsyn ta fakin, dy vod ad v'er nyn yannoo doal.
[9:40] As cheayll paart jeh ny Phariseeyn va marish ny goan shoh, as dooyrt ad rish, Vel shinyn doal neesht?
[9:41] Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy beagh shiu doal, cha beagh peccah eu: agh nish ta shiu gra, Ta shin fakin; shen-y-fa ta nyn beccah tannaghtyn erriu.
[10:1] Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Eshyn nagh vel goll stiagh er y dorrys ayns bwoaillee ny geyrragh, agh ta drappal seose er aght ennagh elley, t'eh shen ny vaarliagh as ny roosteyr.
[10:2] Agh eshyn ta goll stiagh er y dorrys, ta'n fer cheddin bochilley ny geyrragh.
[10:3] Dasyn ta'n dorrysser fosley; as ta ny kirree clashtyn e choraa: as t'eh geamagh er e chirree hene lurg nyn ennym, as dy leeideil ad magh.
[10:4] As tra t'eh cur magh e chirree hene, t'eh goll rhymboo, as ta ny kirree geiyrt er: son ta enney oc er e choraa.
[10:5] As joarree cha n'eiyr ad er, agh roie ee ad er-chea veih: son cha vel enney oc er coraa joarree.
[10:6] Yn coraa-dorraghey shoh loayr Yeesey roo: agh cha hoig ad shen ny v'eh er loayrt roo.
[10:7] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo reesht, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Mish dorrys ny geyrragh.
[10:8] Ta ooilley ny haink roym's, nyn maarlee as nyn roosteyryn: agh cha dug ny kirree geill daue.
[10:9] Mish y dorrys: liorym's my ta dooinney erbee goll stiagh, bee eh er ny hauail, as hed eh stiagh as magh, as yiow eh fassaghey.
[10:10] Cha vel y maarliagh cheet agh dy gheid, as dy varroo as dy stroie: haink mish dy voddagh bea y ve oc, as dy voddagh eh y ve oc ayns mooarane palchey.
[10:11] Mish y bochilley mie: ta'n bochilley mie cur e vioys son ny kirree.
[10:12] Agh eshyn ta failt, as cha nee yn bochilley hene, as nagh vel ny kirree lesh hene, t'eh fakin yn moddey-oaldey cheet, as t'eh faagail ny kirree, as roie er-chea: as ta'n moddey-oaldey dyn dayrtyn ad, as skeayley ny kirree.
[10:13] Ta fer-ny-failley chea, er-y-fa dy nee fer-failt eh, as nagh mooar-lesh son ny kirree.
[10:14] Mish y bochilley mie, as ta enney aym er my chirree, as ta enney ocsyn orrym's.
[10:15] Myr ta enney ec yn Ayr orrym's, shen myr ta enney aym's er yn Ayr: as ta mee scarrey rish my vioys son ny kirree.
[10:16] As kirree elley t'aym, nagh vel jeh'n woaillee shoh: ad shen neesht shegin dou y chur lhiam, as cluinnee ad my choraa; as bee un woaillee ayn, as un vochilley.
[10:17] Shen-y-fa ta my Ayr graihagh orrym's, er-yn-oyr dy vel mee scarrey rish my vioys, dy voddym y ghoaill reesht eh.
[10:18] Cha vel dooinney erbee dy ghoaill voym eh, agh m'aigney hene eh dy scarrey rish: Ta pooar aym dy scarrey rish, as ta pooar aym dy ghoaill reesht eh. Yn sarey shoh hooar mee veih my Ayr.
[10:19] Va streeu er-y-fa shen reesht mastey ny Hewnyn son ny raaghyn shoh.
[10:20] As dooyrt ymmodee jeu, Ta drogh spyrryd ayn, as t'eh ass e cheeayl; cre'n-fa ta shiu geaishtagh rish?
[10:21] Dooyrt feallagh elley, Cha vel ad shoh goan fer ta drogh-spyrryd ayn: Vod drogh spyrryd sooillyn ny doail y osley?
[10:22] As haghyr shoh ec Jerusalem, ec feailley casherickey yn chiamble; as nish va'n geurey.
[10:23] As va Yeesey shooyl ayns y chiamble ayns porch Solomon.
[10:24] Eisht haink ny Hewnyn mygeayrt-y-mysh, as dooyrt ad rish, Caid t'ou freayll shin fo mee-ourys? My she yn Creest oo, insh dooin dy ynrick.
[10:25] Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Ta mee er n'insh diu hannah, as cha ren shiu my chredjal: ta ny obbraghyn ta mee dy yannoo ayns ennym my Ayrey gymmyrkey fenish jee'm.
[10:26] Agh cha vel shiuish credjal; er-yn-oyr nagh vel shiu jeh my hioltane, myr dooyrt mee riu.
[10:27] Ta my chirree clashtyn my choraa, as ta enney aym orroo, as eiyree ad orrym.
[10:28] As ta mee cur daue yn vea veayn, as cha jean ad dy bragh cherraghtyn, as cha n'ghow fer erbee ad ass my laue er-niart.
[10:29] Ta my Ayr hug dou ad, pooaral erskyn ooilley: as cha jarg fer erbee y ghoaill ad ass laue my Ayrey.
[10:30] Ta mish as my Ayr unnane.
[10:31] Eisht hrog ny Hewnyn claghyn reesht dy chlaghey eh.
[10:32] Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Shimmey yn obbyr vie ta mee er hoilshaghey diu veih my Ayr; son quoi j'eh ny obbraghyn cheddin ta shiu ry-hoi m'y chlaghey?
[10:33] Dreggyr ny Hewnyn eh, gra, Son obbyr vie cha vel shin dy dty chlaghey; agh son goan-mollaghtagh, as er-yn-oyr dy vel uss, ta dty ghooinney, jannoo oo hene Jee.
[10:34] Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Nagh vel eh scruit ayns y leigh eu, Dooyrt mee, She Jeeghyn shiu?
[10:35] My t'eh genmys adsyn Jeeghyn, dauesyn va goo Yee er ny choyrt, as nagh vod y scriptyr v'er ny rassey:
[10:36] Vel shiu gra mychionesyn ta'n Ayr er chasherickey, as er choyrt gys y theihll, T'ou loayrt goan-mollaghtagh; er-yn-oyr dy dooyrt mee, She Mac Yee mee?
[10:37] Mannagh vel mee jannoo obbraghyn m'Ayrey, ny cred-jee mee.
[10:38] Agh my ta mee jannoo ad, ga nagh gred shiu mish, cred-jee ny obbraghyn: dy vod shiu toiggal as credjal, dy vel yn Ayr aynym's, as mish aynsyn.
[10:39] Er shoh v'ad reesht son y ghoaill eh: agh chossyn eh ass nyn laueyn
[10:40] As hie eh roish reesht er cheu elley dy Yordan, gys y boayl raad ren Ean hoshiaght bashtey; as duirree eh ayns shen.
[10:41] As va ymmodee cheet huggey, as gra, Cha ren Ean mirril erbee: agh va dy chooilley nhee loayr Ean jeh'n dooinney shoh firrinagh.
[10:42] As ren ymmodee credjal ayn ayns shen.
[11:1] NISH va dooinney dy row ching, va enmyssit Lazarus dy Vethany, balley Voirrey as y chuyr eck Martha.
[11:2] (She yn Voirrey cheddin v'ayn, ish ren ooillaghey yn Chiarn, as rub ny cassyn, echey lesh e folt, yn braar eck Lazarus va ching).
[11:3] Shen-y-fa hug ny shayraghyn echey fys huggey, gra, Hiarn, cur-my-ner, t'eshyn shynney lhiat ching.
[11:4] Tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, dooyrt eh, Cha vel y chingys shoh gys baase, agh son gloyr Yee, dy vod Mac Yee v'er ny ghloyraghey liorish.
[11:5] Nish bynney lesh Yeesey Martha, as y chuyr eck, as Lazarus.
[11:6] Shen-y-fa tra v'eh er chlashtyn dy row eh ching, duirree eh foast daa laa ayns yn un voayl raad v'eh.
[11:7] Eisht ny lurg shen dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Lhig dooin goll reesht gys Judea.
[11:8] Dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, Vainshter, cha voddey neayr as va ny Hewnyn shirrey dty chlaghey; as vel oo son goll gys shen reesht?
[11:9] Dreggyr Yeesey, Nagh vel daa oor yeig 'sy laa? My ta dooinney erbee shooyll ayns y laa, cha vel eh snapperal, er-y-fa dy vel eh fakin soilshey yn theihll shoh.
[11:10] Agh my ta dooinney shooyll ayns yn oie, t'eh snapperal, er-y-fa nagh vel soilshey ayn.
[11:11] Ny goan shoh loayr eh: as ny lurg shen dooyrt eh roo, Ta nyn garrey Lazarus ny chadley; agh ta mish goll dy ghoostey eh ass e chadley.
[11:12] Eisht dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, Hiarn, my t'eh cadley, nee eh coural.
[11:13] Ny-yeih loayr Yeesey jeh'n vaase echey: agh heill adsyn dy row eh er loayrt jeh fea y ghoaill ayns cadley.
[11:14] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo dy foshlit, Ta Lazarus marroo.
[11:15] As 'smie lhiam er y choontey euish, nagh row mee ayns shen (son niartaghey nyn gredjue) ny-yeih hooin-jee huggey.
[11:16] Eisht dooyrt Thomase ta enmyssit Didymus rish e heshey-ostyllyn, Lhig dooinyn goll neesht, dy vod mayd baase y gheddyn marish.
[11:17] Eisht tra va Yeesey er jeet gys Bethany, hooar eh dy row eh er ve kiare laa hannah 'syn oaie.
[11:18] (Nish va Bethany er-gerrey da Jerusalem, mysh daa veeilley jeh).
[11:19] As va ymmodee jeh ny Hewnyn er jeet magh gys Martha as Moirrey, dy gherjaghey ad son nyn mraar.
[11:20] Eisht cha leah as cheayll Martha dy row Yeesey cheet, hie ee magh ny whail: agh hoie Moirrey ayns y thie.
[11:21] Eisht dooyrt Martha rish Yeesey, Hiarn, dy beagh uss er ve ayns shoh, cha beagh my vraar er gheddyn baase.
[11:22] Agh ta fys aym, eer foast, cre-erbee nee oo y yeearree er Jee, dy der Jee dhyt eh.
[11:23] Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Nee dty vraar girree reesht.
[11:24] Dooyrt Martha rish, Ta fys aym dy n'irree eh reesht ec yn irree-seose 'sy laa jerrinagh.
[11:25] Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Mish yn irree seose-reesht veih ny merriu as yn vea: bee eshyn ta credjal aynym's bio, ga dy vow eh baase;
[11:26] As quoi-erbee ta bio, as credjal aynym's, cha vow eh yn baase dy bragh farraghtyn. Vel uss credjal shoh?
[11:27] Dooyrt ee rish, Ta, Hiarn: ta mee credjal dy nee uss yn Creest Mac Yee va ry-hoi cheet gys y theihll.
[11:28] As tra v'ee er ghra shoh, hie ee rhym bee, as deie ee er e shuyr Moirrey er-lheh as dooyrt ee, Ta'n Mainshter er jeet, as t'eh geamagh ort.
[11:29] Cha leah as cheayll ee shen, dirree ee dy tappee dy tappee, as haink ee huggey.
[11:30] Nish cha row Yeesey foast er jeet stiagh ayns y valley, agh v'eh ayns y voayl raad haink Martha ny whail
[11:31] Ny Hewnyn eisht va maree ayns y thie dy gherjaghey ee, tra honnick ad dy dirree Moirrey dy tappee, as dy jagh ee magh, deiyr ad urree, gra, T'ee goll gys yn oaie dy cheayney ayns shen.
[11:32] Eisht tra va Moirrey er jeet raad va Yeesey, as jeeaghyn er, huitt ee sheese ec e chassyn, gra rish, Hiarn, dy beagh uss er ve ayns shoh, cha beagh my vraar er gheddyn baase.
[11:33] Tra honnick Yeesey ee er-y-fa shen keayney, as ny Hewnyn myrgeddin keayney v'er jeet maree, hayrn eh osney hrome, as v'eh seaghnit;
