[14:25] Ny reddyn shoh ta mee er loayrt riu, choud's ta mee foast meriu.
[14:26] Agh nee Fer-ny-gherjagh, ta shen, yn Spyrryd Noo, eh nee yn Ayr y choyrt ayns yn ennym aym's, gynsaghey diu dy chooilley nhee, as tayrnee eh dy chooilley nhee gys nyn gooinaghtyn, cre-erbee ta mish er ghra riu.
[14:27] Shee ta mee dy aagail meriu, my hee ta mee dy choyrt diu: cha nee myr ta'n seihll coyrt, ta mish dy choyrt eh diu. Ny lhig da'n cree eu ve seaghnit, chamoo lhig da aggle y ve er.
[14:28] Ta shiu er chlashtyn kys dooyrt mee riu, Ta mee goll roym, as cheet reesht hiu. Dy beagh shiu graihagh orrym, ghoghe shiu boggey, er-y-fa dy dooyrt mee, Ta mee goll roym gys my Ayr: son ta my Ayr ny syrjey na mish.
[14:29] As nish ta mee er n'insh diu ro-laue, tra hig eh gy-kione, dy vod shiu credjal
[14:30] Veih shoh magh cha loayr-ym cooidvooar riu: son ta prince y theihll shoh cheet, as cha vel nhee erbee echey aynym's.
[14:31] Agh dy vod fys y ve ec y theihll dy vel mish graihagh er yn Ayr; as myr hug yn Ayr sarey dou, myr shen ta mee jannoo. Trog-jee erriu, lhig dooin goll roin.
[15:1] NISH y billey-feeyney firrinagh, as my Ayr yn eirinnagh.
[15:2] Dy chooilley vanglane aynym's nagh vel gymmyrkey mess, t'eh dy ghoaill ersooyl: as dy chooilley vanglane ta gymmyrkey mess, t'eh dy phollal, dy vod eh ve ny s'messoil.
[15:3] Nish ta shiuish glen trooid y goo ta mish er loayrt riu.
[15:4] Jean-jee tannaghtyn aynym's, as mish ayndiuish. Myr nagh vod y banglane mess y ymmyrkey jeh hene, mannagh vel eh tannaghtyn ayns y villey-feeyney: chamoo oddys shiuish, mannagh jean shiu tannaghtyn aynym's.
[15:5] Mish y billey-feeyney, shiuish ny banglaneyn: eshyn ta tannaghtyn aynym's, as mish aynsyn, t'eh shoh cur magh mooarane mess: son scarrit voym's cha vod shiu jannoo monney dy vie.
[15:6] Mannagh vel dooinney tannaghtyn aynym's t'eh tilgit magh myr banglane, as t'eh fioghey; as t'ad dyn deiy as dyn dilgey ad ayns yn aile, as t'ad er nyn lostey.
[15:7] My nee shiu tannaghtyn aynym's, as my ghoan's tannaghtyn ayndiuish, shirree shiu cre sailliu, as bee eh jeant er nyn son.
[15:8] Liorish shoh ta my Ayr er ny ghloyraghey, shiu dy chur magh lane mess, as shoh myr vees shiu ny ynseydee aym's.
[15:9] Myr ta'n Ayr graihagh orrym's, myr shen ta mish er ve graihagh erriuish: jean-jee tannaghtyn ayns y ghraih aym's.
[15:10] My nee shiu my annaghyn y reayll, nee shiu tannaghtyn ayns my ghraih: eer myr ta mish er vreayll annaghyn my Ayrey, as tannaghtyn ayns y ghraih echeysyn.
[15:11] Ny goan shoh ta mee er loayrt riu, dy vod y boggey aym's ve er-mayrn ayndiu, as dy vod y boggey euish v'er ny yannoo magh.
[15:12] Shoh my harey, Shiu dy chur graih yn derrey yeh da'n jeh elley, myr ta mish er ve graihagh erriuish.
[15:13] Graih smoo na shoh cha vel ec dooinney erbee, na dooinney dy scarrey rish e vioys son e chaarjyn.
[15:14] She my chaarjyn shiuish, my nee shiu ny ta mish dy harey diu.
[15:15] Veih shoh magh cha vel mee dy enmys shiu sharvaantyn; son cha vel fys ec y charvaant, cre ta e hiarn dy yannoo: agh ta mee er n'enmys shiu caarjyn; son dy chooilley nhee ta mee er chlashtyn veih my Ayr, ta mee er hoilshaghey diuish.
[15:16] Cha vel shiuish er my reih, agh ta mish er reih shiuish, as er chur shiu ayns pooar, dy vod shiu goll magh as mess y ymmyrkey, as dy vod y mess eu ve beayn: cre erbee nee shiu y hirrey er yn Ayr ayns yn ennym aym's, dy vod eh y chur diu eh.
[15:17] Ny reddyn shoh ta mish dy harey diu, dy vod shiu ve graihagh yn derrey yeh er y jeh elley.
[15:18] My ta dwoaie ec y seihll erriu, ta fys eu dy dug eh dwoaie dooys hoshiaght.
[15:19] Dy beagh shiuish jeh'n theihll, veagh y seihll graihagh er e vooinjer hene: agh son nagh vel shiu jeh'n theihll, agh dy vel mish er reih shiu ass y theihll, shen-y-fa ta dwoaie ec y theihll erriu.
[15:20] Cooinee-jee er y raa loayr mish riu, Cha vel y charvaant ny syrjey na e hiarn. My t'ad er n'yannoo tranlaase orrym's, nee ad myrgeddin tranlaase erriuish: my t'ad er vreayll my ghoan's, freillee ad ny goan euish myrgeddin.
[15:21] Agh dy chooilley nhee jeu shoh nee ad riu kyndagh rish yn ennym aym's, er-y-fa nagh vel enney oc ersyn t'er my choyrt.
[15:22] Mannagh beign's er jeet as er loayrt roo, cha beagh peccah er ve oc: agh nish cha vel leshtal oc son nyn beccah.
[15:23] Eshyn ta dwoaie echey orrym's, ta dwoaie echey er my Ayr myrgeddin.
[15:24] Mannagh beign's er n'yannoo nyn mast' oc lheid ny obbraghyn as nagh ren rieau dooinney erbee elley, cha beagh peccah er ve oc: agh nish t'ad er vakin, as er chur dwoaie chammah dooys as da my Ayr.
[15:25] Agh ta shoh, dy vod y raa ve cooilleenit ta scruit ayns y leigh oc, Hug ad dwoaie dou gyn oyr.
[15:26] Agh tra vees Fer-ny-gherjagh er jeet, eh ver-yms hiu veih yn Ayr, ta shen, Spyrryd ny firriney, ta cheet magh veih yn Ayr, nee eh feanish y ymmyrkey jeem's.
[15:27] As nee shiuish myrgeddin feanish y ymmyrkey, er-y-fa dy vel shiu er ve marym er-dyn toshiaght.
[16:1] NY goan shoh ta mee er loayrt riu, son nagh bee nyn gredjue er ny lhaggaghey.
[16:2] Ver ad shiu magh ass ny kialteenyn: as ta'n oor cheet, quoi-erbee varrys shiu, dy smooinee eh dy bee eh shirveish Jee.
[16:3] As ny reddyn shoh nee ad riu, er-yn-oyr nagh vel enney oc er yn Ayr, ny orrym's.
[16:4] Agh ny reddyn shoh ta mish er n'insh diu, tra hig yn earish, dy vod shiu cooinaghtyn dy dinsh mee diu jeu. As ny goan shoh cha loayr mee riu ec y toshiaght, er-y-fa dy row mee meriu.
[16:5] Agh nish ta mee goll roym huggeysyn t'er my choyrt, as cha vel fer j'iu fenaght jee'm c'raad t'ou goll?
[16:6] Agh er-yn-oyr dy vel mee er ghra ny reddyn shoh riu, ta trimshey er lhieeney ny creeaghyn eu.
[16:7] Ny-yeih ta mish ginsh diu yn irriney; Te ymmyrchagh er nyn son mish dy gholl roym: son mannagh jem roym, cha jig Fer ny-gherjagh hiu; agh my hem's roym, verym hiu eh.
[16:8] As tra vees eh er jeet, nee eh yn seihll y gheyrey mychione peccah, as cairys, as briwnys:
[16:9] Mychione peccah, son nagh vel ad credjal aynym's;
[16:10] Mychione cairys, son dy vel mee goll roym gys yn Ayr, as nagh vaik shiu mee arragh;
[16:11] Mychione briwnys, son dy vel prince y theihll shoh er ny vriwnys.
[16:12] Shimmey red ta aym's foast dy ghra riu, agh cha vod shiu ad y ymmyrkey nish.
[16:13] Agh tra hig eshyn, Spyrryd ny firriney, leeidee eh shiu gys dy chooilley irrinys: son cha loayr eh jeh hene, agh cre-erbee nee eh y chlashtyn, shen loayrys eh; as soilshee eh diu reddyn ta ry-heet.
[16:14] Nee eh mish y ghloyraghey: son yiow eh jeh ny ta lhiam's as soilshee eh diuish eh.
[16:15] Ta dy chooilley nhee t'ec yn Ayr lhiam's: shen-y-fa dooyrt mee, dy gow eh jeh ny ta lhiam's, as dy soilshee eh diuish eh.
[16:16] Tammylt beg as cha vaik shiu mee: as reesht, tammylt beg, as hee shiu mee, er-y-fa dy vel mee goll roym gys yn Ayr.
[16:17] Eisht dooyrt paart jeh e ostyllyn eddyr ad-hene, Cre shoh t'eh dy ghra rooin, Tammylt beg as cha vaik shiu mee: as reesht, tammylt beg, as hee shiu mee: as, Er-yn-oyr dy vel mee goll roym gys yn Ayr?
[16:18] Dooyrt ad er-y-fa shen, Cre shoh t'eh dy ghra, Tammylt beg? cha s'ain cre t'eh dy ghra.
[16:19] Nish va fys ec Yeesey dy row ad aignagh dy enaght jeh, as dooyrt eh roo, Vel shiu briaght nyn mast' eu hene, er-y-fa dy dooyrt mee, Tammylt beg, as cha vaik shiu mee: as reesht, tammylt beg as hee shiu mee?
[16:20] Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Dy jean shiuish keayney as dobberan, agh nee yn seihll boggey y ghoaill: as bee shiuish trimshagh, agh bee yn trimshey eu er ny hyndaa gys boggey.
[16:21] Ta ben, tra t'ee er-troailt, as trimshey eck, er-yn-oyr dy vel yn oor eck er jeet: agh cha leah as t'ee er ny livrey jeh'n lhiannoo, cha vel ee ny sodjey cooinaghtyn er yn angaish, son boggey dy vel dooinney er ny ruggey gys y theihll.
[16:22] As ta nish er-y-fa shen trimshey euish: agh hee-yms shiu reesht, as gowee yn cree eu boggey, as y boggey eu cha gow dooinney erbee veue.
[16:23] As ayns y laa shen cha jean shiu nhee erbee y enaght jeem's: Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cre-erbee hirrys shiu er yn Ayr ayns yn ennym aym's, ver eh diu eh.
[16:24] Cha vel shiu foast er hirrey nhee erbee ayns yn ennym aym's shir-jee as yiow shiu, dy vod y boggey eu v'er ny yannoo magh.
[16:25] Ny reddyn shoh ta mee er loayrt riu ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey: agh ta'n traa cheet tra nagh loayrym riu ny smoo ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey, agh soilshee-ym diu dy foshlit jeh'n Ayr.
[16:26] Ayns y laa shen nee shiu geearree ayns y ennym aym's: as cha vel mee gra riu, dy guee-ym gys yn Ayr er nyn son:
[16:27] Son ta'n Ayr hene graihagh erriu, er-y-fa dy vel shiuish er ve graihagh orrym's, as dy chred shiu dy daink mee magh veih Jee.
[16:28] Haink mee magh veih'n Ayr, as ta mee er jeet gys y theihll: reesht, ta mee faagail y seihll, as goll roym gys yn Ayr.
[16:29] Dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, Cur-my-ner, nish t'ou loayrt dy foshlit, as cha vel oo loayrt coraa-dorraghey erbee.
[16:30] Nish ta shin shickyr dy vel fys ayd er dy chooilley nhee, as nagh vel feme ayd dooinney erbee dy enaght jeed: liorish shoh ta shin credjal dy daink oo magh veih Jee.
[16:31] Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Vel shiu nish credjal?
[16:32] Cur-my-ner ta'n oor cheet, as eer nish er jeet, dy bee shiu er nyn skeayley dy chooilley ghooinney gys e ynnyd hene, as dy vaag shiu mish my lomarcan: as foast cha vel mee my lomarcan, er-y-fa dy vel yn Ayr marym.
[16:33] Ny reddyn shoh ta mee er loayrt riu, aynym's dy vod shee y ve eu. Ayns y theihll vees seaghyn eu: agh bee-jee dy yien mie, ta mish er gheddyn barriaght er y theihll.
[17:1] NY goan shoh loayr Yeesey; as hrog eh seose e hooillyn gys niau, as dooyrt eh, Ayr, ta'n oor er jeet; jean dty Vac y ghloyraghey, dy vod dty Vac myrgeddin uss y ghloyraghey.
[17:2] Myr t'ou er chur da pooar harrish ooilley sheelnaue, dy vod eh yn vea veayn y choyrt da whilleen as t'ou er chur da.
[17:3] As shoh yn vea veayn, tushtey y ve oc jeed's yn ynrycan Jee firrinagh, as jeh Yeesey Creest t'ou uss er choyrt.
[17:4] Ta mee er ghloyraghey oo er y thalloo: ta mee er chooilleeney yn obbyr hug oo dou dy yannoo.
[17:5] As nish, O Ayr, jean mish y ghloyraghey mayrt hene, lesh y ghloyr v'aym mayrt roish my row seihll ayn.
[17:6] Ta mee er hoilshaghey dty ennym gys ny deiney hug oo dou ass y theihll: lhiat's ad, as hug oo ad dooys; as t'ad er vreayll dty ghoo.
[17:7] Nish t'ad er hoiggal dy nee void's ta dy chooilley nhee t'ou er choyrt dou.
[17:8] Son hug mish dauesyn ny goan hug uss dooys; as t'ad er ghoaill huc hene ad, as er hoiggal ayns shickyrys dy daink mee magh voids, as t'ad er chredjal dy ren oo my choyrt.
[17:9] Ta mee guee ort er nyn son: cha vel mee guee son theihll, agh er ny son ocsyn t'ou er choyrt dou, son she lhiat hene ad.
[17:10] As ta ooilley ny ta lhiam's lhiat's, as ny ta lhiat's lhiam's, as ta mee er my ghloyraghey ayndoo.
[17:11] As nish cha vel mish dy ve ny sodjey ayns y theihll, agh t'ad shoh ayns y theihll, as ta mish cheet hood's. Ayr chasherick, freill trooid dty ennym hene adsyn t'ou er chur dou, dy vod adsyn ve unnane, myr ta shinyn unnane.
[17:12] Choud as va mee maroo ayns y theihll, dreill mee ad ayns dty ennym's: adsyn hug oo dou dreill mee, as cha vel unnane oc caillit, mannagh vel mac y toyrt-mow: dy voddagh yn scriptyr ve cooilleenit.
[17:13] As nish ta mee cheet hood's, as ny reddyn shoh ta mee dy loayrt ayns y theihll, dy vod y boggey aym's y ve oc jeant magh ayndoo hene.
[17:14] Ta mee er chur daue dty ghoo; as ta'n seihll er chur dwoaie daue, er-y-fa nagh vel ad jeh'n theihll, myr nagh vel mish jeh'n theihll.
[17:15] Cha vel mee guee ort dy ghoaill ad ass y theihll, agh oo dy reayll ad veih'n olk.
[17:16] Cha vel adsyn jeh'n theihll, myr nagh vel mish jeh'n theihll.
[17:17] Jean ad y chasherickey son dty irriney: dty ghoo she firrinys eh.
[17:18] Myr t'ou uss er my choyrt gys y theihll, myr shen ta mish myrgeddin er chur adsyn gys y theihll.
[17:19] As er y ghraih ocsyn ta mish dy chasherickey mee hene, dy vod adsyn myrgeddin v'er nyn gasherickey gys yn irriney.
[17:20] Chamoo ta mee guee er ny son oc shoh nyn lomarcan, agh myrgeddin er ny son ocsyn nee credjal aynym's trooid y goo oc.
[17:21] Dy vod ad ooilley ve unnane, myr t'ou uss ayr aynym's, as mish aynyd's; dy vod adsyn myrgeddin ve unnane ayninyn: dy vod y seihll credjal dy ren oo my choyrt.
[17:22] As y ghloyr hug uss dooys, ta mish er chur dauesyn: dy vod ad ve unnane, eer myr ta shinyn unnane.
[17:23] Mish ayndoosyn, as uss aynym's, dy vod ad ve jeant slane firrinagh ayns unnaneys, as dy vod fys ve ec y seihll dy vel oo er my choyrt, as dy vel oo er ve graihagh orroosyn, myr t'ou er ve graihagh orrym's
[17:24] Ayr, ta mee geearree adsyn t'ou er chur dou dy ve marym raad ta mee; dy vod ad fakin my ghloyr t'ou er chur dou: son t'ou er ve graihagh orrym's roish my row yn seihll er ny chroo.
[17:25] Ayr chairagh, cha ghow yn seihll tushtey jeed; agh ta tushtey er ve aym's jeed, as t'ad shoh er hoiggal dy vel oo er my choyrt.
[17:26] As ta mee er hoilshaghey daue dt'ennym's, as nee'm y hoilshaghey eh: dy vod y graih, liorish t'ou er ve graihagh orrym's, ve ayndoo, as mish ayndoosyn.
[18:1] TRA va Yeesey er loayrt ny goan shoh, hie eh magh marish e ostyllyn harrish y strooan Cedron, raad va garey, as hie eshyn as e ostyllyn stiagh ayn.
[18:2] As bione da Yuaase neesht va dy vrah eh, yn ynnyd: son boallagh Yeesey dy mennick taaghey yn voayl shen marish e ostyllyn.
[18:3] Hooar Yuaase eisht sheshaght dy gheiney, as sidooryn veih ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny Phariseeyn, as haink eh ayns shen lesh lonteyryn, as torchyn, as armyn.
[18:4] Va fys ec Yeesey er-y-fa shen er dy chooilley nhee harragh er, as hie eh magh, as dooyrt eh roo, Quoi ta shiu dy hirrey?
[18:5] Dreggyr ad eh, Yeesey dy Nazareth. Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Mish eh. As va Yuaase myrgeddin ren y vrah eh ny hassoo maroo.
[18:6] Cha leah eisht as v'eh er ghra roo, Mish eh, hie ad gour nyn drommey, as huitt ad gys y thalloo.
[18:7] Eisht denee eh jeu reesht, Quoi ta shiu dy hirrey? As dooyrt adsyn, Yeesey dy Nazareth.
[18:8] Dreggyr Yeesey, Ta mee er n'insh diu dy nee mish eh. My ta shiu er-y-fa shen dy my hirrey, lhig-jee daue shoh goll roue:
[18:9] Shoh myr va'n raa shen loayr eh cooilleenit, Jeusyn hug oo dou, cha vel mee er choayll unnane.
[18:10] Eisht va cliwe ec Simon Peddyr, as hayrn eh eh, as woaill eh fer-mooinjerey yn ard-saggyrt, as ghiare eh yn chleaysh jeh. Va ennym yn er-mooinjerey shen Malchus.
[18:11] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish Peddyr, Cur seose dty chliwe ayns y fine: yn cappan ta my Ayr er chur dou, nagh niu-ym eh?
[18:12] Eisht ghow yn cheshaght, as y captan, as fir-oik ny Hewnyn Yeesey, as chiangle ad eh.
[18:13] As hug ad lhieu ersooyl eh gys Annas hoshiaght (son v'eh shen ny ayr-'sy-leigh da Caiaphas, va ny ard-saggyrt yn vlein shen).
[18:14] Nish she Caiaphas v'er choyrlaghey ny Hewnyn, dy row eh ymmyrchagh un dooinney dy ve er ny choyrt gy-baase son y pobble.
[18:15] As deiyr Simon Peddyr as ostyl elley er Yeesey. Yn ostyl shen va ainjys ec yn ard-saggyrt er, as hie eh stiagh marish Yeesey gys thie yn ard-saggyrt,
[18:16] Agh hass Peddyr ec y dorrys er cheu mooie. Eisht hie magh yn ostyl elley shen va ainjys ec yn ard-saggyrt er, as loayr eh reeish va currym y dorrys urree, as hug eh lesh stiagh Peddyr.
[18:17] Eisht dooyrt y ven-aeg va currym y dorrys urree rish Peddyr, Nagh nee fer jeh eiyrtyssee yn dooinney shoh uss neesht? Dooyrt eshyn, Cha nee.
[18:18] As va ny sharvaantyn as ny fir-oik nyn shassoo ayns shen, ec aile geayil v'ad er n'yannoo (son ve feayr) as v'ad dyn jiow ad-hene.
[18:19] Denee yn ard-saggyrt eisht jeh Yeesey mychione e eiyrtyssee, as mychione yn ynsagh echey.
[18:20] Dreggyr Yeesey eh, Loayr mee dy foshlit rish y theihll: dynsee mee kinjagh ayns y cheeill, as ayns y chiamble, raad ta ny Hewnyn kinjagh taaghey, as dy follit cha vel mee er ghra nhee erbee
[18:21] Cre'n-fa t'ou fenaght jeem's? fenee jeusyn t'er my chlashtyn, cre ta mee er ghra roo: cur-my-ner ta fys ocsyn cre ta mee er ghra.
[18:22] As tra v'eh erreish ny goan shoh y loayrt woaill fer jeh ny fir-oik va ny hassoo ayns shen Yeesey lesh bass e laue, gra, Nee shen myr t'ou freggyrt yn ard-saggyrt?
[18:23] Dansoor Yeesey eh, My ta mee er loayrt dy olk, ymmyrk feanish jeh'n olk: agh my loayr mee dy mie, cre'n-fa woaill uss mee?
[18:24] (Nish va Annas er choyrt eh kianlt gys Caiaphas yn ard-saggyrt)
[18:25] As va Simon Peddyr ny hassoo as dy hiow eh-hene: dooyrt ad er-y-fa shen rish, Nagh nee fer jeh e eiyrtyssee uss neesht? Dob eh, as dooyrt eh, Cha nee.
[18:26] Dooyrt fer jeh sharvaantyn yn ard saggyrt (va mooinjerys dasyn va Peddyr er ghiarey yn chleaysh jeh) Nagh vaik mish oo marish ayns y gharey?
[18:27] Eisht dob Peddyr reesht, as chelleeragh gherr y kellagh.
[18:28] Eisht hug ad lhieu Yeesey veih Caiaphas gys halley ny briwnys: as ve moghey, as cha jagh ad-hene stiagh ayns halley ny briwnys, er-aggle dy beagh ad anchasherick; as nagh voddagh ad yn Eayncaisht y ee.
[18:29] Hie Pilate eisht magh huc, as dooyrt eh, Cre ta shiu dy chur gys lieh yn dooinney shoh?
[18:30] Dreggyr adsyn as dooyrt ad, Er-be dy nee drogh-yantagh eh, cha beagh shin er livrey hood's eh.
[18:31] Eisht dooyrt Pilate roo Gow-jee shiuish eh, as jean-jee eh y vriwnys cordail rish y leigh eu hene. Dooyrt ny Hewnyn er-y-fa shen rish, Cha vel eh lowal dooinyn dooinney erbee y chur gy-baase:
[18:32] Shoh myr va cooilleenit yn raa loayr Yeesey, cowraghey cre'n baase v'eh dy hurranse.
[18:33] Eisht hie Pilate stiagh reesht ayns halley ny briwnys, as deie eh er Yeesey, as dooyrt eh rish, Nee ree ny Hewnyn oo?
[18:34] Dreggyr Yeesey eh, Vel uss dy ghra shoh jeed hene, ny nee feallagh elley dinsh dhyt eh my-mychione's?
[18:35] Dreggyr Pilate, Vel mish my Hew? she dty ashoon hene as ny ard-saggyrtyn t'er livrey oo seose hym's: Cre t'ou er n'yannoo?
[18:36] Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha vel my reeriaght's jeh'n theihll shoh: dy beagh my reeriaght jeh'n theihll shoh; eisht veagh my harvaantyn er chaggey, nagh beign er my livrey gys ny Hewnyn, agh nish cha nee veih shoh ta my reeriaght.
[18:37] Dooyrt Pilate er-y-fa shen rish, Vel oo dty ree eisht? Dreggyr Yeesey, T'ou uss er ghra eh, ta mee my ree. Er son shoh ruggyr mee, as er-yn-oyr shoh haink mee gys y theihll, dy ymmyrkey feanish gys yn irriney, Ta dy chooilley unnane ta jeh'n irriney clashtyn my choraa.
[18:38] Dooyrt Pilate rish, Cre ta'n irriney shen? as tra v'eh er ghra shoh, hie eh magh reesht gys ny Hewnyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Cha vel mish er gheddyn foill erbee ayn.
[18:39] Agh ta cliaghtey eu mee dy eaysley diu fer ec y Chaisht: nailliu er-y-fa shen mee dy eaysley diu ree ny Hewnyn?
[18:40] Eisht deie ad ooilley reesht, gra, Cha nee eh shoh, agh Barabbas. Nish va Barabbas ny roosteyr.
[19:1] EISHT ghow Pilate er-y-fa shen Yeesey, as doardee eh eh dy ve scuitchit.
[19:2] As fee ny sidooryn attey dy ghrineyn, as hug ad eh er e chione, as hug ad er coamrey purple.
[19:3] As dooyrt ad, Dy vannee dhyt's, Ree ny Hewnyn: as woaill ad eh lesh nyn laueyn.
[19:4] Haink Pilate er-y-fa shen magh reesht, as dooyrt eh roo, Cur-my-ner, ta mish dy choyrt lhiam magh hiu eh, dy vod fys y ve eu nagh vel mish er gheddyn foill erbee ayn.
[19:5] Eisht haink Yeesey magh, ceau yn attey dy ghrineyn as y coamrey purple. As dooyrt Pilate roo, Cur-jee my-ner yn dooinney.
[19:6] Shen-y-fa tra honnick ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny fir-oik eh, deie ad, gra, Jean y chrossey eh, jean y chrossey eh. Dooyrt Pilate roo, Gow-jee shiuish eh, as Jean-jee eh y chrossey: son cha vel mish er gheddyn foill er bee ayn.
[19:7] Dreggyr ny Hewnyn eh, Ta leigh ainyn, as liorish y leigh ain lhisagh eh v'er ny choyrt gy-baase, er-y-fa dy ghow eh er dy nee Mac Yee v'eh.
[19:8] Tra cheayll Pilate er-y-fa shen yn raa shoh, v'eh ny s'agglee;
[19:9] As hie Pilate reesht gys halley ny briwnys, as dooyrt eh rish Yeesey, Cre voish t'ou? Agh cha dug Yeesey ansoor da.
[19:10] Eisht dooyrt Pilate rish, Nagh loayr oo rhym's? nagh vel fys ayd dy vel pooar aym's dy dty chrossey, as pooar dy dty eaysley?
[19:11] Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha voddagh pooar erbee y ve ayd harrym's, mannagh beagh eh er ny choyrt dhyt veih'n yrjid; shen-y-fa ta peccah smoo lhie ersyn ren m'y livrey hood.
[19:12] As veih shen magh va Pilate shirrey dy eaysley eh: agh deie ny Hewnyn, gra, My lhiggys oo yn raad da yn dooinney shoh, cha nee carrey da Cesar oo: quoi-erbee ta jannoo eh-hene ny ree, t'eh loayrt noi Cesar.
[19:13] Tra cheayll Pilate er-y-fa shen yn raa shoh, hug eh lesh Yeesey magh, as hoie eh sheese er stoyl ny briwnys, ayns ynnyd ta enmyssit yn Pavement, agh ayns Hebrew, Gabbatha.
[19:14] As she er laa aarlaghey ny Caisht ve, as mysh y cheyoo oor: as dooyrt eh rish ny Hewnyn, Cur-jee my-ner yn ree eu.
[19:15] Agh dyllee ad, Ersooyl lesh, ersooyl lesh, jean y chrossey eh. Dooyrt Pilate roo, Jean-ym yn ree euish y chrossey? Dreggyr ny ard-saggyrtyn, Cha vel ree ainyn agh Cesar.
[19:16] Er shoh ren eh eshyn y livrey huc dy ve er ny chrossey. As ghow ad Yeesey as leeid ad eh ersooyl.
[19:17] As dymmyrk eh e chrosh, as hie eh magh gys ynnyd yiarragh ad ynnyd y vollag rish, ta enmyssit ayns Hebrew, Golgotha.
[19:18] Raad ren ad eshyn y chrossey, as jees elley marish, fer er dagh cheu, as Yeesey ayns y vean.
[19:19] As ren Pilate screeuyn, as hug eh er y chrosh eh. As va'n screeu, YEESEY DY NAZARETH REE NY HEWNYN.
[19:20] Yn screeu shoh eisht ren ymmodee jeh ny Hewnyn y lhaih, son va'n boayl raad v'eh er ny chrossey er-gerrey da'n ard valley: as ve scruit ayns Hebrew, as Greek, as Latin.
[19:21] Eisht dooyrt ard-saggyrtyn ny Hewnyn rish Pilate, Ny scrieu, Ree ny Hewnyn; agh dy dooyrt eh, She ree ny Hewnyn mee.
[19:22] Dreggyr Pilate, Ny ta scruit aym, te scruit.
[19:23] Eisht ghow ny sidooryn, tra v'ad er chrossey Yeesey, e gharmadyn (as ren ad kiare ayrnyn jeu, ayrn da dy chooilley hidoor) as myrgeddin e chooat: nish va'n cooat ooilley feeit, veih heose dy heese, fegooish seam.
[19:24] Dooyrt ad er-y-fa shen nyn mast' oc hene, Ny lhig dooin y raipey eh, agh lhottyn y hilgey er, quoi echey vees eh: dy voddagh y scriptyr ve cooilleenit, ta gra, Reynn ad my gharmad nyn mast' oc, as er my chooat ren ad lottyn y hilgey. Shoh myr ren ny sidooryn.
[19:25] Nish va nyn shassoo liorish crosh Yeesey, e voir, as shuyr e vayrey, Moirrey ben Cleopas, as Moirrey Malaine.
[19:26] Tra honnick Yeesey er-y-fa shen e voir, as yn ostyl bynney lesh ny hassoo lioree, dooyrt eh rish e voir, Ven, cur-my-ner dty vac.
[19:27] Eisht dooyrt eh rish yn ostyl, Cur-my-ner dty voir. As veih'n oor shen ghow yn ostyl ee gys e hie hene.
[19:28] Ny lurg shoh, son dy row fys ec Yeesey dy row dy chooilley nhee nish cooilleenit, dy voddagh y scriptyr ve jeant mie, dooyrt eh, Ta mee paagh.
[19:29] Nish va saagh er ny hoiaghey lane vinegar: as lhieen ad spunge leih y vinegar, as hug ad eh er hyssop, as heeyn ad eh seose gys e veeal.
[19:30] Tra va Yeesey er-y-fa shen er ghoaill y vinegar, dooyrt eh, Te cooilleenit: as chroym eh e chione, as phaart eh.
[19:31] Shen-y-fa son dy nee laa yn aarlaghey ve, as nagh beagh ny kirp er y chrosh er laa yn doonaght (son va'n doonaght shen ny ard-laa) ghuee ny Hewnyn er Pilate, ny lurgaghyn oc dy ve brisht, as ad dy ve goit ersooyl.
[19:32] Eisht haink ny sidooryn as vrish ad lurgaghyn y chied er, as y jeh elley v'er ny chrossey marish.
[19:33] Agh tra haink ad gys Yeesey, as dy vaik ad dy row eh hannah marroo, cha vrish ad ny lurgaghyn echeysyn.
[19:34] Agh ren fer jeh ny sidooryn lesh shleiy yn lhiattee echey y hoylley, as chelleeragh haink magh ass fuill as ushtey.
[19:35] As dymmyrk eshyn honnick eh feanish, as ta'n eanish echey firrinagh: as ta fys echey dy vel eh gra yn irriney, dy vod shiuish credjal.
[19:36] Son liorish jannoo ny reddyn shoh va'n scriptyr cooilleenit, Cha bee craue jeh er ny vrishey.
[19:37] As reesht ta scriptyr elley gra, Jeeaghee ad ersyn t'ad er hoylley.
[19:38] As ny lurg shoh ren Joseph dy Arimathea (va fer jeh ynseydee Yeesey, agh dy follit, ayns aggle roish ny Hewnyn) guee er-Pilate, eh dy lhiggey da corp Yeesey y ghoaill ersooyl; as hug Pilate kied da: Haink eh er-y-fa shen, as hug eh lesh corp Yeesey.
[19:39] As haink myrgeddin Nicodemus (va roie er jeet gys Yeesey ayns yn oie) as hug eh lesh mysh keead punt dy vyrrh as dy aloes kione y cheilley.
[19:40] Eisht ghow ad corp Yeesey, as hoill ad eh ayns aanrityn, lesh spiceyn, myr va cliaghtey ny Hewnyn dy oanluckey.
[19:41] Nish er-gerrey da'n ynnyd raad v'eh er ny chrossey, va garey; as ayns y gharey oaie noa, ayn nagh jagh rieau dooinney er coyrt.
[19:42] Ayns shen ren ad Yeesey er-y-fa shen y oanluckey, son dy nee laa aarlaghey ny Hewnyn ve, as dy row yn oaie er-gerrey daue.
[20:1] ER y chied laa jeh'n chiaghtin, haink Moirrey Malaine dy moghey, tra ve foast dorraghey, gys yn oaie, as honnick ee yn chlagh goit ersooyl jeh'n oaie.
[20:2] Eisht roie ee, as haink ee gys Simon Peddyr, as gys yn ostyl elley bynney lesh Yeesey, as dooyrt ee roo, T'ad er ghoaill ersooyl y Chiarn ass yn oaie, as cha s'ain c'raad t'ad er choyrt eh.
[20:3] Hie Peddyr er-y-fa shen magh, as yn ostyl elley shen, as haink ad gys yn oaie.
[20:4] Son v'ad ny-neesht er roie cooidjagh: agh va'n ostyl elley er roie ny s'bieau na Peddyr, as er jeet hoshiaght gys yn oaie.
[20:5] As chroym eh sheese, as honnick eh ny aanrityn nyn lhie, ny-yeih cha jagh eh stiagh.
[20:6] Eisht haink Simon Peddyr geiyrt er, as hie eh stiagh 'syn oaie, as honnick eh ny aanrityn nyn lhie.
[20:7] As y naptin va mysh e chione, cha nee ny lhie marish ny aanrityn elley, agh fillit er-y-cheilley ayns ynnyd er-lheh.
[20:8] Eisht hie stiagh myrgeddin yn ostyl elley shen haink hoshiaght gys yn oaie, as honnick eh as ren eh credjal.
[20:9] Son cha row foast toiggal oc jeh'n scriptyr, dy beign da girree veih ny merriu.
[20:10] Eisht hie ny ostyllyn rhymboo reesht gys nyn dhie hene.
[20:11] Agh va Moirrey ny shassoo cheu mooie jeh'n oaie keayney: as myr v'ee keayney, chroym ee sheese as yeeagh ee stiagh ayns yn oaie.
[20:12] As honnick ee daa ainle nyn soie ayns coamraghyn sollys, yn derrey yeh ec y chione, as y jeh elley ec ny cassyn raad va corp Yeesey ny lhie.
[20:13] As dooyrt ad r'ee, Ven, cre'n-fa t'ou keayney? Dooyrt ish roo, Er-yn-oyr dy vel ad er ghoaill ersooyl my Hiarn, as nagh s'aym c'raad t'ad er choyrt eh.
[20:14] As tra v'ee er ghra shoh, hyndaa ee mygeayrt, as honnick ee Yeesey ny hassoo, as cha row fys eck dy nee Yeesey v'ayn.
[20:15] Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Ven, cre'n-fa t'ou keayney? quoi t'ou dy hirrey? Heill ish dy nee yn gareyder v'ayn, as dooyrt ee rish, Vainshter, my t'ou er chur lhiat ass shoh eh, insh dou c'raad t'ou er choyrt eh, as goym ersooyl eh.
[20:16] 
[20:17] Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Ny benn rhym; son cha vel mee foast er gholl seose gys my Ayr; agh gow gys my vraaraghyn, as abbyr roo, Ta mee goll seose gys my Ayr's as yn Ayr euish, as gys my Yee's as y Jee euish.
[20:18] Haink Moirrey Malaine as dinsh ee da ny ostyllyn, dy row ee er vakin y Chiarn, as dy row eh er loayrt ny goan shoh r'ee.
[20:19] Eisht er y laa cheddin, yn chied laa jeh'n chiaghtin, ayns yn astyr, tra va ny dorryssyn dooint, raad va ny ostyllyn er nyn jaglym cooidjagh ayns aggle roish ny Hewnyn, haink Yeesey as hass eh kiongoyrt roo, as dooyrt eh roo, Shee dy row hiu.
[20:20] As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, yeeagh eh daue e laueyn as e lhiattee. Eisht ghow ny ostyllyn boggey tra honnick ad y Chiarn.
[20:21] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo reesht, Shee dy row hiu; myr ta my Ayr er my choyrt's, myr shen ta mish coyrt shiuish
[20:22] As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, heid eh orroo, as dooyrt eh roo, Gow-jee yn Spyrryd Noo.
[20:23] Da quoi-erbee ta shiuish leih peccaghyn, t'ad er nyn leih daue; as da quoi erbee nagh vel shiu cur feaysley, cha vel ad feayshlit.
[20:24] Agh cha row Thomase, fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig va enmyssit Didymus, maroo tra haink Yeesey.
[20:25] Dooyrt ny ostyllyn elley er-y-fa shen rish, Ta shin er vakin y Chiarn. Agh dooyrt eshyn roo, Mannagh vaikym ayns ny laueyn echey ynnyd ny treinaghyn, as mannagh derrym my vair ayns ynnyd ny treinaghyn, as my laue y choyrt stiagh ayns e lhiattee, cha greidym.
[20:26] As lurg hoght laa reesht va ny ostyllyn echey sthie, as Thomase maroo: eisht haink Yeesey, as ny dorryssyn dooint, as hass eh kiongoyrt roo, as dooyrt eh, Shee dy row hiu.
[20:27] Eisht dooyrt eh rish Thomase, Sheeyn ayns shoh dty vair, as loaghtee my laueyn; as sheeyn dty laue, as cur ee stiagh ayns my lhiattee: as ny bee mee-chredjuagh, agh credjuagh.
[20:28] As dreggyr Thomase as dooyrt eh rish, My Hiarn, as my Yee.
[20:29] Dooyrt Yeesey rishyn, Homase, Er-y fa dy vel oo er my akin, t'ou er chredjal; bannit t'adsyn nagh vel er vakin, as foast ta er chredjal.
[20:30] As ymmodee cowraghyn elley dy jarroo ren Yeesey ayns fenish e ostyllyn, nagh vel scruit ayns y lioar shoh.
[20:31] Agh t'ad shoh scruit, dy voddagh shiuish credjal dy nee Yeesey yn Creest Mac Yee, as liorish credjal shiu dy chosney bea trooid yn ennym echeysyn. [ (John 20:32) Dooyrt Yeesey,Voirrey. Hyndaa ee ee-hene, as dooyrt ee rish, Rabboni, ta shen dy ghra, Vainshter. ]
[21:1] LURG shoh hoilshee Yeesey eh-hene reesht da ny ostyllyn, ec faarkey Tiberias; as er yn aght shoh hoilshee eh eh-hene.
[21:2] Va Simon Peddyr, as Thomase sliennooit Didymus, as Nathanael dy Chana ayns Galilee; as mec Zebedee, as jees elley jeh ny ostyllyn er nyn jaglym dy cheilley.
[21:3] Dooyrt Simon Peddyr roo, Ta mish son goll dy eeastagh. Dooyrt adsyn rish, Hem mainyn myrgeddin mayrt. Hie ad magh, as er-y-chooyl ghow ad lhuingys; as yn oie shen cha haare ad monney.
[21:4] Agh 'sy vadran, va Yeesey ny hassoo er y traie: agh cha row fys ec ny ostyllyn dy nee Yeesey v'ayn.
[21:5] Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Chloan, vel shiu er dayrtyn veg y veaghey? Dooyrt adsyn rish, Cha vel.
[21:6] As dooyrt eh roo, Cuir-jee magh yn lieen er y cheu-yesh jeh'n lhong, as bee eh eu. Eisht chuir ad: as nish cha row dy niart oc yn lieen y ghoaill stiagh va lhied y thummyd eeast ayn.
[21:7] Shen-y-fa dooyrt yn ostyl shen bynney lesh Yeesey rish Peddyr, She yn Chiarn t'ayn. Nish tra cheayll Simon Peddyr dy nee yn Chiarn v'ayn, hug eh e chooat-eeastee mysh (son v'eh 'sy lheiney) as hilg eh eh-hene ayns y cheayn.
[21:8] As haink ny ostyllyn elley ayns lhong veg (son cha row ad foddey veih'n thalloo, agh mysh keead stundayrt) sleodey lhieu yn lieen as yn eeast ayn.
[21:9] Cha leah eisht as v'ad er jeet gys y thalloo, honnick ad aile smarageagh, as eeast ny lhie er, as arran liorish.
[21:10] Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Cur-jee lhieu jeh'n eeast ta shiu nish er ghoaill.
[21:11] Hie Simon Peddyr er-board, as hayrn eh yn lieen gys thalloo lane dy eeastyn mooarey, shiaght-feed as three-jeig: as son ooilley dy row whilleen ayn, ny-yeih cha vrish y lieen.
[21:12] Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Tar-jee gys nyn mee. Agh cha by-lhoys da fer jeh ny ostyl nyn fenaght jeh, Quoi oo hene? cur enney er dy nee eh va'n Chiarn.
[21:13] Eisht haink Yeesey, as ghow eh arran, as hirveish eh orroo eh, as eeast myrgeddin.
[21:14] Shoh nish yn trass cheayrt hoilshee Yeesey eh-hene da e ostyllyn, erreish da v'er n'irree veill ny merriu.
[21:15] Myr shen tra v'ad erreish bee, dooyrt Yeesey rish Simon Peddyr, Simon mac Yonas, vel oo ny s'graihlee orrym's na orroo shoh? Dooyrt eh rish, Ta mee, Hiarn; ta fys ayd dy vel graih aym ort. Dooyrt eh rish, Jeeagh dy mie da my eayin.
[21:16] Dooyrt eh rish reesht yn nah cheayrt, Simon mac Yonas, vel oo graihagh orrym? Dooyrt eh rish, Ta mee, Hiarn; ta fys ayd hene dy vel graih aym ort. Dooyrt eh rish, Bee dty vochilley mie er my chirree.
[21:17] Dooyrt eh rish yn trass cheayrt, Simon mac Yonas, vel oo graihagh orrym? Va Peddyr mooar-seaghnit dy dooyrt eh rish yn trass cheayrt, Vel oo graihagh orrym? As dooyrt eh rish, Hiarn, ta fys ayd's er dy chooilley nhee, as fys ayd hene dy vel mee graihagh ort. Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Jeeagh dy mie da my chirree.
[21:18] Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Tra v'ou aeg ren oo oo-hene y chryssey, as jimmee oo raad erbee dy bailt: agh tra vees oo shenn, sheeynee oo magh dty laueyn, as nee fer elley oo y chryssey, as ver eh lesh oo raad nagh nailt.
[21:19] Shoh loayr eh, cowraghey liorish cre'n baase v'eh dy ghloyraghey Jee. As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, dooyrt eh rish, Eiyr orrym.
[21:20] Eisht hyndaa Peddyr mygeayrt, as honnick eh cheet geiyrt orroo yn ostyl bynney lesh Yeesey; yn fer cheddin ren lhie rish e oghrish ec shibber, as dooyrt Hiarn, quoi eh ta dy dty vrah?
[21:21] Honnick Peddyr eh shoh, as dooyrt eh rish Yeesey, Hiarn, as cre'n erree hig er y dooinney shoh?
[21:22] Dooyrt Yeesey rish, My she m'aigney's eh eshyn dy uirriaght derrey hig-ym, cre ta shen dhyt's? Eiyr uss orrym's.
[21:23] Eisht hie yn raa shen magh mastey ny braaraghyn, nagh row yn ostyl shen dy gheddyn baase: agh cha dooyrt Yeesey rish, Cha vow eh baase: agh, My she m'aigney's eh eshyn dy uirriaght derrey hig-yms, cre ta shen dhyt's.
[21:24] Shoh yn ostyl dymmyrk feanish jeh ny reddyn shoh, as ren ny reddyn shoh y scrieu: as ta fys ain dy vel yn eanish echey firrinagh.
[21:25] As ta myrgeddin ymmodee reddyn elley ren Yeesey, dy beagh ad ooilley scruit, ta mee dy heiltyn nagh gummagh y seihll hene ny lioaryn veagh scruit. Amen.
